Regression-covered (`zimones_hypothesis_primer_declined`, plus the two pre-existing odd/even tests updated to explicitly decline the now-legal primer choice) and the whole suite stays green, so Silkguard's own identical latent gap (hexproof rider dropped alongside a fully-declined counter distribution) is fixed for free too, though untested here (out of scope). **Still blocked:** twinflame (Strive #85), striding_shotcaller (DFC). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15, rider):** closed primal_might — pump-then-fight now share one cast target (pump targets the ally, the enemy is a resolution-time up-to-one pick, mirroring Effect::Fight's own resolution-time second creature); `Fight { ally_is_shared_target }` the reusable primitive. Not one of #73's own 11 cards (it carried a standalone approximates note). Still blocked: twinflame (Strive #85), striding_shotcaller (DFC).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed twinflame, landing Strive (CR 601.2f/702.42) as a new per-extra-target additional cost. `AdditionalCost.strive: Option<&'static Cost>` (TOML `[cost.additional.strive]`, the `[cost]`-shaped sibling of `kicker`). The ordering crux (CR 601.2c chooses targets before CR 601.2f locks the cost, but this engine puts a spell on the stack before pausing to choose multi-targets) is solved the same way immoral_bargain's `sacrifice_scaled` solved it: the caster declares the target count up front — a new `Intent::Cast.strive_count: u8` (mirrors `kicked`/`sacrifice_cost`'s cast-time slot) — `Game::cast_cost` multiplies `strive.{generic,colored,colorless}` by `strive_count.saturating_sub(1)` and folds it in (pip-sum only, same `ponytail:` as kicker's own fold), and a new `TargetCount.strive_scaled` (the `sacrifice_scaled`/`x_scaled` sibling) has `Game::choose_spell_targets` substitute the declared count as an always-exact `{N, N}` clamp via a new `Game::spell_strive_count` (reads a new `Spell::strive_count`, set from the `SpellCast` event, mirroring `spell_sacrifice_count`). `Game::validate_cast` additionally rejects a declared count that exceeds the legal-target count or `MAX_TARGETS` up front (`Reject::IllegalTarget`) — Strive has no separate cost-paying vector to derive the count from (unlike sacrifice), so an over-declared count would otherwise overpay for targets `choose_spell_targets` could never fill. Separately, `create_token_copy` adopted multi-target: a new `targets: TargetCount` field (named apart from its existing `count: Amount`, the "how many targets" vs. "copies per target" split `put_counters` already established) drives the ordinary multi-target step-expansion in `effects.rs`'s `resolve_spell` — no special-cased resolution loop, the effect just runs once per chosen target like every other multi-target effect. A new `exile_at_next_end_step: bool` (mirrors `create_token`'s own field, distinct from `sacrifice_at_next_end_step` because exile skips dies-triggers) replaces twinflame's old sacrifice-based cleanup with the oracle-correct exile. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** twinflame — Strive's escalating cost, "any number of target creatures you control," one haste copy per chosen target, and end-step exile (not sacrifice) are all scripted and tested (a Zulaport Cutthroat copy proves exile via no dies-trigger firing, versus sacrifice which would). Single-target `create_token_copy` (`count = 1`, `targets` defaulted) is behavior-preserving — the existing determined_iteration/rionya/rite_of_replication/leitmotif_composer/replication_technique tests are unchanged. **#73's only remaining card is striding_shotcaller** (DFC/Prepared back face — a different unlanded prereq, untouched). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed **multiple independent target clauses per spell/ability** and closed magma_opus (and kinetic_ooze, #65's residual). One spell/ability may now carry more than one targeting effect, each with its *own* target set. Spell path: a runtime `Spell::targets_second: TargetList` holds a second clause (clause 0 stays `Spell::targets`, `Copy`-preserving — no `Vec` on the `Copy` `Spell`); a new `Game::spell_target_clause(def, n)` enumerates the n-th non-single `Timing::Spell` targeting ability, and `choose_spell_targets` now chains clause-by-clause (`Game::advance_spell_target_clauses`) at cast — clause 0 chosen, then clause 1, then the CR 601.2d divided-damage/counter split runs once every clause is settled. `PendingChoice::ChooseSpellTargets` and `Event::SpellTargetsChosen` grew a `clause: u8` (the schema wire view drops it — engine-internal ordering); `apply.rs` routes clause 0/1 to the two `TargetList`s; the non-modal resolution step-builder pulls each multi-target ability's targets from its own clause. Ability path: rather than thread a per-clause list onto the `Copy` `StackItem::Ability` (single `target`), a second targeting *step* in a triggered ability's `Sequence` chooses its set **at resolution** (ponytail CR 603.3d) via a new no-target-of-its-own effect `double_counters_on_chosen_creatures` (pauses on a new `PendingChoice::DoubleCountersTargets`, mirrors `phase_out`/`Proliferate`'s any-subset choice, reuses `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`). Two clauses max per spell (bump to a `[TargetList; N]` array when a card prints three — none does). **Trimmed to a precise residual:** magma_opus — the divided-damage clause *and* the "Tap two target permanents" clause now both resolve with independent cast-time targets; only the alternative `{U/R}{U/R}, Discard this card: Create a Treasure` activated-from-hand ability stays dropped (#82, alt costs), plus the standing division-keyed-by-permanent ponytail (a player can't be a divided target — no pool card needs it). **Still blocked:** striding_shotcaller (DFC), magma_opus's #82 residual. Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-16):** landed magma_opus's divided-damage-to-a-player residual — the standing
"division keyed by permanent, so a player can't be a divided target" ponytail the 2026-07-15 note
left (and its #82 alt-cost residual is already closed by the modeled `[hand_ability]`). The divided
`deal_damage` clause's filter widened from `creature_or_planeswalker` to `target = "any"`
(creature-or-player, CR 601.2d's "any number of targets"). A parallel `Copy`
`Spell::damage_division_players: [Option<(PlayerId, i32)>; MAX_TARGETS]` carries player shares beside
the object-keyed `DamageAssignment`, and a dedicated `Intent::DivideSpellDamage { assignment:
Vec<(Target, i32)> }` (its own `Target`-keyed wire — `WireSpellDamage`/`WireIntent::DivideSpellDamage`
— split from combat's object-only `AssignDamage`) lets a player be named in the division answer;
`effects.rs`'s divided read pulls a `Target::Player` share from the player array then falls through to
the existing life-loss arm. Combat's `DamageAssignment`/`Intent::AssignDamage` were left untouched.
**Trimmed (residual only):** magma_opus — the divided clause now splits across creatures *and*
players; the "or planeswalker" half closed 2026-07-16 (`target = "any"` reaches planeswalkers now
that `AnyTarget` chains them — see #66's damage-to-planeswalker note), so the divided clause is fully
faithful. **Still blocked:** striding_shotcaller (DFC). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-16):** landed the **ability-path** multiple-independent-target-clause capability the 2026-07-15 note left as a resolution-time ponytail, and closed kinetic_ooze (this entry's and #99's last residual). A triggered ability may now carry a *second* independent target clause chosen as the trigger goes on the stack (CR 603.3d — real targeting, shroud/hexproof/protection enforced, responders react to the set), the ability analog of the spell path's `Spell::targets_second`. Runtime `StackItem::Ability` (and the `TriggeredAbilityOnStack` event / `ResolveCtx`) grew a `targets_second: TargetList` — `Copy`-preserving (fixed array, off `CardDef`). A new targeted effect `double_counters_on_target_creatures { target, count }` replaces the old no-target `double_counters_on_chosen_creatures`; it reads its chosen set from `targets_second` at resolution (per-target CR 608.2b gone-target skip). At placement, `Game::place_ability_second_clause` — reached from every terminal single-ability push path (destroy chosen / declined / no-legal-target) — finds the second clause via `Effect::reads_second_target_clause` (only `double_counters_on_target_creatures`, so a `Sequence` step that merely shares the one chosen target, Killian's goad, is *not* mistaken for one), honors the X≥10 intervening-if at placement (CR 603.4 — the clause is absent, no targets chosen, when X<10), and pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseAbilityTargets` (answered by `Intent::ChooseTargets`, projected to a new `PendingChoiceView::ChooseAbilityTargets` mirroring `ChooseSpellTargets`) or auto-fills the forced set. The old resolution-time subset — `Effect::DoubleCountersOnChosenCreatures`, `PendingChoice::DoubleCountersTargets` and its schema mirror, `begin_double_counters_on_chosen`/`answer_double_counters` — is fully deleted (no dead shortcut left). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** kinetic_ooze — the X≥10 rider's "any number of other target creatures" is chosen at placement with real targeting; a hexproof opponent's creature is not a legal doubling target, and choosing zero / X<10 are both covered. Two clauses max per ability (no pool card prints a third). **Still blocked:** striding_shotcaller (DFC). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.

### 74. `delayed-until-next-turn` — 11 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
Widen v1 #27's landed `ScheduleAtNextUpkeep` into a general delayed-trigger schedule: `fire_at: Step` (next end step — "sacrifice/exile it at the beginning of the next end step", the myriad/Twinflame-family cleanup and Gift of Immortality's return), event-fired one-shots ("the next time you cast an instant or sorcery this turn, copy it" — Thunderclap Drake, Surge to Victory), a schedule entry referencing specific minted objects (the tokens to exile, not a re-scan), and the exile-play permission expiring at the end of your *next* turn (Atsushi's residual). One schedule structure, three drain sites.
*Cards:* angel_of_indemnity, atsushi_the_blazing_sky, determined_iteration, ghoulish_impetus, gift_of_immortality, manaform_hellkite, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, surge_to_victory, thunderclap_drake
**Progress (2026-07):** generalized `ScheduleAtNextUpkeep` into `fire_at: Step` (renamed the drain to `Game::fire_delayed_triggers`, `scheduled: Vec<(controller, source, Step, Effect)>`), so a schedule can fire at the next end step as well as the next upkeep. Two drain sites of the slice built: (1) `CreateTokenCopy { sacrifice_at_next_end_step }` schedules a `SacrificeObject` against each *specific minted token* (not a re-scan) at `Step::End`; (2) Atsushi's exile-play permission extended to expire at the end of your *next* turn via an `extended` flag on `play_from_exile` that shields the entry from this turn's cleanup, then arms (`Event::PlayFromExilePermissionArmed`) at its controller's next untap so it clears at that turn's cleanup. **Faithful (notes deleted):** atsushi_the_blazing_sky (the impulse-play window now lasts through the controller's next turn; only the standard resolution-time mode-choice ponytail remains). **Trimmed:** determined_iteration — the delayed sacrifice at the next end step is modeled; residual note is only the dropped "gains haste" rider (no per-token haste grant on a token minted mid-ability, #88). **Still blocked (untouched):** the event-fired "next time you cast an instant/sorcery, copy it" one-shots (muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, thunderclap_drake, manaform_hellkite), Gift of Immortality's delayed return, and the myriad-family cleanup (angel_of_indemnity, ghoulish_impetus).
**Progress (2026-07-14, via #69):** surge_to_victory cleared — its "copy the exiled card on
combat damage" clause turned out to need a *repeatable, controller-scoped* delayed watch
(`Effect::ScheduleThisTurnCombatDamageCopy`/`pending_combat_damage_copy`), not this entry's
event-armed-but-one-shot `pending_next_cast` shape (Thunderclap Drake's "next cast" is a
different CR 603.7 duration than "whenever ... this turn"). Landed under #69, not this entry;
still counts against this entry's card list as done. The remaining event-fired "next cast, copy
it" one-shots (thunderclap_drake et al.) are unaffected and still blocked.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the event-armed sibling of `scheduled` this entry's sketch called for — a *third* drain site, event-fired rather than step-fired. `Effect::ScheduleNextCastTrigger { filter, then }` arms a `pending_next_cast: Vec<(controller, source, SpellFilter, &'static [Effect])>` queue (`Event::NextCastTriggerArmed`); a new `Game::fire_next_cast_triggers` (its own `PostIntentPhase::NextCastTriggers`, right after `DelayedTriggers`) scans each batch's `Event::SpellCast` and fires+removes (`Event::NextCastTriggerConsumed`, CR 603.7's "next" — at most once) every armed watch whose controller cast a spell matching its filter, contextualizing `then` with the triggering spell's `{X}` exactly like `queue_cast_spell_triggers` already does; an unconsumed watch is cleared at the next turn's Untap (same boundary `spells_cast_this_turn` resets at). Also widened `Effect::is_mana_ability` to recognize a `Sequence` containing an `AddMana` step (CR 605.3a doesn't require a mana ability to do *only* that) and switched the mana-ability resolution path (cast.rs) from a bare `execute_effect` call to `resolve_effect`, so a composite mana ability resolves every step off-stack instead of panicking on `Sequence`. **This landed exactly one card, and it's a #68 card, not one of this entry's own** — brass_infiniscope (see #68's note below); none of #74's own 11 listed cards are touched yet. **Still blocked, unchanged:** the event-fired "copy the triggering spell" one-shots (muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, surge_to_victory, thunderclap_drake, manaform_hellkite — the new queue's *shape* fits, but each needs a command-zone-cast counter and/or copy-the-triggering-spell machinery this wave didn't build), Gift of Immortality's delayed return, and the myriad-family cleanup. Do NOT mark #74 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** built the copy-the-triggering-spell primitive this entry's "copy" drain site was still missing. `TriggerContext` grew `triggering_spell: Option<ObjectId>`, set from the matched `Event::SpellCast { spell, .. }` in `fire_next_cast_triggers` alongside the existing `cast_x`, and baked into a placed trigger's effect tree by a new `fill_triggering_spell` walker (mirrors `fill_dying_enchanted_creature`). New `Effect::CopyTriggeringSpell { triggering_spell, count, may_choose_new_targets }` resolves by reusing `mint_spell_copies`' existing mint-plus-retarget path (`may_choose_new_targets = true`, every current consumer) or a bare mint with no retarget (`false`, CR 707.10c's declined case — not exercised by any pool card yet); guard-returns with no copies if `triggering_spell` is `None` or has already left the stack (countered in response, CR 603.4). **Faithful (note deleted):** thunderclap_drake — all three abilities now scripted: the static reducer's `filter` switched from the `noncreature` stand-in to the real `SpellFilter::InstantOrSorcery` (the arm already existed, unused by this card until now), and the `{2}{U}, Sacrifice this creature` ability is `schedule_next_cast_trigger { filter = "instant_or_sorcery", then = [{ type = "copy_triggering_spell", count = "commander_casts_from_command_zone", may_choose_new_targets = true }] }`. **Still blocked:** muddle_the_ever_changing and redoubled_stormsinger (need myriad/become-a-copy machinery, not this primitive), rionya_fire_dancer (needs begin-combat-cast tracking + #89), surge_to_victory (copies a spell from a *graveyard*, not the stack — a distinct source, not this primitive), manaform_hellkite (its cast trigger creates a token, not a spell copy — this entry's card list mis-scoped it; already scripted via #89's `create_token`/`set_base_pt`, unrelated to this primitive, with a residual #101 mana-spent-to-cast gap). Do NOT mark #74 LANDED — angel_of_indemnity, ghoulish_impetus (myriad-family cleanup) and gift_of_immortality (delayed return) are also still untouched.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed Gift of Immortality's delayed return, the last item this entry's original sketch named ("Gift of Immortality's return"). Two new no-target effects: `Effect::ScheduleReturnThisAuraAttachedToReanimated` (no fields) — resolves as the second step of the existing `enchanted_creature_dies` ability, reading the just-reanimated creature back off this same resolution's own `Event::ReanimatedToBattlefield` (mirrors `AttachSelfToReanimated`'s read-back idiom) and scheduling the payload at `Step::End` via the existing `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled` — and `Effect::ReturnThisAuraAttachedTo { creature: Option<ObjectId> }` (internal only, `creature` baked in at schedule time, same synthetic-`then` shape as `SacrificeObject`/`ExileObject`) — the delayed payload `Game::fire_delayed_triggers` drains at the next end step: guard-returns with no return if the Aura (`source`, resolved through `current_id`) has since left the graveyard or `creature` (also `current_id`-resolved) no longer sits on the battlefield, otherwise moves the Aura graveyard→battlefield through the same `Event::ReanimatedToBattlefield` choke `ReanimateDyingEnchantedCreature` uses and attaches it in the same batch via `Event::AttachedTo`. Because `fire_delayed_triggers` already places its drained entries through the normal `place_pending_triggers` stack path (confirmed by reading `triggers.rs`), the return genuinely uses the stack — no off-stack ponytail was needed for this slice. **Faithful (note deleted):** gift_of_immortality — both sentences now scripted (`reanimate_dying_enchanted_creature` then `schedule_return_this_aura_attached_to_reanimated` in one `enchanted_creature_dies` ability). New engine test coverage: `gift_of_immortality_returns_aura_attached_at_next_end_step` (full lifecycle — reanimate, Aura stays in the graveyard through the rest of the turn, returns attached at the next end step), `gift_of_immortality_aura_return_no_ops_if_reanimated_creature_left` (guard-return when the reanimated creature is destroyed again before the end step), `plain_aura_death_unrelated_ability_unchanged` (Angelic Destiny's unrelated `enchanted_creature_dies` ability schedules nothing). Do NOT mark #74 LANDED — angel_of_indemnity and ghoulish_impetus (myriad-family cleanup, ghoulish additionally blocked on a choose-host `PendingChoice`, #79 residual) remain untouched, alongside the already-noted muddle_the_ever_changing/redoubled_stormsinger/rionya_fire_dancer/surge_to_victory blocks.
**Progress (2026-07-13):** landed ghoulish_impetus's delayed return, the choose-host slice #79 unblocked. Two new fieldless effects picking up where Gift of Immortality's same-creature return left off: `Effect::ReturnThisAuraFromGraveyardAttachedToChosenHost` (the immediate form, also used directly by screams_from_within under #87/#79) — guard-returns if this ability's own source (the Aura, resolved through `current_id`) has since left the graveyard, else moves it graveyard→battlefield unattached through the same `Game::reanimate_event` choke, then calls the existing `Game::maybe_pause_attach_deployed_aura` (a deployed Aura's own choose-host pause, #79) to raise `PendingChoice::ChooseAttachHostForAura` over the legal hosts on the battlefield — and `Effect::ScheduleReturnThisAuraFromGraveyardAttachedToChosenHost` (the delayed form ghoulish_impetus's `enchanted_creature_dies` ability uses), which schedules the former at `Step::End` via the existing `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled`, mirroring `ScheduleReturnThisAuraAttachedToReanimated`'s emit shape verbatim. Both effects share one internal helper, `Game::begin_return_aura_from_graveyard_attached_to_chosen_host` (entry + pause, called only from the immediate effect's `resolve_effect` arm — the schedule effect just arms the delayed trigger, no read-back needed). **Faithful (notes deleted):** ghoulish_impetus — both the static grant and the dies-return (now choosing a new host) are fully scripted. New engine test coverage: `ghoulish_impetus_returns_at_next_end_step_attached_to_chosen_creature` (full lifecycle through the choose-host pause), `ghoulish_impetus_no_return_if_aura_left_graveyard` (guard-return when the Aura itself is exiled out of the graveyard before the end step). **Still blocked, unchanged:** angel_of_indemnity (myriad-family cleanup), muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, surge_to_victory (the event-fired one-shots noted in earlier progress entries — rionya_fire_dancer already landed separately under #88's 2026-07-12 note, manaform_hellkite already scripted separately per #74's own 2026-07-12 note). Do NOT mark #74 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-14, via #88):** redoubled_stormsinger cleared off this entry's still-blocked list — its "sacrifice those tokens at the beginning of the next end step" reuses the already-landed `CreateTokenCopy.sacrifice_at_next_end_step` delayed-trigger machinery verbatim (`Step::End` schedule, no new drain site). Landed under #88 (the myriad/tapped-attacking-copy assembly), not this entry; the card was never one of #74's *own* event-fired-one-shot cards, just mis-tracked on this list from an earlier progress note. Do NOT mark #74 LANDED — see the other cards' notes above/below for their own status.

Also noting a bookkeeping gap in this entry's own tracking: angel_of_indemnity has carried no `approximates` note since wave 130 landed the Encore keyword (its "myriad-family cleanup" — the per-opponent must-attack haste-copy-then-sac body) — it was never re-checked off this list. Between that and muddle, **every one of #74's 11 cards is now faithful except manaform_hellkite**, which carries a residual `approximates` note scoped to #101 (mana-spent-to-cast vs. cast mana value) — an unrelated, unlanded prereq, not myriad/copy machinery. manaform_hellkite/#101 is the sole remaining blocker.

This entry landed piecemeal across #69/#79/#88/#89/#101/#127/#130 rather than as one build, matching its "one schedule structure, three drain sites" sketch.

### 75. `counter-kinds` — 6 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
The kind-keyed counter map v1 #39 deliberately deferred (only the finality bool landed): charge/story/vow/study counters as a small `(kind → count)` map on `Permanent`, with enters-with-N-of-kind, accrual triggers, remove-N-of-kind as an activation cost (Staff of the Storyteller's "{W}, remove a story counter: draw"), counter-count conditions, and counter-scaled `AddMana` ("add one mana per charge counter" — Astral Cornucopia, Elementalist's Palette). The `+1/+1` path and its replacement pipeline stay untouched; the map is for named non-P/T kinds.
*Cards:* astral_cornucopia, elementalists_palette, lattice_library, mana_bloom, promise_of_loyalty, staff_of_the_storyteller

**Landed:** a `CounterKind` enum (`Charge`, `Story` — only the kinds real cards land) keying a fixed `Permanent::kind_counters: [u8; 2]` array (kept off the +1/+1 replacement pipeline); `Effect::EntersWithCounters` grew `kind: Option<CounterKind>` (`None` = the +1/+1 path, `Some(k)` places the raw amount in the kind map), `ActivationCost::remove_counters_kind` (remove-N-of-kind as a cost, gated by CR 602.2b), `Amount::PerCounterOfKindOnSource`, `Condition::SourceHasNoCountersOfKind` (the "== 0" intervening-if), and `Event::KindCountersPlaced` (+ its `VisibleEvent` mirror — counters are public). Fully faithful (note deleted): mana_bloom (enters with X charge counters, "remove a charge counter: add one mana of any color" once-each-turn, upkeep self-bounce when it has no charge counters — its whole cost is a single `{X}`, so #68's multiplier gap never applies). Trimmed to a precise residual: astral_cornucopia (enters-with-X-charge + `{T}: one mana per charge counter` now faithful; the `{X}{X}{X}` cost stays a single `{X}` — `Cost.x` is a bool not a u8 multiplier, #68), staff_of_the_storyteller (the `{W}, {T}, remove a story counter: draw` ability now faithful; the story-counter *accrual* trigger stays dropped, blocked on #81's `Trigger::YouCreateToken`), promise_of_loyalty (the vow counter's "can't attack you / your planeswalkers" restriction stays dropped — per-creature attack restrictions aren't wired into declare-attackers legality, #80 — and the counter itself is left unplaced since it has no observable effect without that restriction).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** added `SpendRestriction::HasX` ("spend this mana only on costs that contain `{X}`", CR 106.9) — the one primitive the note's "restricted + counter-scaled `AddMana` wiring" gap was actually missing, since restricted mana (#120) and counter-scaled `AddMana` (`repeat = { per_counter_of_kind = "charge" }`, this entry's own `astral_cornucopia` half) had both already landed separately. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** elementalists_palette — all three abilities now scripted, including the `{T}: Add {C} for each charge counter... Spend this mana only on costs that contain {X}` tap (`add_mana`, `mana = ["colorless"]`, `repeat = { per_counter_of_kind = "charge" }`, `restriction = "has_x"`).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** added `CounterKind::Study` (`COUNT` 2 → 3, `kind_counters: [u8; 3]`) — the one primitive lattice_library's note was still missing, since the "first {X} spell each turn" cast trigger (#67/#68) and a token entering with variable +1/+1 counters (#89) had both already landed separately. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** lattice_library — `enters_with_counters { count = "x", kind = "study" }` places the study counters as the enchantment enters (its whole cost is a single `{X}`, so #68's multiplier gap never applies), and both the ETB and the recurring `cast_spell { spell_filter = "has_x", nth_each_turn = 1 }` trigger mint a 0/0 Fractal with `enters_with = { per_counter_of_kind = "study" }`, sized live to the study counters already on the enchantment.

### 76. `search-library-extensions` — 7 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Search widenings on the landed search flow: wire `CardFilter::LandWithSubtype` (landed for Nature's Lore) into the remaining consumers (Three Visits' Forest, Claim Jumper's Plains), "up to N" in one search with one shuffle + reveal (Land Tax's three basics, Cultivate's two, Springbloom's two — a repeat-select loop in the existing search `PendingChoice`), search-to-battlefield-tapped as a destination, and the catch-up "repeat this process once" rider (Claim Jumper). Also the opponent-landfall trigger already landed for Archaeomancer's Map — its "put a land from hand" search half rides here.
*Cards:* archaeomancers_map, bitterthorn_nissas_animus, claim_jumper, cultivate, land_tax, springbloom_druid, three_visits

**Landed:** `Effect::SearchLibrary` grew a `count: u8` (default 1, `de::one_u8`) — the max cards one search may find; `PendingChoice::SearchLibrary` grew `remaining: u8` and `search_library` now re-pauses (over `matches` minus the pick) after a found card while `remaining > 1` and matches are left, shuffling only once at the true end (CR 701.19f) — a fail-to-find still ends the search immediately, always legal. Fully faithful (notes deleted): three_visits (`land_with_subtype = ["Forest"]`, matching Nature's Lore's spelling), land_tax (`count = 3`). Trimmed to a precise residual: springbloom_druid (`count = 2` now faithful; the "sacrifice a land" additional-cost gate stays dropped — no ETB-trigger additional cost in the DSL), archaeomancers_map (`count = 2` + `land_with_subtype = ["Plains"]` now faithful; the filter also matches a nonbasic Plains-typed land — e.g. a check land — which the printed "basic Plains cards" wording excludes, and the pool has several such duals), claim_jumper (a real `[[abilities]]` ETB now exists — `count = 2` search for Plains to battlefield tapped, gated on the opponent-lands intervening-if — but "repeat this process once" re-checks that condition *between* the two fetches, which `search_library`'s repeat-loop doesn't thread; modeled as a flat `count = 2`, a broadening once the opponent catches up mid-search).
**Left blocked:** bitterthorn_nissas_animus (Living weapon — auto-create-and-attach token on ETB — has no engine entry point; its attack-trigger land search is otherwise exactly this wave's shape and would be trivial once living weapon lands).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** `Effect::SearchLibrary` grew `overflow: Option<SearchDest>` (default none) — the first find still lands on `to_zone`, every find after the first lands on `overflow` instead, carried on `PendingChoice::SearchLibrary` and applied in `search_library`'s re-pause (`dest: overflow.unwrap_or(dest)`), so one search can now route to two destinations while still shuffling once (CR 701.19f). Fully faithful (note deleted): cultivate — one `search_library` (`count = 2`, `to_zone = "battlefield"`, `tapped = true`, `overflow = "hand"`) replaces the old two-independent-searches modeling; the "reveal those cards" clause stays unmodeled (searches reveal nothing to opponents in this engine, the same untracked gap Land Tax's "reveal them" already carries with no note).
**Still blocked:** bitterthorn_nissas_animus (unchanged — blocked on Living Weapon, an external increment, not this increment's search shape; its attack-trigger land search is otherwise exactly this shape and lands trivially once Living Weapon does).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus landed via #79 once Living Weapon (`Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken`, #89) closed the blocker — the search half was already exactly this wave's shape (`filter = "basic_land"`, `to_zone = "battlefield"`, `tapped = true`). **Faithful (note deleted):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed claim_jumper's "repeat this process once" re-gate residual with no engine change — its ETB is now two sequenced `search_library` effects (`count` defaults to 1), the second wrapped in `Effect::Conditional { condition = opponent_controls_more_lands }`, so the second fetch is re-evaluated live at resolution (after the first Plains has entered) and cancels once land parity is reached (the flat `count = 2` broadening in the "Landed" line above is gone). **Faithful (note deleted):** claim_jumper. Tests: `claim_jumper_second_fetch_regated_on_land_parity` (opponent ahead by one → the second search never opens), `claim_jumper_fetches_two_when_still_behind` (ahead by two → it opens and fetches). **Still blocked:** none remaining — the full #76 pool is now faithful.

### 77. `prepare-back-face-authoring` — 7 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Author the remaining soc prepare cards onto the *landed* v1 #46 `CardDef::back`/`CastPrepared` machinery — each blocked only on small back-face verbs, most of which land in other v2 increments: each-player-loses-life (Vandal's Edit — Defacing Duskmage), draw-X + `ManaValueAtLeast` reducer (Braingeyser — Dirgur, dep #67/#68), Pest-per-opponent (Turn Stones — Eccentric Pestfinder, dep #64), Replenish mass return (Eiganjo, dep #69), Stensian's X-drain + combat-chain triggers, Striding Shotcaller's X-multitarget face (dep #73), Yavimaya Bloomsage's power-7 condition + EOT-mana-grant face (dep #71). This entry is the authoring sweep once those verbs exist.
*Cards:* defacing_duskmage, dirgur_focusmage, eccentric_pestfinder, eiganjo_dynastorian, stensian_sanguinist, striding_shotcaller, yavimaya_bloomsage

**Progress (2026-07-11):** authored the prepare cards whose front trigger and back-face verb were
already landed, onto the existing v1 #46 `[back]`/`CastPrepared` machinery — zero engine changes
needed (the stale approximates notes claiming "no prepared/DFC support" were wrong since #46).
**Faithful (notes deleted):** eiganjo_dynastorian (`you_attack_with_creatures at_least = 2` →
`become_prepared`; Replenish back face is `mass_return_from_graveyard { filter = "enchantment" }`,
covered by the new `prepare_eiganjo_replenish_returns_enchantments` test), defacing_duskmage
(`player_draws { drawer = "opponent", nth_each_turn = 2 }` → `become_prepared`; Vandal's Edit back
face composes `draw_cards` + `each_opponent_loses_life` + `lose_life`, ponytail-noted as sequential
rather than CR-simultaneous "each player loses 2 life" — unobservable for the pool). **Still
blocked:** dirgur_focusmage (front trigger needs a cast-zone qualifier, "from your hand",
#67/#68), stensian_sanguinist (combat-damage-to-a-player trigger + grant-deathtouch, #65/#97),
striding_shotcaller (X-multitarget back face, #73), yavimaya_bloomsage (target-power condition +
Channel restricted-mana back face, #75/#120). Do not mark #77 LANDED — four cards remain, all
blocked.

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the token-controller fix eccentric_pestfinder was waiting on —
new `TokenController::OnePerOpponent` (mints one token per opponent, all under the ability's own
controller), distinct from the existing `EachOpponent` (one per opponent, each under that
opponent). Turn Stones' back face now wires `create_token controller = "one_per_opponent"`, so
"For each opponent, *you* create a ... Pest ..." routes every minted Pest's "when this dies, you
gain 1 life" to the actual caster instead of the opponent who happened to receive it. **Faithful
(note deleted):** eccentric_pestfinder.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the cast-zone qualifier dirgur_focusmage was waiting on — a new
`from_hand: bool` on `Trigger::CastSpell` (`#[serde(default)]` false = the existing "any zone"
behavior), read off a new `Spell::cast_from_hand` engine-internal flag set at `Event::SpellCast`
apply time (`self.zone_of(from) == Zone::Hand`, checked before the source card moves onto the
stack) — no `Event`/schema surface, the flag never leaves `Spell`. Along the way, closed a second,
until-now-unnoticed gap the card's own back face needed: `Game::cast_prepared`
hardcoded its cast's `{X}` to 0 (`Intent::CastPrepared` had no `x` field at all), so an `{X}` back
face like Braingeyser could never draw more than zero cards. `Intent::CastPrepared` and
`Event::PreparedSpellCast` both grow an `x: u32` (mirroring `Intent::Cast`'s), threaded through
`cast_prepared`'s cost/target legality the same way `validate_cast` already does — a small wire
surface addition (`crates/schema` mirrors), unlike the `from_hand` flag itself. **Faithful (note
deleted):** dirgur_focusmage — reducer tightened to `instant_or_sorcery` (was `noncreature`), the
prepare trigger gated on instant-or-sorcery + MV≥5 + `from_hand = true`, Braingeyser's back face
drawing `{X}` cards to a target player. **Still blocked, untouched:** stensian_sanguinist
(combat-damage-to-a-player trigger + grant-deathtouch, #65/#97), striding_shotcaller
(X-multitarget back face, #73), yavimaya_bloomsage (target-power condition + Channel
restricted-mana back face, #75/#120). Do not mark #77 LANDED — three cards remain, all blocked.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed striding_shotcaller — its blocker ("X-multitarget back face,
#73") was stale: #68 (`TargetCount.x_scaled`) and #73 (silkguard's `put_counters.targets` shape)
are both landed, so the front trigger (`deals_combat_damage_to_player`/`who = "your_creatures"` →
`become_prepared`) and the back face's per-target counter+flying (one `[[back.abilities]]` whose
`put_counters`/`pump_until_end_of_turn` steps share a `Sequence` target, re-run once per chosen
creature by the existing non-modal multi-target expansion) plus the separate single-fire
`draw_cards` ability were pure authoring, no DSL surface added. One real engine gap surfaced along
the way, not anticipated by the dispatch: `Game::cast_prepared` had never been wired to the
choose-after-cast multi-target flow `Game::cast_with_kind` already gives a directly-cast
multi-target spell (`Intent::CastPrepared` only ever accepted a single up-front `target`, so
casting a prepared *multi*-target back face rejected with `IllegalTarget` before payment). Fixed
at `cast_prepared` itself — reuses the existing `spell_multi_target`/`choose_spell_targets`/
`PendingChoice::ChooseSpellTargets` machinery verbatim, no new `Effect`/`Event`/schema surface,
same "up to X"-is-declinable and X=0-forces-empty-choice semantics a direct multi-target cast
already has. **Faithful (note deleted):** striding_shotcaller. **Still blocked, untouched:**
stensian_sanguinist (delayed "that creature deals combat damage" prepared trigger +
grant-deathtouch-to-a-targeted-creature, #65/#97), yavimaya_bloomsage (target-power condition +
Channel restricted-mana back face, #75/#120). Do not mark #77 LANDED — two cards remain, both
blocked.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed stensian_sanguinist fully, and yavimaya_bloomsage's front face.
Stensian's clause A ("Whenever you attack, target creature gains deathtouch until end of turn")
is pure authoring onto the landed `pump_until_end_of_turn`/`you_attack_with_creatures` primitives.
Clause B ("Whenever that creature deals combat damage to a player this combat, this creature
becomes prepared") was the real gap: a new object-scoped CR 603.7 delayed watch, sibling to #74's
filter-scoped `ScheduleNextCastTrigger`/`pending_next_cast` — a new `Effect::ArmCombatDamageWatch`
(no target/filter of its own; reads the enclosing `pump_until_end_of_turn` step's shared target)
arms `Game::pending_combat_damage_watch: Vec<(controller, source, watched)>` via a new
`Event::CombatDamageWatchArmed`; a new `Game::fire_combat_damage_watch_triggers` (its own
`PostIntentPhase::CombatDamageWatchTriggers`, mirroring `fire_next_cast_triggers`) scans
`Event::CombatDamageDealtToPlayer` each batch, fires a placeholder-`Trigger` `BecomePrepared`
ability for any matching `watched` id, and removes the entry via `Event::CombatDamageWatchConsumed`;
an unconsumed watch is cleared at `Step::EndCombat`'s `StepBegan` (CR "this combat" — narrower
than `pending_next_cast`'s turn-boundary expiry). The back face, Exsanguinate, needed one more
fix: `Effect::EachOpponentDrain` only ever gained the controller a flat per-opponent `amount`
(correct for Zulaport Cutthroat/Silverquill Charm/Eriette, all fixed-number gains) — Exsanguinate's
"you gain life equal to the life lost this way" is the *summed* total across every opponent, a
real divergence in a 3+ player pod. Added `sum_gain: bool` (default `false`, existing cards
unchanged) to gate the summed reading. **Fully faithful (note deleted): stensian_sanguinist** —
both front-face clauses and the Exsanguinate back face, covered by five new tests (deathtouch
grant + expiry, the watch firing off the *targeted* creature specifically, a non-targeted
creature's damage not arming it, the watch clearing at end of combat so a later combat's damage
from the same object doesn't stale-fire, and Exsanguinate's summed lifegain in a 3-player pod).
yavimaya_bloomsage's front face needed a new `Condition::TargetPowerAtLeast { at_least }` — no
existing `Condition` arm reads the *resolving effect's own chosen target's* power (only
`TriggerContext`-derived reads existed); special-cased directly in the `Effect::Conditional`
resolve site against the shared `target` (mirroring how `ability_condition_holds` special-cases
source-based conditions `TriggerContext` can't reach), with a `false` fallback arm in
`condition_holds` itself for exhaustiveness. The `put_counters` + `conditional { become_prepared }`
two-step `effects` sequence is pure authoring once the condition existed. **yavimaya_bloomsage:
front face faithful, Channel back face still TRIMMED** — Channel (an activate-from-hand
mana-ability-window special action with a life payment) has no landed primitive; flag-don't-force,
left unauthored per #75/#120. Do not mark #77 LANDED — yavimaya_bloomsage carries a residual.

**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed yavimaya_bloomsage's Channel back face, closing #77's last
residual. The one real gap was a *player*-scoped granted mana ability — every existing granted
mana ability (`grant_mana_ability`, Goldspan/Galazeth) attaches to a surviving permanent source,
but Channel is cast from hand and its copy leaves nothing behind to hang a `Game::ability_at`
grant off of. Modeled as a fieldless `Effect::GrantChannelColorlessManaThisTurn` that sets a new
per-turn flag (`Player::channel_colorless_mana_this_turn`, cleared at the next Untap alongside
`flash_permission_this_turn`) via a new `Event::ChannelColorlessManaGranted` (+ its
`VisibleEvent` mirror — public, no redaction, mirroring `FlashPermissionGranted`). The granted
"pay 1 life: add {C}" action itself is a new standalone `Intent::ChannelColorlessMana` (mirroring
`Intent::TapForMana`'s directness) rather than a `meaningful_actions`/`ability_at`-enumerated
ability — a **ponytail**: CR 602/605's "any time you could activate a mana ability" window isn't
independently gated, the action is just legal whenever the flag holds (like every other mana
ability in this engine), and it isn't wired into the client's `paid_mana_activates` radial (which
already excludes every other pay-life mana ability, permanent or not) — a client-surfacing
follow-up, not an engine gap. **Fully faithful (note deleted): yavimaya_bloomsage** — front
trigger, `become_prepared`, and the Channel back face (`[back.kind] = instant`, no printed mana
cost, one `grant_channel_colorless_mana_this_turn` effect), covered by a new authoring test (the
back face parses to the grant) and a full front-trigger → prepare → cast-copy → pay-life-for-{C}
→ expires-at-Untap test. **#77 is now fully LANDED** — all seven cards faithful.

### 78. `sacrifice-cost-filters` — 8 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
`SacrificeCost` grows a `PermanentFilter` axis beyond None/This/Creature: "another creature" (`other: true` — Izoni's sac outlet can currently eat itself; Umbral Zealot, Wight, Woe Strider, Yahenni), subtype sacs ("sacrifice a Food" — Gilded Goose's mana ability, Gyome, Goose Mother), "a creature or artifact". The filter struct and its `matches` already exist — this is swapping the closed enum's payload and updating the two sacrifice choke points.
*Cards:* gilded_goose, gyome_master_chef, izoni, the_goose_mother, umbral_collar_zealot, wight_of_the_reliquary, woe_strider, yahenni_undying_partisan
**Landed:** `SacrificeCost::Creature` now carries a `PermanentFilter` (bare-string `"creature"` sugar still parses to an any-creature-you-control filter; `{ creature = { other = true } }` adds "another creature" self-exclusion), consulted at both choke points (`activate_ability`'s cost resolution and `sacrifice_candidates`). Fully faithful (note deleted): izoni's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the Insect token's color only, #63/#64), wight_of_the_reliquary's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the dynamic P/T only, #95), woe_strider's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the Goat token's color only, #64), yahenni_undying_partisan's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the death-trigger/self-target clauses owned by #72). Trimmed to a precise residual: umbral_collar_zealot ("or artifact" sacrifice option still dropped — no artifact-sac filter target in the pool).
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the "Sacrifice a Food" residual named above, as part of #65's Food-sacrifice-family slice — `SacrificeCost::Creature`'s two choke points (`activate_ability`, `sacrifice_candidates`) now accept *any* permanent matching the filter, not just a creature (the variant keeps its name; a `// ponytail:` on it notes the widened scope), and `de.rs` grows a `{ permanent = { … } }` sacrifice-cost table key that leaves `types` unforced (the existing `{ creature = { … } }` key is unchanged, still forcing `types = creature`). Fully faithful (notes deleted): gilded_goose (its "{T}, Sacrifice a Food: Add one mana of any color" — the last residual off #78's own Food-mint slice), gyome_master_chef (needed both this and #65's `nontoken_creatures_entered_this_turn` amount — see #65), the_goose_mother (pure authoring once Food-sacrifice and `may_sacrifice`'s existing subtype-filter axis covered it — no engine change of its own), umbral_collar_zealot ("Sacrifice another creature or artifact" is now `sacrifice = { permanent = { types = "artifact_or_creature", other = true } }` — the `{ permanent = { … } }` key's unforced `types` plus the existing `artifact_or_creature` type-union filter value cover it, pure authoring, no engine change). **Not still blocked** — #78 is now fully landed; nothing on its card list remains open.

## Tier 2 — multi-card M/L increments

### 79. `attach-riders` — 7 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Attach an Aura/Equipment as part of effect resolution: "if it's an Aura, you may attach it to the token" (Ajani's Chosen), Animate Dead attaching itself to the reanimated creature, "attached to that token" (Forum Filibuster), Fractal Harness's ETB self-attach, and move/re-attach with a choose-host `PendingChoice` ("when a creature enters, you may attach this to it" — Screams from Within; "return this from your graveyard attached to a new creature" — Shielded by Faith). Sketch: an `attach_to{target|minted-token|reanimated|chosen-host}` effect step reusing the existing attachment state, sequenced after the create/reanimate step; the choose-host form adds one `PendingChoice`.
*Cards:* ajanis_chosen, animate_dead, bitterthorn_nissas_animus, forum_filibuster, fractal_harness, screams_from_within, shielded_by_faith
**Landed:** three fieldless read-back attach steps sequenced after the create/reanimate step, reusing the existing `Event::AttachedTo` state — `Effect::AttachTriggeringAuraToMintedToken` (reads the just-minted token off this resolution's own `Event::TokenCreated`, attaches the triggering Aura if it is one — Ajani's Chosen), `Effect::AttachSelfToEntering` (attaches the ability's own source to the `permanent_enters` permanent; the "may" is the ability's `optional` flag / existing `MayYesNo` surface — Shielded by Faith), and `Effect::AttachSelfToReanimated` (reads the just-reanimated permanent off this resolution's own `Event::ReanimatedToBattlefield` — Animate Dead). `contextualize_effect`/`fill_entering_permanent` now recurse into a `Sequence` so a create-then-attach ability shares the one entering id. Bug fixed with regression coverage: `Event::AttachedTo`'s characteristics-cache invalidation only dropped the new host, never the vacated old host (a creature that lost an Aura's grant kept stale cached P/T/keywords). **Faithful (notes deleted):** ajanis_chosen, shielded_by_faith. **Trimmed:** animate_dead — now reanimates and attaches the Aura to the reanimated creature; residual note is only the -1/-0 penalty (#126) and "sacrifice it when this Aura leaves the battlefield" (#87).
**Still blocked:** forum_filibuster, screams_from_within (choose-host `PendingChoice` move/re-attach — untouched). fractal_harness's ETB self-attach landed via #89 (2026-07-12) as the analogous `Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken` — no longer blocked.
**Progress (2026-07-13):** the *deploy-time* choose-host form landed — `PendingChoice::ChooseAttachHostForAura` / `Intent::ChooseAttachHost` / `Game::choose_attach_host`, raised by `Game::maybe_pause_attach_deployed_aura` whenever an Aura is put onto the battlefield without being cast (Songbirds' Blessing #84, Armored Skyhunter #94), reusing the Aura spell's own `enchant`-restriction target legality; with no legal host it stays unattached for CR 704.5m to sweep. This is a sibling to — not — the *move/re-attach* form still owed forum_filibuster and screams_from_within (return-from-graveyard-attached / when-a-creature-enters), which stay blocked.
**Progress (2026-07-13, later same day):** screams_from_within landed, reusing the just-built `ChooseAttachHostForAura` deploy-time pause directly (`Game::begin_return_aura_from_graveyard_attached_to_chosen_host` moves the Aura graveyard→battlefield unattached, then calls `Game::maybe_pause_attach_deployed_aura` verbatim — see #74/#87's 2026-07-13 notes for the full mechanism). **Faithful (note deleted):** screams_from_within. **Still blocked:** forum_filibuster ("attached to that token" — a different read-back address, not a choose-host pause).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus landed — pure card authoring, no engine change. Living Weapon composes the already-landed `Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken` (#89) as an ETB `create_token` → `attach_self_to_minted_token` pair (the token enters 0/0 but the Equipment's own `grant_to_attached` +1/+1 lands the same resolution, so it survives as a 1/1, mirroring fractal_harness); the attack-trigger land search composes `Effect::SearchLibrary { filter = "basic_land", to_zone = "battlefield", tapped = true }` (#76) with `optional = true` and `timing = "equipped_creature_attacks"` (#89's `EnchantedCreatureAttacks` alias). **Faithful (note deleted):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus.

### 80. `attack-restriction-statics` — 7 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
The unlanded restriction half of v1 #52: "can't block" (Bloodghast), "can block only creatures with flying" (Brazen Borrower), "Inklings can't attack you" (Combat Calligrapher), "enchanted creatures can't attack you or a planeswalker you control" (Eriette), "attacks each combat if able" (Furygale's tokens), per-creature vow-marked "can't attack you" (Promise of Loyalty, dep #75), plus the attack tax's flat amount becoming an `Amount` evaluated per attacker (Nils' "pay {X} where X is the number of counters on it" — rides the landed v1 #52 tax slice). Sketch: restriction/requirement statics fed into the existing declare-attackers/blockers legality checks in `combat.rs`, filter-scoped per defender.
*Cards:* bloodghast, brazen_borrower, combat_calligrapher, eriette_of_the_charmed_apple, furygale_flocking, nils_discipline_enforcer, promise_of_loyalty

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the block-restriction half and the "can't attack you" attack-restriction half. Two new block-legality keyword tags on the shared `Game::can_block` check: `cant_block` (CR 509.1a, Bloodghast) and `can_block_only_flyers` (Brazen Borrower's printed static — not a named MTG keyword, a card-specific tag like `lesser_power_cant_block`). New `Effect::CantBeAttackedBy { filter }` — a `timing = "static"` attack restriction scanned per declared (attacker, defender) pair in `Game::declare_attackers`, mirroring `attack_tax_owed`'s defender-permanent enumeration, `filter`-scoped so only the static's own controller is protected; plus a new `enchanted_by_you` `PermanentFilter` axis ("enchanted by an Aura you control", reusing `auras_controlled_by_attached_to`). ponytail-noted: the "or planeswalkers you control" clause is unobservable while every attack target is a `PlayerId` (planeswalker defenders unmodeled — same as Mangara/Tomik in #91). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** eriette_of_the_charmed_apple (its end-step drain was already scripted). **Trimmed:** bloodghast (residual: conditional haste + landfall self-reanimation), brazen_borrower (residual: the Petty Theft adventure half, #131), combat_calligrapher (residual: the tapped-and-attacking token trigger, #88). **Still blocked:** furygale_flocking (forced-attack *requirement* scoped to minted tokens this turn — a whole requirement pipeline), nils_discipline_enforcer (counter-scaled attack *tax* + per-player multi-target — #68 X-in-costs + #102), promise_of_loyalty (vow-counter-marked "can't attack you" — needs a Vow `CounterKind`, #75 landed only Charge/Story). Do not mark #80 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the two remaining attack-legality riders. Part A — a per-token, this-turn *must-attack requirement*: new `combat_extras.must_attack: Vec<(ObjectId, PlayerId)>` (sibling of `goaded`, cleared at the next Untap), `Event::MustAttackDeclared`, and a `create_token.must_attack_defender` bool that emits one per minted token naming an opponent of the controller; enforced by a requirement loop in `Game::declare_attackers` mirroring the goad loop (CR 508.1a "if able"). Part B — the vow restriction: new `CounterKind::Vow` (COUNT 3→4), a `Permanent::vow_protected: Option<PlayerId>` scalar, `Event::VowCountersPlaced`, and a new `Effect::PlaceVowCounters { filter }` run as Promise's `each_player_sacrifices` `then` — it vow-marks every surviving creature (protected = the caster) and the restriction is read live in `declare_attackers` (attacker with a vow counter can't attack its `vow_protected` player), so removing the counter lifts it. Both events mirrored in `crates/schema` (public combat state, no redaction). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** promise_of_loyalty. **Trimmed:** furygale_flocking (residual: per-opponent scaling still flattened to 1v1 — a different unlanded item; dropped the "forced-attack rider isn't modeled" clause). **Still blocked:** nils_discipline_enforcer (counter-scaled attack *tax* + per-player multi-target — #68 X-in-costs + #102, out of scope). Do not mark #80 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15):** nils_discipline_enforcer fully faithful — per-player ability-controller-chosen up-to-one counter fan-out (#102) + counter-scaled per-attacker attack tax (this entry). New `Effect::CounterScaledAttackTax` (a fieldless `timing = "static"`) read in `Game::attack_tax_owed`: reworked to sum per (attacker, defender) pair, adding each such attacker's own counter count (`Game::total_counters`, CR 122.1 — all counter kinds) for every defender-controlled counter-scaled taxer; a counterless attacker owes nothing. The flat `Effect::AttackTax` summand is behavior-preserving (full suite green). nils was the last card of this list. **#80 LANDED.**

### 81. `watch-trigger-arms` — 7 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07-11, partial pool)**
A batch of small watch-trigger arms over events that already exist: `Trigger::YouCreateToken` (off `Event::TokenCreated` — Staff of the Storyteller), a `PermanentFilter` on dies-watches ("an enchantment you control is put into a graveyard" — Starfield Mystic), an opponent/you controller scope on creature-dies watches (Yahenni), an exile-destination batch watch ("cards are put into exile from your library and/or graveyard" — Laelia, mirroring the landed graveyard-exits accumulator), a per-player per-turn draw tally ("opponent draws their second card each turn" — Faerie Mastermind, the cast-counter shape applied to draws), a first-life-loss-each-turn flag (Intermediate Chirography level 2), and `Trigger::LeavesBattlefield` on the source with linked-exile context (Skyclave's "when this leaves…").
*Cards:* faerie_mastermind, intermediate_chirography, laelia_the_blade_reforged, skyclave_apparition, staff_of_the_storyteller, starfield_mystic, yahenni_undying_partisan

**Progress (2026-07):** landed the opponent-controller scope on the creature-dies watch — new fieldless `Trigger::CreatureAnOpponentControlsDies`, queued in `queue_death_watcher`'s `else` branch (`controller != dead_controller` = "an opponent controls it", CR 102.2 FFA pod). Fully faithful (note deleted): yahenni_undying_partisan.

Landed next: an enchantment-you-control death watch — new fieldless `Trigger::EnchantmentYouControlDies`, queued by a narrow `queue_enchantment_death_watchers` scan (kept separate from `batch_creature_deaths`/`queue_watch_death_triggers`, which must stay creature-only for the CR 603.6c look-back). "You control" only, no opponent-controller or `*IncludingThis` sibling yet. Fully faithful (note deleted): starfield_mystic.

Landed next: a per-player per-turn draw tally — `Player::draws_this_turn` (bumped on `Event::CardDrawn`, reset at Untap alongside `spells_cast_this_turn`; `Event::DrewFromEmptyLibrary` doesn't count, CR 120.3) feeding new `Trigger::PlayerDraws { drawer: CasterScope, nth_each_turn: Option<u8> }`, queued by `queue_player_draws_triggers` off `Event::CardDrawn` — a direct mirror of `queue_cast_spell_triggers`/`Trigger::CastSpell`, reusing `CasterScope` rather than a parallel scope enum. Fully faithful (note deleted): faerie_mastermind.

Landed next: the you-create-token watch — new fieldless `Trigger::YouCreateToken`, fired off `Event::TokenCreated` and deduped to once per event batch (CR 603.3b's "one or more") via a `creature_tokens_created_this_batch` scratch accumulator, mirroring `graveyard_exits_this_batch`'s drain-dedup-clear shape rather than the draw-tally's per-event ordinal math (a cleaner fit for "one or more" semantics than "the last matching event in the batch"). Gated to creature tokens (`def.kind`); "you" scope only, fieldless (flag-don't-force — no pool card needs opponent/any-player yet). Also generalized `Effect::PutCounters` with an `Option<CounterKind>` `kind` field (`None` = +1/+1 through the replacement pipeline, `Some(k)` bypasses it and emits `Event::KindCountersPlaced`, mirroring `EntersWithCounters`'s own kind split) rather than minting a new effect variant. Fully faithful (note deleted): staff_of_the_storyteller. **Still blocked:** skyclave_apparition (`Trigger::LeavesBattlefield` + sized token, #64/#65), laelia_the_blade_reforged (exile-destination batch watch, a new event accumulator) / intermediate_chirography (first-life-loss-each-turn flag, blocked on Class level-2 / #133).

**Progress (2026-07-10):** landed the exile-destination batch watch — new fieldless
`Trigger::CardsExiledFromYourLibraryOrGraveyard`, mirroring `CardsLeaveYourGraveyard`'s
`graveyard_exits_this_batch` accumulator with a sibling `library_or_graveyard_exits_this_batch`
pushed by `Game::create_object`'s single zone-move choke point (guard: `from` was a `Library` or
`Graveyard` card, `object` enters `Zone::Exile`), drained/deduped/fired once per batch the same
way. Fully faithful (note deleted): laelia_the_blade_reforged. **Still blocked:**
skyclave_apparition (`Trigger::LeavesBattlefield` + sized token, #64/#65) / intermediate_chirography
(first-life-loss-each-turn flag, blocked on Class level-2 / #133) — #81 not fully LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the last remaining arm — Skyclave Apparition's "when this
leaves the battlefield" linked-exile Illusion drawback. Not a real `Trigger::LeavesBattlefield`
(that surface was never built): forked the O-Ring linked-exile machinery instead — a sibling
`Effect::ExileTargetMintingIllusionOnLeave` records the link into a new
`exile_links.illusion_on_source_leave` list (`Event::ExiledUntilSourceLeavesMintingIllusion`),
and a sibling `Game::check_leaves_battlefield_illusions` (swept to a fixpoint alongside
`check_state_based_actions`/`check_linked_exile_returns`, same as O-Ring's own return) mints the
exiled card's owner an X/X blue Illusion token (X = the exiled card's mana value, new
`illusion_token()` helper) the moment the source leaves, then drops the link
(`Event::LeavesIllusionMinted`) so it fires exactly once — unlike O-Ring's return, the exiled
card is never returned and stays in `Zone::Exile` forever, so there's no zone-change guard to
stop a re-fire. ponytail (engine-side, not on the card): the mint is off-stack like O-Ring's
return, not a real triggered ability — CR 603 says it should use the stack and be respondable;
this can't be, same divergence `check_linked_exile_returns` already documents. Fully faithful
(note deleted): skyclave_apparition. **Still blocked:** intermediate_chirography (first-life-loss-
each-turn flag, blocked on Class level-2 / #133) — the sole remaining card; #81 LANDED
(partial pool) with that one prereq-blocked exception.

**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed the residual nontoken gate on the creature-you-control-dies
watch — new fieldless `Trigger::CreatureYouControlDiesNontoken` /
`Trigger::CreatureYouControlDiesIncludingThisNontoken`, threaded off a `dying_is_token: bool`
passed down from the two death call sites in `enqueue_triggers` (`Event::MovedToGraveyard` =
`false`, `Event::TokenCeasedToExist` = `true`) through `queue_watch_death_triggers` /
`queue_death_watcher`; the `IncludingThisNontoken` arm self-fires unconditionally in
`queue_self_death_watcher` since the "nontoken" qualifier only scopes the *other*-creature half.
Fully faithful (notes deleted): blight_mound, pawn_of_ulamog (also restored its dropped
including-this self-fire).

### 82. `nonmana-activation-costs` — 6 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-11)**
Non-mana cost flavors on activated/triggered abilities beyond sac-one/pay-life/remove-counters: mill-a-card (Millikin), sacrifice-two-creatures (Priest of Forgotten Gods), return-self-to-hand (Rootha), may-discard as a triggered-ability cost (Quintorius Chaser's +1; Conspiracy Theorist's "pay {1} and discard a card" — reusing v1 #11's spell-side discard plumbing on the landed pay-or-decline trigger `Cost`), and exile-a-filtered-card-from-your-graveyard as a cost (Quintorius Loremaster). Sketch: extend `ActivationCost` / the trigger `PayCost` path arm by arm; each is one gate check + one payment event.
*Cards:* conspiracy_theorist, millikin, priest_of_forgotten_gods, quintorius_history_chaser, quintorius_loremaster, rootha_mercurial_artist

**Progress (2026-07):** 3 of 6 cards landed — the paid-on-activation flavors. New `ActivationCost.return_self` (bool — bounces the ability's own source on activation via the existing `ReturnedToHand`/`TokenCeasedToExist` events) and `ActivationCost.mill_self` (u8 — mills the activator's own library, gated payable so an empty library can't pay it, CR 602.2b); `SacrificeCost::Creature` grew a `count: u8` (`sacrifice = { creature = { other = true }, count = 2 }`) so the activator names exactly N distinct controlled creatures, propagated by widening `Intent::{ActivateAbility,TakeAction}.sacrifice` from `Option<ObjectId>` to `Vec<ObjectId>`. **Faithful (notes deleted):** rootha_mercurial_artist (return-self), millikin (mill-a-card). **Trimmed:** priest_of_forgotten_gods — "Sacrifice two other creatures" is now faithful; residual note is only the edict targeting each opponent rather than "any number of target players". **Still blocked:** quintorius_history_chaser + conspiracy_theorist (their "may discard a card. If you do, …" is an effect-internal optional sub-action, CR 608.2c, not an activation/trigger cost gate — a distinct unlanded mechanism), quintorius_loremaster + conspiracy_theorist (also need #86 play-from-exile); the exile-a-graveyard-card-as-cost flavor never landed.

**Progress (2026-07-11):** 4 of 6 cards now landed. New `Effect::MayDiscard { then }` — the effect-internal optional sub-action (CR 608.2c) the previous progress note flagged as unlanded: pauses on a `PendingChoice::MayDiscard` (empty hand skips straight past) so the controller may discard one card from hand; `then` runs only "if you do", reusing `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s "empty declines, one entry picks" wire shape exactly as `MaySacrifice`/`MayReturnFromGraveyard` do. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** quintorius_history_chaser — its +1 is now `may_discard` with `then = [draw_cards 2, mill_self 1]`; its "whenever cards leave your graveyard, create a 3/2 Spirit" trigger also landed for free on the already-existing `Trigger::CardsLeaveYourGraveyard` (from #81), copied from quintorius_field_historian's identical ability. **Still blocked:** conspiracy_theorist's own may-discard loot still needs #86 play-from-exile for its second ability; quintorius_loremaster also needs #86; the exile-a-graveyard-card-as-cost flavor never landed. Do not mark #82 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-11, later same day):** quintorius_loremaster's dependency on #86 is now resolved — see #86's progress note. Its end-step "exile target noncreature, nonland card from your graveyard" turned out not to need activation-cost plumbing at all: it's a triggered ability's own targeted effect step (`Effect::ExileTargetFromGraveyardWithThis`, CR 603, not a CR 602/118.9 cost), so it landed under #86 instead of here; #82's own remaining scope is unchanged (conspiracy_theorist's may-discard loot, still needing #86 play-from-exile for its second ability). Do not mark #82 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-11, closing slice):** conspiracy_theorist landed — #82 is fully LANDED, 6 of 6 cards. Its "whenever this creature attacks, you may pay {1} and discard a card. If you do, draw a card" reuses the same `optional = true` + `[abilities.cost]` paid-trigger gate as `vanguard_of_the_restless`'s pay-{2}{W}-or-decline, resolving to `Effect::MayDiscard { then = [draw_cards 1] }`; its "whenever you discard one or more nonland cards, you may exile one of them … you may cast it this turn" copies `containment_construct`'s `you_discard` + `exile_from_graveyard_may_play` shape verbatim (the #86 play-from-exile prereq this card was blocked on). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** conspiracy_theorist, modulo three ponytail'd residuals left as gap notes on the card: (1) "pay {1} and discard" modeled as a paid gate then a separate may-discard rather than one all-or-nothing cost — lets a player pay {1} and decline the discard, a strictly-dominated line no one takes; (2) `Trigger::YouDiscard` is unfiltered (fires on a discarded land too, strictly upside); (3) it fires once per discarded card rather than offering one "choose one of them" pick across a multi-card discard (unobservable for single-card discards, the only case this card's own loot produces).

**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed a per-card residual #82's own scope left open — magma_opus's alternative "{U/R}{U/R}, Discard this card: Create a Treasure token." (not one of the 6 cards listed above; it surfaced only after #82 landed). New general primitive, the from-hand sibling of `CardDef::cycling` for a card whose hand-activated ability has an authored payload instead of cycling's fixed draw-1 (CR 113.6/602.5e): `CardDef::hand_ability: Option<HandActivatedAbility>` (`{ cost: Cost, effects: &'static [Effect] }`, `[hand_ability]`/`[hand_ability.cost]`/`[[hand_ability.effects]]` in TOML) plus `Game::activate_hand_ability`/`Intent::ActivateHandAbility`/`MeaningfulAction::ActivateHandAbility` — a line-for-line clone of `Game::cycle`'s skeleton (priority check, hand+owner check, pay cost, discard via `MovedToGraveyard`, keep priority) except the payload is the card's own authored effect list, run inline through `Game::run` (the same resolving-ability executor a stack ability uses) rather than a hardcoded draw. ponytail-noted, mirroring cycling's own: resolved immediately rather than placed on the stack, since no pool card responds to this activation. **Fully faithful (first `approximates` sentence deleted):** magma_opus — its "{U/R}{U/R}, Discard this card: Create a Treasure token." ability is now scripted (`[hand_ability]` with a hybrid `{U/R}{U/R}` cost and a `create_treasure` effect) and offered as a meaningful action from hand. Its sole remaining residual (unrelated to this slice, unchanged): the main spell's divided-damage clause targets creatures/planeswalkers only, not "any number of targets" broadly, since CR 601.2d's division bookkeeping (`DamageAssignment`) is keyed by permanent, not player — a player-as-divided-damage-target is a separate, unbuilt increment.

### 83. `storm-copy-count` — 6 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
**Landed (all 6 faithful):** changing_loyalty (Replicate, CR 702.108), creative_technique + replication_technique (Demonstrate, CR 702.147), mirrorwing_dragon (spell-targets-this copy watch), ominous_harvest (permanents-died-this-turn count), plumb_the_forbidden (sacrifice-count). **Still blocked:** none.
Spell-copy with an `Amount`-scaled count and controller extensions on the landed `SpellCopied` + retarget machinery: Gravestorm (copy per permanent died this turn — Ominous Harvest), copy-per-sacrificed-creature (Plumb the Forbidden, dep #92), copy-for-each-creature with per-copy retargeting (Mirrorwing), Replicate (copy per payment — Changing Loyalty), and Demonstrate's opponent-controlled copy (Creative Technique). Sketch: an on-cast copy rider with an `Amount` count and a copy-controller field; the retarget choice per copy reuses `ChooseSpellTargets`.
*Cards:* changing_loyalty, creative_technique, mirrorwing_dragon, ominous_harvest, plumb_the_forbidden, replication_technique
**Landed:** `Effect::CopyThisSpell { count: Amount }` — a resolution-time rider that mints `count` copies of the resolving spell itself, guarded so a copy never re-fires it (CR 706.9: a copy is never cast); all copies mint up front, then each copy's CR 707.10c retarget is queued one at a time through the existing `resolve_sequence` pause/resume via the internal `Effect::RetargetSpellCopy` so multiple retargeting copies don't clobber each other's `PendingChoice`. Two new `Amount`s feed the count: `SpellSacrificeCount` (creatures sacrificed to the spell's additional cost, reads the existing `spell_sacrifice_count` seam) and a game-wide `PermanentsDiedThisTurn` (new `Game::permanents_died_this_turn`, bumped on `Event::MovedToGraveyard` for a live battlefield `Object::Permanent` — CR 700.4 "died", reset at Untap; counts every player's permanents, any type, unlike the per-controller-creature `CreaturesDiedThisTurn`). ponytail-noted: copies resolve as the spell's own trailing effect rather than CR 706.9's true copy-when-cast stack ordering, and a token's death isn't counted (goes through the ambiguous `TokenCeasedToExist`). **Faithful (notes deleted):** ominous_harvest, plumb_the_forbidden.
**Still blocked:** creative_technique + replication_technique (Demonstrate needs an optional "may copy" + choose-a-copy-controller decision), changing_loyalty (Replicate's copy-per-payment count), mirrorwing_dragon ("whenever a spell targets this, copy it" watch trigger) — untouched.
**Progress (2026-07-14):** Landed the Demonstrate slice (CR 702.147), closing creative_technique and replication_technique. New `CardDef::demonstrate: bool` (a rules-keyword like `cascade`, fabricated at the same cast choke — `Effect::Demonstrate { spell }` placed as a `TriggerGroup` above the cast spell). Resolution pauses on the existing `MayYesNo` "copy it?" surface; accepting mints one copy under the controller via `Game::mint_spell_copies` (its usual CR 707.10c retarget), then pauses the controller on a `PendingChoice::ChooseTarget` (reused, `TargetSpec::OpponentPlayer`-scoped legal list) to choose an opponent, who gets a second copy the same way. The two copies can't share one `mint_spell_copies` call (different controllers, one `ResolveCtx` per call), so a new `Game::pending_demonstrate_opponent_copy: Option<(PlayerId, ObjectId)>` defers the opponent's mint until the controller's own copy's retarget (if any) fully clears — drained by `Game::resume_deferred_sequence`, the same "wait for the current pause" shape `pending_spell_finish` already uses. **Fully faithful (approximates trimmed to only the residual):** replication_technique (`approximates`/`ponytail:` deleted — Demonstrate was its only gap). **Trimmed:** creative_technique — Demonstrate clause deleted from `approximates`; residual is only the pre-existing "in a random order" deterministic-bottom-order stand-in (unrelated to Demonstrate). ponytail-noted on `Effect::Demonstrate`: the two copies mint/retarget sequentially (controller's fully resolved before the opponent's exists) rather than CR 707.10c's true simultaneous-objects-with-APNAP-ordered-retargets — no pool Demonstrate card has a response window that would see the difference (mirrors `CopyThisSpell`'s existing approximation). **Still blocked, untouched — do not conflate with Demonstrate, which is done:** changing_loyalty (Replicate's copy-per-payment count), mirrorwing_dragon ("whenever a spell targets this, copy it" watch trigger). Do not mark #83 LANDED — 2 cards remain.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** Landed mirrorwing_dragon's watch trigger, closing that card. New `Trigger::SpellTargetsThisOnly { filter: SpellFilter }` (`timing = "spell_targets_this"`, reuses `cast_spell`'s `spell_filter` sibling) — a `BecomesTargeted` twin narrowed to "only": fires off the same single-`Target` `Event::SpellCast` field, self-referential on the targeted permanent's own controller (`Game::queue_spell_targets_this_only_triggers`). New `Effect::CopyTriggeringSpellForEachOtherCreatureYouControl { triggering_spell }` (baked in by `fill_triggering_spell`, same context-fill machinery `CopyTriggeringSpell` uses): reads the *spell's own* controller off the still-live triggering spell (not this ability's controller — "that player copies"), enumerates the spell's controller's other creatures the spell's own target spec could legally target (`Game::legal_targets_for`, honoring hexproof/protection), and mints one copy per creature via `SpellCopied` + a direct `SpellTargetsChosen` per copy — set at mint rather than routed through the interactive `RetargetSpellCopy` pause, since the "different one of those creatures" assignment has no player choice to offer (CR 707.10c's per-copy retarget only exists for a chosen count, not an enumerated one). Two `ponytail:`s on the effect: "could target" is approximated as "a legal target of the spell's own spec, other than this permanent" (exact for the pool's single-target instant/sorcery consumers), and the distinct-target assignment is engine-chosen by enumeration order (mirrors `CopyThisSpell`'s existing retarget-ordering approximation). **Fully faithful (approximates/ponytail deleted):** mirrorwing_dragon. **Still blocked:** changing_loyalty (Replicate's copy-per-payment count) — 1 card remains, do not mark #83 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15, closing slice):** Landed Replicate's copy-per-payment count (CR 702.108), closing changing_loyalty. New `AdditionalCost::replicate: Option<&'static Cost>` (`[cost.additional.replicate]`, same `[cost]`-shaped sub-table as the landed `kicker`/`strive` siblings) plus a caster-declared pre-stack `Intent::Cast.replicate_count: u8` (mirroring `strive_count` end to end: folded into `Game::cast_cost` — multiplied by the count directly, not `saturating_sub(1)`, since each replicate payment is a full extra instance of the cost, unlike Strive's "beyond the first" — and recorded on the resulting `Spell::replicate_count`, read via the new `Game::spell_replicate_count`). Unlike Cascade/Demonstrate (rules-keyword *triggered* abilities fabricated at the cast choke), Replicate's copy doesn't use the stack (CR 702.108c) — its copies mint directly inside `Game::cast_with_kind` right after `Event::SpellCast`, reusing the landed `Game::mint_spell_copies(Amount::Fixed(replicate_count), ...)` rider (same per-copy CR 707.10c `RetargetSpellCopy` pause `CopyThisSpell` uses). The pool's real work was CR 707.10a — "a copy of a permanent spell becomes a token as it resolves" — which nothing had exercised yet (every prior `mint_spell_copies` consumer copies an instant/sorcery): `Event::PermanentEntered`'s apply now reads the resolving spell's own `copy` flag and sets the entered `Permanent::token` from it (one shared choke for both the Creature/Enchantment/Artifact/Planeswalker and Aura resolution paths), so a copied permanent already rides every existing token-cease mechanism (dies/sacrifice/bounce/exile) for free. Three real gaps surfaced and fixed along the way, each was previously unreachable because no prior copy consumer targeted a permanent: (1) `Effect::RetargetSpellCopy`'s target-spec lookup only scanned for a `Timing::Spell` ability — meaningless for an Aura, whose cast-target requirement is `CardKind::Aura`-derived, not effect-carried (CR 303.4a) — switched to the general `Game::required_target` helper (already used by the original cast's own legality check), so a copied Aura now gets a real CR 707.10c retarget choice; (2) `resolve_spell`'s `CardKind::Aura` branch sent an illegal-retarget fizzle straight to `MovedToGraveyard` unconditionally — a copy that fails to resolve must cease to exist instead (CR 707.10a/111.7, mirroring `finish_instant_sorcery_resolution`'s own copy guard), fixed with a `spell.copy` guard; (3) the state-based "unattached Aura" sweep (`Game::check_state_based_actions`) also routed every falling-off Aura through `graveyard_or_command` unconditionally — a *token* Aura (a Replicate copy whose host died or was destroyed) needs the same `Permanent::token` branch every other token-leaves-the-battlefield path already has, fixed by checking `p.token` there too. Fixing (3) surfaced a second latent bug it depends on: `Trigger::EnchantedCreatureDies`/`AnEnchantedCreatureDies`'s shared `dying_creature_attachments` snapshot re-read a dying Aura's controller/def live at trigger-queue time (`self.controller_of(aura)`/`self.def_of(aura)`), which panics (or, behind the pre-existing "skip if `Object::Removed`" guard, silently drops the trigger) once a token Aura's own same-batch `TokenCeasedToExist` tombstones it straight to `Object::Removed` with no `Moved` lineage to follow (unlike an ordinary Aura's `MovedToGraveyard`, which still resolves post-move) — fixed by widening the snapshot tuple to capture `(host, aura, controller, def)` at push time (when the Aura is still live) instead of re-deriving them later, and replacing the "is this object Removed" heuristic with the real CR 800.4a condition it was standing in for (`self.players[controller].lost`) so a vanished-but-legitimate token Aura's dies-trigger fires correctly instead of being conflated with "its owner left the game." **Fully faithful (approximates deleted):** changing_loyalty — Replicate copies are token Auras with a real CR 707.10c retarget choice and full copied functionality (a copy attached to an opponent's creature steals it on death exactly like the original). ponytail-noted (mirrors kicker/strive precedent): the cost fold sums generic/colored/colorless pips only (no pool replicate cost carries a hybrid pip), and only a single replicate cost is modeled (Changing Loyalty is the pool's only replicate card). New reusable surface for any future replicate/permanent-copy card: `AdditionalCost::replicate`, `Intent::Cast.replicate_count`/`Spell::replicate_count`, and copied-permanent-spell → token resolution. **All 6 `storm-copy-count` cards are now faithful** (changing_loyalty, creative_technique, mirrorwing_dragon, ominous_harvest, plumb_the_forbidden, replication_technique) — #83 promoted to LANDED.

### 84. `reveal-until` — 6 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Reveal from the top of the library until a condition matches, then route: first nonland (Chaos Warp's replacement land check), an Aura card → hand/battlefield-attached (Songbird's Blessing), until X lands with a variable put-count (Open the Way), reveal-top-then-conditionally-deploy ("if it's a permanent card, put it onto the battlefield" — Chaos Warp; Demonstrate hit — Creative Technique), and reveal-top-and-branch engines (Goblin Guide's defender reveal, Keen Duelist's symmetric MV drain). Sketch: a bounded reveal loop variant of the landed `LookAtTop` with a stop predicate, revealed cards public, plus a conditional dest.
*Cards:* chaos_warp, creative_technique, goblin_guide, keen_duelist, open_the_way, songbirds_blessing
