**Landed:** the count-1 slice — a public reveal (new `Event::RevealedTopOfLibrary`, unlike `LookAtTop`'s private look). `Effect::RevealTopToHand { filter, defender }`: reveals the *defending* player's top card (read off the attack trigger's context, extended to carry `(attacker, defender)` for the self `Trigger::Attacks` too, not just the watch-others triggers) and routes it to hand if it matches `filter`, else it stays on top. `Effect::RevealTopAndDrainMutual` (`TargetSpec::OpponentPlayer`): the controller and the chosen opponent each reveal their top card, each loses life equal to the *other's* mana value, then each puts their own revealed card into hand (not a draw). **Faithful (notes deleted):** goblin_guide, keen_duelist. **Still blocked (notes untouched, no true reveal-until-predicate loop built — count-1 only):** chaos_warp (also needs battlefield→library shuffle-into, #105), creative_technique (needs spell-copy, #83), open_the_way (needs X-scaling, #68/#89), songbirds_blessing (needs Aura re-attach, #79).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the genuine reveal-until-a-count loop, scoped to open_the_way. New `Effect::RevealUntil { filter, count: Amount, matched_dest: SearchDest, matched_tapped: bool, rest_dest: RestDest }` (pure `execute_effect` arm — fully deterministic given the library, no player choice): walks the controller's own top-of-library one card at a time, revealing each publicly (`Event::RevealedTopOfLibrary`) until `count` cards match `filter` or the library runs out (CR 120-style "as many as possible"); each match routes to `matched_dest` (`Battlefield` via the existing `Event::SearchedToBattlefield`, tapped per `matched_tapped`), every other revealed card goes to `rest_dest` (`RestDest::Bottom`, the enum `LookAtTop` already uses — no new enum needed). New `Event::PutOnBottomOfLibrary { player, card }` for the non-matching reveals: a same-zone reorder, not a zone change (CR 400.7), so it reuses the card's existing object id rather than minting a new one the way `TuckedToLibrary` (graveyard→library, a real zone change) does; schema-mirrored as public (the card was already revealed). "In a random order" is approximated as bottom-in-library-order, the same deterministic no-`rand` stand-in `select_from_top`'s `RestDest::Bottom` arm already uses (ponytail-noted on the card). **Fully faithful (approximates + ponytail block deleted):** open_the_way. **Still blocked, each behind a *different* prereq — do not conflate with this landed reveal-until loop:** chaos_warp (needs a battlefield→library tuck, #105, *plus* a reveal-top-**one**-and-maybe-deploy shape, different from reveal-until-N), songbirds_blessing (reveal-until-an-Aura then attach it, #79's choose-host attach), creative_technique (reveal + spell-copy, #83). Do not mark #84 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** chaos_warp's own reveal-top-one-and-maybe-deploy landed as part of closing #105's battlefield→library tuck (`Effect::ShuffleTargetPermanentIntoLibraryThenReveal` — see #105's dated note for the full shape). **Fully faithful (approximates deleted):** chaos_warp. **Still blocked:** songbirds_blessing (needs Aura re-attach, #79), creative_technique (needs spell-copy, #83). Do not mark #84 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed the reveal-until-first-match-with-a-routed-pause slice, closing songbirds_blessing's and creative_technique's reveal-until cores. Two new sibling effects to the landed no-pause `RevealUntil` — kept separate rather than widening it with a pause axis, since `RevealUntil` is deliberately deterministic and makes no player choice: `Effect::RevealUntilMayDeploy { filter }` (songbirds_blessing) and `Effect::RevealUntilExileCastFree { filter }` (creative_technique). Both walk the controller's own top-of-library one card at a time, bottoming every non-match via the same per-card loop shape `RevealUntil` uses, until the first card matching `filter` or the library runs out; a hit pauses instead of auto-routing. `RevealUntilMayDeploy` pauses on a new `PendingChoice::RevealedCardToBattlefieldOrHand` — a single card, left unmoved on top of the library until answered: accepting routes it via the existing `Event::SearchedToBattlefield` (untapped), declining via `Event::SearchedToHand`. `RevealUntilExileCastFree` reuses #86's `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledDigToCastFree` outright (a single-candidate batch: `candidates = exiled = vec![hit]`), no new pending-choice needed. New `CardFilter::Nonland` (the inverse of `Land`). New `Effect::ShuffleLibrary` (TOML `shuffle_library`, untargeted, `&mut self`-only for the injected PRNG) precedes creative_technique's reveal-until step as its own `[[abilities.effects]]` in the same `Sequence` (CR 701.19's mandatory shuffle before the reveal). Found and fixed a pre-existing engine bug along the way, with a regression test: `Game::queue_permanent_enters_triggers` unconditionally read the live-only `self.permanent(entering)`, which panics when the entering permanent already left the battlefield in the same event batch's state-based sweep (CR 704's SBAs precede trigger placement) — an unattached Aura (CR 704.5m) hits exactly this path; fixed to read it via `Game::as_permanent` instead. **Trimmed (each still carries a residual — not fully faithful):** songbirds_blessing — the reveal-until-Aura loop, the battlefield-or-hand pause, and the hand routing are all faithful now; the residual is CR 303.4f's attach-a-host step (#79's choose-host `PendingChoice`, unbuilt) — an Aura accepted onto the battlefield this way enters unattached, which CR 704.5m makes illegal, so the very next state-based sweep immediately puts it into the graveyard (same residual armored_skyhunter's dig already carries). creative_technique — the shuffle-then-reveal-until-nonland-exile-cast-free core is faithful now; the residual is Demonstrate (the copy-on-cast rider — "you may copy it, if you do, choose an opponent to also copy it" — a shared gap with replication_technique, not a reveal-until behavior, out of scope here).
**Landed:** the reveal-until capability is complete across every reveal-until shape (reveal-until-N, reveal-until-first-match with a routed battlefield/hand or exile-cast-free pause, reveal-top-one-and-deploy, reveal-and-branch). **Faithful (notes deleted):** goblin_guide, keen_duelist, open_the_way, chaos_warp. **Still blocked (notes trimmed to the residual, each gated on a *different* increment, not on reveal-until):** songbirds_blessing (Aura choose-host attach, #79 — an accepted Aura enters unattached and CR 704.5m sweeps it to the graveyard), creative_technique (Demonstrate/spell-copy, #83).
**Progress (2026-07-13):** the deploy-time choose-host `PendingChoice::ChooseAttachHostForAura` landed (see #79's dated note), closing songbirds_blessing's attach-a-host residual — an Aura accepted onto the battlefield off the reveal now pauses its controller to choose a legal host (CR 303.4f); with no legal host it stays unattached for CR 704.5m to sweep. **Trimmed (residual is now only the random-order stand-in — `approximates` reduced to `"in a random order"` → deterministic bottom-order):** songbirds_blessing. Still blocked: creative_technique (Demonstrate/spell-copy, #83).

### 85. `cost-reduction-dynamic-2` — 6 cards, M
Grow the landed `reduce_own_generic`/`ReduceSpellCost` pair: a `Condition` gate ("{2} less if you gained life this turn" — Mortality Spear; the flag exists), `PerPermanentMatching` scaling (affinity for Auras — Pearl-Ear; for planeswalkers — Tomik), a summed-power amount ("{1} less per total power" — Volcanic Salvo), a per-graveyard-card-type count (Furygale — instant/sorcery cards in your graveyard), and a cast-zone predicate ("spells you cast from anywhere other than your hand cost {2} less" — Advanced Reconstruction level 3; flashback/escape/impulse already carry their source zone).
*Cards:* advanced_reconstruction, furygale_flocking, mortality_spear, pearl_ear_imperial_advisor, tomik_wielder_of_law, volcanic_salvo

**Progress (2026-07):** 3 of 6 cards landed. New `Amount::TotalPowerYouControl` (`"total_power_you_control"`) and `Amount::IfCondition { condition, then }` (the `{ condition = ..., then = ... }` table form), both resolved through `reduce_own_generic`'s existing `resolve_amount` at cast time. Fully faithful (notes deleted): volcanic_salvo ("{X} less where X is total power of creatures you control"), mortality_spear ("{2} less if you gained life this turn" — `{ condition = { type = "you_gained_life_this_turn" }, then = 2 }`). Trimmed: tomik_wielder_of_law — affinity for planeswalkers is now faithful (`reduce_own_generic = { per_permanent = { types = ["planeswalker"] } }`); note trimmed to the residual punisher trigger (#91). **Still blocked:** pearl_ear_imperial_advisor (its "enchantment spells you cast have affinity for Auras" discounts *other* spells, needing a dynamic-`Amount` `reduce_spell_cost` + enchantment filter, not the self-reducer), advanced_reconstruction (cast-zone predicate, #133), furygale_flocking (per-graveyard-card-type count).

**Progress (2026-07-11):** 4 of 6 cards now landed. `Effect::ReduceSpellCost.amount` grew from a bare `u8` to a live `Amount`, resolved through the same `Game::resolve_amount` as `reduce_own_generic` (source = the reducer permanent, `x = 0`), clamped to `>= 0` and summed across every matching reducer in `Game::cost_reduction`. **Fully faithful (note trimmed):** pearl_ear_imperial_advisor — "Enchantment spells you cast have affinity for Auras" is now `reduce_spell_cost` with `amount = { per_permanent = { subtypes = ["Aura"], controller = "you" } }` and `filter = "enchantment"`; its note is trimmed to only the residual "targets a modified permanent" draw trigger (dep #90's still-unlanded "modified" `PermanentFilter` predicate). **Still blocked:** furygale_flocking's graveyard instant/sorcery count turned out structural, not small — `TypeSet`/`CardKind::types()` has no INSTANT/SORCERY bit, and `CardFilter::Permanent`/`PermanentWithManaValueAtMost`/`NonlandPermanentWithManaValueAtMost` (search-library filters used by several other cards) rely on `CardKind::Spell.types().is_empty()` to exclude instants/sorceries from "permanent" matches — adding those bits would silently make every instant/sorcery match those "permanent" search filters too. Needs a graveyard-scoped spell-speed axis that doesn't touch `TypeSet`, not attempted this slice. advanced_reconstruction unchanged (cast-zone predicate, #133).

**Progress (2026-07-11):** 5 of 6 cards now landed. furygale_flocking's graveyard instant/sorcery count turned out not to need the `TypeSet` route the prior note flagged as structural — a bespoke `Amount::InstantOrSorceryCardsInYourGraveyard` reads `CardKind::Spell` directly off each graveyard card (reusing the existing `Game::graveyard_cards` enumerator, no `TypeSet` bit touched, no risk to the `CardFilter::Permanent`-family search filters). Wired as `reduce_own_generic = "instant_or_sorcery_cards_in_your_graveyard"`, resolved through the same `Game::resolve_amount` as `total_power_you_control`. **Fully faithful (note trimmed):** furygale_flocking — cost reduction is now exact; note trimmed to the still-flattened per-opponent token scaling and the unmodeled forced-attack rider. **Still blocked:** advanced_reconstruction unchanged (cast-zone predicate, #133).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed the "once-per-turn dynamic self-reducer" this section names but that none of its own 6 listed cards forced — zimone_infinite_analyst (not one of the 6; a separate consumer of the same `ReduceSpellCost` machinery). New `Effect::ReduceSpellCost.first_x_spell_each_turn: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`) gates the reducer to the controller's first spell this turn matching `filter`, read in `Game::cost_reduction` off the already-existing `Player::x_spells_cast_this_turn` tally (no new per-turn state — `cost_reduction` runs before the current cast's own tally bump, so a 0 reading means this cast is the turn's first). zimone_infinite_analyst is `reduce_spell_cost { amount = "per_counter_on_source", filter = "has_x", first_x_spell_each_turn = true }`, paired with its already-landed counter-trigger ability. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** zimone_infinite_analyst. ponytail: the gate is wired specifically to the {X}-spell tally (Zimone's only pool consumer, `filter = "has_x"`) rather than a general per-filter "first matching this turn" counter; a differently-filtered once-per-turn reducer needs its own per-turn tally. **#85 itself is NOT fully landed** — advanced_reconstruction (this section's own 6th listed card) is still blocked on the unrelated cast-zone predicate (#133); do not mark #85 LANDED.

### 86. `free-cast-from-exile` — 5 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
The "may cast while exiled" generalization v1 #37 left open: a cast permission on source-linked exile piles checked in `Game::cast`'s `playable_zone`, with an expiry key ("this turn" / "for as long as it remains exiled") and a pay-nothing flavor (cast-without-paying-mana-cost — Plargg's upkeep exile-and-cast, Loremaster's cast-from-exile ability, Herald of Amity's dig-and-cast-free Aura, Renegade Bull's exile-a-copy-then-cast-free). Conspiracy Theorist's discard-to-impulse-cast is the smallest slice. The impulse-play permission and `exiled_with` piles exist; this is the permission entry + free-cost flag.
*Cards:* conspiracy_theorist, herald_of_amity, plargg_and_nassari, quintorius_loremaster, renegade_bull

**Progress (2026-07-11):** the core pay-nothing permission landed, with quintorius_loremaster as its one faithful consumer. New `play_permissions.cast_from_exile_free: Vec<(ObjectId, PlayerId)>` (`state.rs`), distinct from the pre-existing `play_from_exile` (which still charges normal cost) — checked in `playable_zone`'s `Zone::Exile` arm and forced to `Cost::FREE` in `cast_cost` (CR 118.5 "without paying its mana cost"), cleared unconditionally at cleanup (`Event::CastFromExileFreeEnded`, no `until_next_turn` extension needed yet). New `Effect::CastExiledWithThisFree` (Quintorius's activated ability) pauses on a `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledWithCardToCast` over the source's `exiled_with` pile — "up to one," mirroring `CashOutExiledWithThis`/`ChooseExiledWithCard` exactly, except accepting grants the free-cast permission instead of cashing the card out (it stays in the pile). Also landed, as a prerequisite: `Effect::ExileTargetFromGraveyardWithThis` (a targeted counterpart to `ExileDiscardedWithThis`, hardcoding a `noncreature_nonland` `CardFilter` target since the target restriction is fixed) for Quintorius's end step — this turned out to be a plain triggered-ability target step, not an activation cost, so it also resolves #82's still-open quintorius_loremaster item (#82 stays not-LANDED; see its own note). **Fully faithful (note trimmed):** quintorius_loremaster — residual is only the activated ability's "if that spell would be put into a graveyard, put it on the bottom of its owner's library instead" replacement rider (a replacement effect scoped to one cast object, #128 territory), untouched.
**Still blocked, each behind a *different* unlanded prereq — do not conflate with the free-cast permission itself, which is now done:** conspiracy_theorist (needs a "whenever you discard" trigger paired with *normal-cost* impulse play, not free-cast — a different permission entirely); herald_of_amity (needs a filtered dig-8-and-cast-an-Aura reveal effect + a dynamic-Aura-count pump, neither built); plargg_and_nassari (needs each-player-exile-from-library + opponent-chooses, #107); renegade_bull (needs copy-a-graveyard-instant/sorcery, #83's copy machinery, extended to a graveyard source). Do not mark #86 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed the dig-and-cast-an-Aura-free slice, herald_of_amity as its sole consumer. New `Effect::ExileTopCastMatchingFree { count: u32, filter: CardFilter }` (TOML `exile_top_cast_matching_free`) exiles the top `count` library cards face-up via a new `Event::ExiledFromLibraryToChooseCastFree` (mirrors `ExiledFromLibraryMayPlay`'s zone-move/library-retain shape but attaches no play permission), then pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledDigToCastFree` — "up to one" over the subset matching `filter`, mirroring `ChooseExiledWithCardToCast`'s public (non-`private_items`) exile-zone visibility. Unlike that sibling, answering here also sweeps every *other* card in the exiled batch (non-matching, or simply not chosen) to the bottom of the library via `Event::TuckedToLibrary` (its `create_object`-based apply is zone-agnostic, so the existing graveyard→library event reuses cleanly for exile→library too) — a genuine second rule that `ChooseExiledWithCardToCast`'s pile doesn't have (its non-chosen candidates just stay put). No candidates matching `filter` skips the pause entirely and bottoms the whole batch immediately (mirrors `begin_cast_exiled_with_this_free`'s empty-pile no-op). New `CardFilter::Aura` (TOML `"aura"`, the `AuraOrEquipment` reader minus the Equipment half). The attack pump was pure authoring, no engine change: `power`/`toughness = { per_permanent = { subtypes = ["Aura"], controller = "you" } }` on the already-landed `Effect::PumpSelfUntilEndOfTurn`, the same shape #95's Eidolon of Countless Battles/Sage's Reverie already prove. herald_of_amity is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted; two `ponytail:` code comments remain: the free cast is offered at a later priority window than mid-resolution, and "random order" for the bottomed rest is the deterministic library-order stand-in every impulse-dig effect in this pool uses). **Still blocked, unchanged prereqs:** plargg_and_nassari (#107, each-player-exile-from-library + opponent-chooses), renegade_bull (#83 extended to a graveyard source, copy-a-graveyard-instant/sorcery). conspiracy_theorist untouched this slice (its own distinct normal-cost impulse-play permission). Do not mark #86 LANDED — 2 cards remain.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed renegade_bull's exile-a-copy-then-cast-free attack trigger, the #83-extended-to-a-graveyard-source slice. New `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardSpellAndCopyFree { filter: CardFilter }` (TOML `exile_target_graveyard_spell_and_copy_free`) — a targeted counterpart to `ExileTargetFromGraveyardWithThis` with an authored `filter` instead of a fixed one — exiles the "up to one" chosen graveyard target, then mints one free copy of it onto the stack via `Game::mint_spell_copies` (the same Storm/Twincast core `Effect::CopyThisSpell` uses), with the just-exiled card standing in for a live spell as the copy source. `mint_spell_copies` could not take an arbitrary `CardDef` source outright — its `Event::SpellCopied` apply arm hard-required a live `Object::Spell` (`self.spell(original)`) — so this slice widened that one apply arm (`apply.rs`) to also accept an `Object::Card` source (graveyard/exile), defaulting the fields a bare card doesn't carry (targets/x/modes/flashback/escape/sacrifice_count/kicked) the same way `PreparedSpellCast`'s from-a-`CardDef` mint already does; behavior for every existing live-spell `SpellCopied` caller (Twincast, storm, Gravestorm) is unchanged. That widening is exactly the reusable primitive #86's own brief flagged for surge_to_victory's copy clause once that card is in scope — note left here for whoever picks it up. renegade_bull's attack trigger is now scripted (`approximates` trimmed to its residuals): the mint routes through `Event::SpellCopied`, so only Magecraft triggers fire for the free copy (CR 707.10's "cast or copy" watch), not a general "whenever you cast a spell" trigger — Renegade Bull's own first ability (a `Trigger::CastSpell`, not Magecraft) does not refire off its own free copy; and the effect's fixed `min:1` target count models "up to one target"/"you may cast" as mandatory once a legal target exists (no decline). **Still blocked:** plargg_and_nassari (#107, each-player-exile-from-library + opponent-chooses) is the only card left in #86. Do not mark #86 LANDED — 1 card remains.
**Progress (2026-07-12) — #86 LANDED:** plargg_and_nassari's upkeep exile-and-cast landed as part of #107 (`opponent-chooses`), consuming the #86 free-cast permission (`Event::CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted`) for the "cast up to two … without paying their mana costs" clause. All five cards now script their cast-from-exile-without-paying mechanic; the residual `approximates` remaining on quintorius_loremaster (#128 replacement rider), renegade_bull (#83 Magecraft-only copy nuance), and plargg_and_nassari (#107's next-opponent / later-priority-window ponytails) are all outside #86's free-cast scope. #86 is complete.
**Progress (2026-07-15, renegade_bull closing slice):** Closed renegade_bull's own residual left by the 2026-07-12 note above — its attack trigger's free copy now fires real "whenever you cast" watchers, including its own +X/+0. `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardSpellAndCopyFree` renamed to `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardSpellCastFree` (TOML `exile_target_graveyard_spell_cast_free`, sole consumer renegade_bull) and repointed off `Game::mint_spell_copies` onto the #86 free-cast-permission primitive: it exiles the chosen graveyard card, then pushes `Event::CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted` for it directly (no pending choice needed — the target is already the ability's own chosen target), the same event `cast_exiled_with_this_free` (Quintorius) grants. The controller now genuinely *casts* the exiled card at their next opportunity via the ordinary `Intent::Cast` free-cast-from-exile path (`cast.rs`'s `may_cast_from_exile_free` check, `Cost::FREE`), so it's a real `Event::SpellCast` — Renegade Bull's own `Trigger::CastSpell` ability fires off it (+X/+0, X = the cast spell's mana value) and so does every other "whenever you cast an instant or sorcery" watcher on the battlefield, not just Magecraft. Also closed the "up to one target"/"you may cast" mandatory approximation the 2026-07-12 note flagged: the effect gained a `count: TargetCount` field (`#[serde(default)]`, `{1,1}`; Renegade Bull authors `{0,1}`) — reusing the existing `ChooseTarget { optional }` pending-choice plumbing (`min == 0` already wires an optional pause there) — so the controller may now decline the graveyard target outright even with a legal one available, and separately may simply not act on the granted free-cast permission ("you may cast" falls out for free once casting is the controller's own later choice rather than an automatic mint). **Fully faithful (`approximates` deleted):** renegade_bull. `ponytail:` left on the effect: CR 707.10c's literal reading mints a copy and casts *that*; this casts the exiled card itself instead (the same "cast that card" shape `cast_exiled_with_this_free`/`exile_top_cast_matching_free` already use for their own free casts) — unobservable for this pool, since nothing reads the resolved spell's post-resolution zone (a true copy ceases to exist there; the exiled original goes to its owner's graveyard normally instead). No other #86 card touched; #86 stays LANDED.

### 87. `aura-lifecycle-payoffs` — 5 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
The unlanded v1 #43 halves on the landed `EnchantedCreatureDies` snapshot machinery: `Trigger::ThisAuraLeaves` / Aura-put-into-graveyard ("when this is put into a graveyard from the battlefield, return it to hand" — Fallen Ideal; "sacrifice it when this leaves" — Animate Dead's rider), and host-dies look-back payoffs acting on "that card": reanimate the dying host (Gift of Immortality, with #74's next-end-step return), return this Aura from the graveyard attached to a new creature (Ghoulish Impetus, dep #79), and Changing Loyalty's reanimate-under-your-control.
*Cards:* animate_dead, changing_loyalty, fallen_ideal, ghoulish_impetus, gift_of_immortality
**Landed:** `Trigger::ThisAuraLeaves` (TOML timing `"this_put_into_graveyard"`) — a self-referential, permanent-kind-agnostic twin of `Trigger::Dies`, fired off `Event::MovedToGraveyard`/`Event::TokenCeasedToExist`, guarded (via `BatchTriggerScratch::permanents_put_into_graveyard_from_battlefield`, captured at `apply.rs`'s `MovedToGraveyard` choke point) to objects that were a live battlefield `Object::Permanent` immediately before the move, so a milled/discarded copy of the same card does not fire it. Reuses the existing `Effect::ReturnThisToHand`. fallen_ideal's return-to-hand rider is now faithful; its `approximates` is trimmed to only the still-dropped granted activated ability (#123).
**Landed (2026-07, reanimate-dying-enchanted-creature slice):** `Effect::ReanimateDyingEnchantedCreature { under_owner }` (TOML `reanimate_dying_enchanted_creature`) — a `TriggerContext::dying_enchanted_creature` look-back payoff off the already-landed `Trigger::EnchantedCreatureDies`, reanimating the specific creature the Aura was attached to when it died ("that card", CR 603.10a last-known information) under either the ability's own controller (`under_owner = false` — changing_loyalty's "under your control") or the card's owner (`under_owner = true` — gift_of_immortality's "under its owner's control"); guard-returns if that card no longer sits in a graveyard (exiled in response). Shares its ETB/event plumbing with `Effect::ReanimateToBattlefield` via a factored `Game::reanimate_event` core. changing_loyalty is now faithful (its former continuous-control-Aura approximation is replaced with the real dies-trigger; `approximates` trimmed to only the unlanded Replicate rider, #83). gift_of_immortality's reanimate clause is now faithful; `approximates` trimmed to only its second sentence (return this Aura to the battlefield attached to that creature at the next end step — needs a graveyard-Aura-return-attached-to-a-specific-creature delayed effect, a separate unlanded primitive; #74's next-end-step delay alone isn't enough).
**Still blocked:** animate_dead's "sacrifice it when this leaves" needs a leaves-*any*-zone thread (not just graveyard-from-battlefield) plus host-reference plumbing to act on the enchanted creature.
**Progress (2026-07-13):** ghoulish_impetus landed — see #74/#79's 2026-07-13 notes for the mechanism (`Effect::ReturnThisAuraFromGraveyardAttachedToChosenHost`/`ScheduleReturnThisAuraFromGraveyardAttachedToChosenHost`, reusing #79's `ChooseAttachHostForAura`). **Faithful (note deleted):** ghoulish_impetus. **Still blocked:** animate_dead's "sacrifice it when this leaves" (unchanged, above) is the only card left on #87's list.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** animate_dead landed — **#87 is now LANDED**, every listed card is faithful (to its established residual). Part A, the "-1/-0" static, was free: a second `[[abilities]] timing = "static"` with the already-landed `grant_to_attached { power = -1, toughness = 0 }` (`Amount::Fixed` already accepts negative literals, screams_from_within precedent — no engine change). Part B is the real work: a new leaves-to-*any*-zone self-trigger, distinct from `Trigger::ThisAuraLeaves` (which stays graveyard-only, Fallen Ideal's own semantics untouched). New `Trigger::ThisPermanentLeavesBattlefield` (TOML `this_leaves_battlefield`) fires off `MovedToGraveyard`/`MovedToExile`/`ReturnedToHand`/`TuckedToLibrary`/`TokenCeasedToExist` — a new `BatchTriggerScratch::permanents_left_battlefield: Vec<(ObjectId, Option<ObjectId>)>` captures `(pre-move id, `Game::attached_to` host)` at each of those `Game::apply` exit choke points, mirroring exactly where/how `permanents_put_into_graveyard_from_battlefield` is populated (CR 603.10a last-known information, read before the exit tears the attachment down). A new `Game::queue_leaves_battlefield_triggers` helper (triggers.rs) looks the exiting object up in that scratch and fires the trigger with the captured host threaded into a new `TriggerContext::left_battlefield_host: Option<ObjectId>`. New `Effect::SacrificeEnchantedCreature { creature: Option<ObjectId> }` (`#[serde(skip)]`, baked from `ctx.left_battlefield_host` via a new `fill_left_battlefield_host` contextualize-effect hook, mirroring `fill_dying_enchanted_creature`) resolves by reusing the existing sacrifice choke (`Game::sacrifice_event` + `Event::Sacrificed`, `by` = the *creature's own* controller, not the ability's — CR "that creature's controller sacrifices it") with the same guard-return shape as `Effect::SacrificeObject`: no-op if the context never captured a host, or if that creature no longer sits on the battlefield. One non-obvious wrinkle surfaced and fixed: the new `MovedToExile`/`ReturnedToHand`/`TuckedToLibrary` trigger-scan arm needs the same `Object::Removed` guard the `MovedToGraveyard` arm already carries (CR 800.4a — a card whose owner leaves the game in the same SBA sweep is already gone by the time triggers scan the batch; caught by the pre-existing `dirgur_does_not_prepare_on_flashback_instant` regression test, which exercises a flashback spell's own post-resolution exile coinciding with an empty-library loss). Also surfaced (documented, not a bug): animate_dead is typed `enchantment` not `aura` kind (the established reanimate-on-ETB approximation), so CR 704.5m's Aura-orphan state-based action doesn't apply to it — when its host dies first, it merely becomes unattached and stays on the battlefield rather than falling off to the graveyard; the `animate_dead_no_op_if_host_already_gone` test exercises the resulting fizzle path (a host-less `SacrificeEnchantedCreature`) rather than the SBA-orphan path the brief sketched, since that path doesn't arise for this card. `approximates` trimmed to only the reanimate-on-ETB residual ("enchant creature card in a graveyard" approximated by reanimate-on-ETB rather than selecting a graveyard card at cast). **Faithful (note trimmed):** animate_dead.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed animate_dead's remaining "enchant creature card in a graveyard" residual — the graveyard target is now chosen AT CAST (CR 303.4a/601.2c, respondable), not a fresh pick after the Aura's already on the battlefield. New `CardDef.enchant_graveyard: bool` (TOML `enchant_graveyard = true`) — the graveyard-card twin of `enchant`'s battlefield-permanent Aura target — makes `Game::required_target` report `TargetSpec::CreatureCardInAnyGraveyard` for the card at cast, same as any other Aura's enchant-subject requirement. The chosen target is locked onto the entering permanent as a new `Permanent::cast_time_enchant_target: Option<ObjectId>` (`Event::PermanentEntered`'s apply arm, mirroring the existing `entered_with_x` "read the spell before it's gone" idiom — the `Spell` object is destroyed by the time the card's own `etb` ability resolves). A new `TargetSpec::ThisAurasGraveyardTarget` (TOML `"this_auras_graveyard_target"`) reads that captured id back as a **fixed reference** — the same no-pause, no-shroud/hexproof-check treatment `"this"`/`"enchanted_creature"` already get in `Game::place_targeted_ability` and `Game::legal_targets_for` — so the card's `reanimate_to_battlefield` effect places straight onto the stack with the cast-time choice already fixed, empty (CR 603.3c: ability dropped) if that card has since left the graveyard. `Game::resolve_spell` gained a CR 608.2b/303.4f-style fizzle re-check scoped to `enchant_graveyard` cards (the pool's only non-Aura-kind permanent with a cast-time target): if the chosen graveyard card is exiled in response before Animate Dead resolves, the Aura goes straight to the graveyard rather than entering unattached. Kind stays `enchantment`, not `aura` (per the brief: the `CardKind::Aura` resolution path expects an existing battlefield host to attach to, which a graveyard card isn't yet) — `approximates` trimmed to that residual only (kind tag + the "loses/gains enchant ability" self-rewrite modeled implicitly as staying attached). **animate_dead is now fully faithful to its established residual** (the kind-tag note is the only thing left, matching the brief's allowed trim). New engine tests: `animate_dead_targets_graveyard_creature_at_cast` (no-target cast is illegal; the chosen target causes no `PendingChoice` at cast or at ETB placement), `animate_dead_fizzles_if_target_exiled_in_response` (CR 608.2b). `ponytail:` narrow single-card scope on both the new `enchant_graveyard` field and `ThisAurasGraveyardTarget` — the pool has exactly one Aura whose enchant subject is a graveyard card.

### 88. `token-entry-riders` — 5 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
Entry riders on token creation and `CreateTokenCopy` (which landed with fixed count and plain entry): enters tapped-and-attacking (myriad — Redoubled Stormsinger; Combat Calligrapher's Inkling, which also enters under the *attacking player's* control — extend `TokenController` with the trigger's subject player and hook the declared-attack state mid-combat), gains haste (Rionya), and copying the set of tokens that entered this turn (dep #70's timestamp). Pairs with #74 for the exile/sacrifice-at-end-step cleanup.
*Cards:* combat_calligrapher, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, twinflame
**Progress (2026-07-11):** the "gains haste" rider landed for `Effect::CreateTokenCopy` — a `haste: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`) that, when set, pushes an until-EOT `Event::TempBoost { keywords: &[Keyword::Haste] }` per minted token (reusing the existing keyword-union event, no schema change). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** determined_iteration. **Still blocked:** the tapped-and-attacking/myriad/attacking-player-controller half (combat_calligrapher, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, twinflame) is untouched — needs `TokenController`'s attacking-player extension and mid-combat attack-state hookup, not attempted this slice. rionya_fire_dancer also wants "gains haste" but is blocked on begin-combat-cast tracking + variable-P/T (#89), unrelated prereqs, not this rider. Do not mark #88 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the tapped-and-attacking/attacking-player-controller slice, scoped to combat_calligrapher only. New `Effect::CreateToken.enters_tapped_and_attacking: bool` (TOML, `#[serde(default)]` false) plus an internal (never TOML-authored, `#[serde(skip)]`) `attacking_context: Option<(PlayerId, PlayerId)>` baked from `TriggerContext::attack` by a new `contextualize_effect` `CreateToken` arm at trigger placement — the same "watch-others payload fill" shape `RevealTopToHand`/`DefendingPlayerSacrifices` already use. At resolution, a `Some(attacking_context)` overrides the `TokenController` recipient match (CR 111.4: minted under the *attacking* player) and each minted token gets a `Tapped` event plus a new `Event::TokenEnteredAttacking { token, defender }` (pushes into `combat.attackers`/`attack_targets`, mirroring `AttackerDeclared`'s apply arm). `TokenEnteredAttacking` deliberately carries no trigger-scan arm — CR 508.4, a token put onto the battlefield attacking was never declared as an attacker, so reusing `AttackerDeclared` here would re-fire Combat Calligrapher and infinite-loop; the omission is the fix (regression-tested: exactly one token mints, no loop). Schema mirror added (`VisibleEvent::TokenEnteredAttacking` + projection arm; combat state is public, no redaction). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** combat_calligrapher. **Still blocked, untouched:** redoubled_stormsinger (myriad copy set, needs #70's entered-this-turn permanent-filter timestamp axis too), twinflame (Strive escalating per-target cost, #85), muddle_the_ever_changing (become-a-copy-until-EOT, #127), rionya_fire_dancer (begin-combat spells-cast count + temporary copies, #89/#83). Do not mark #88 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed twinflame's `haste`/`sacrifice_at_next_end_step` riders on its existing `create_token_copy` (already-landed `Effect::CreateTokenCopy` fields — no engine change) and rionya_fire_dancer's whole begin-combat trigger. New `Player::instants_and_sorceries_cast_this_turn: u32` tally (sibling of `greatest_instant_or_sorcery_mana_value_cast_this_turn`: bumped in the `Event::SpellCast` apply arm's existing instant-or-sorcery guard, reset at Untap; a copied spell doesn't bump it, same "cast" boundary as the mv tally) plus a new `Amount::OnePlusInstantsAndSorceriesCastThisTurn` (TOML `"one_plus_instants_and_sorceries_cast_this_turn"`, a live read like the mv `Amount`, `tally + 1`; ponytail: the baked "one plus" is Rionya-specific — split into a raw count + successor combinator if a second card needs a different offset). rionya_fire_dancer's ability is `timing = "begin_combat"` + `create_token_copy { target = { permanent = { types = "creature", controller = "you", other = true } }, count = "one_plus_instants_and_sorceries_cast_this_turn", haste = true, sacrifice_at_next_end_step = true }` — `other = true` excludes Rionya herself from her own "another target creature you control," and `begin_combat` is already controller-scoped (no intervening-if needed, unlike Rootha's conditional trigger). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** rionya_fire_dancer. **Trimmed to its Strive residual only (multi-target/escalating-cost, #85 territory):** twinflame — haste and the end-step exile are now faithful. **Still blocked, untouched:** redoubled_stormsinger (needs #70's entered-this-turn timestamp for its myriad copy set), muddle_the_ever_changing (#127 become-a-copy). Do not mark #88 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed redoubled_stormsinger — an assembly of already-landed pieces, no new prereq. New single-purpose `Effect::CopyEachEnteredThisTurnTokenTappedAttacking { attacking_context }` (no target — enumerates internally): `attacking_context: Option<(PlayerId, PlayerId)>` is filled by a new `contextualize_effect` arm from `TriggerContext::attack` at trigger placement, the same "watch payload fill" shape `CreateToken.attacking_context` (#88's combat_calligrapher slice) already uses, paired with `timing = "attacks"` (`Trigger::Attacks`, already self-referential and already populates `ctx.attack`, so no `triggers.rs` change was needed). At resolution it scans the attacking player's own battlefield for `token && creature && controller_you && entered_this_turn` (the already-landed `PermanentFilter.entered_this_turn` axis, #70) and, per match, mints a copy reusing `CreateToken`'s tapped-and-attacking apply path (`Event::Tapped` + `Event::TokenEnteredAttacking`, never `AttackerDeclared` — CR 508.4, so a minted copy can't re-trigger Redoubled itself; regression-tested) and schedules `CreateTokenCopy`'s `sacrifice_at_next_end_step` delayed trigger (`Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled` → `Effect::SacrificeObject` at `Step::End`) verbatim. No schema change (`Effect` is card-dsl-only; the events it emits were already wire-mirrored by the combat_calligrapher slice). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** redoubled_stormsinger. This also clears redoubled_stormsinger off #74's still-blocked list (its delayed sacrifice-at-next-end-step is the same already-landed `Step::End` delayed-trigger machinery #74 covers). **Still blocked:** muddle_the_ever_changing — its Magecraft "becomes a copy of another target creature you control ... and gains myriad" needs #127 (become-a-copy-until-EOT), an XL, unbuilt prereq. Do not mark #88 LANDED — one card remains.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed muddle_the_ever_changing, this entry's last card, now that #127 (become-a-copy-until-EOT) is built. Two new effects on the landed `BecameCopy`/`ChooseTarget` substrate: `Effect::BecomeCopyOfTargetCreatureGainingMyriad { target }` — a real CR 601.2c target (not a resolution-time pause; "up to one" is `optional = true` on the magecraft ability, the same shape Skyclave Apparition's "up to one target" already uses) that on resolution emits an until-EOT `BecameCopy` plus an until-EOT `myriad` keyword grant via `TempBoost` (the same "gains a keyword" shape `Game::answer_enter_as_copy`'s `gains_haste` rider uses) — and `Effect::MyriadTokenCopies`, the myriad payload itself: never TOML-authored, synthesized by a new `Game::queue_myriad_triggers` off a new `Keyword::Myriad` the same way Prowess's pump is synthesized from `Keyword::Prowess` (`Game::queue_prowess_triggers`). For each opponent other than the defending player it mints a tapped-and-attacking token copy of the attacker's current characteristics (`Event::TokenCreated`/`Tapped`/`TokenEnteredAttacking`, never `AttackerDeclared` — CR 508.4, so a minted copy can't re-trigger myriad; regression-tested, same pattern as combat_calligrapher/redoubled_stormsinger), reusing `Game::token_count_after_replacements` for Doubling Season, and schedules the token's exile at the *true* end of combat via `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled { fire_at: Step::EndCombat }` — `Step::EndCombat` was already a `fire_delayed_triggers` boundary (Decayed's own sacrifice uses it), so no new drain site was needed and no residual end-step-vs-end-of-combat note is required. New `PermanentFilter.nonlegendary: bool` axis (CR 205.4a) for "nonlegendary creature you control." **Fully faithful (note + ponytail header deleted):** muddle_the_ever_changing — both the become-a-copy trigger and its granted myriad are scripted. New engine tests: `muddle_becomes_copy_of_chosen_creature_until_end_of_turn_on_magecraft`, `muddle_magecraft_declined_no_copy`, `muddle_copy_has_myriad_mints_tapped_attacking_copies_per_opponent`, `muddle_myriad_tokens_exiled_at_end_of_combat`. **This lands #88 — all 5 cards (combat_calligrapher, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, twinflame) are now faithful** (twinflame's own Strive residual cleared separately under #85, wave 130). **#88 `token-entry-riders` LANDED (2026-07-15).**

### 89. `variable-pt-tokens` — 5 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Token base P/T and enters-with-counters set from a dynamic `Amount` at creation, routed through the counter-replacement pipeline: Manaform Hellkite's X/X Dragon Illusion (X = the cast spell's MV, dep #65's context read), Rootha's X/X off spells-cast-this-turn, Fractal Harness / Lattice Library's variable-counter 0/0 Fractals (which die without their counters — the SBA sweep already handles that), and Oversimplify's per-player Fractal with counters equal to each player's exiled power.
*Cards:* fractal_harness, lattice_library, manaform_hellkite, oversimplify, rootha_mastering_the_moment
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the enters-with-*counters* slice only (not base-P/T-set-from-Amount): `Effect::CreateToken` gained `enters_with: Amount` (TOML `enters_with`, `#[serde(default)]` zero — behavior-preserving), applied to each minted token via `Game::counters_after_replacements` (CR 614 doublers/Hardened Scales apply) in a new `Game::resolve_effect` special case, since placing counters needs the token already in game state (`execute_effect` is pure `&self` and can't apply mid-resolution). `fill_cast_mana_value` now also fills `CreateToken.enters_with`. Also fixed a latent gap this surfaced: `Trigger::Magecraft` never threaded `TriggerContext::cast_mana_value` (only the general `CastSpell` form did), so `Amount::TriggeringSpellManaValue` silently resolved to 0 inside a Magecraft ability — added `Game::queue_magecraft_triggers` (mirrors `queue_controller_triggers` but injects `cast_mana_value`), wired at both the cast (`Event::SpellCast`) and copy (`Event::SpellCopied`) trigger sites. **Fully faithful (note trimmed to its unrelated residual):** deekah_fractal_theorist — the Magecraft "create a 0/0 … Fractal … put X +1/+1 counters on it" is exact; residual is only the dropped `{3}{U}: target creature token can't be blocked this turn` (needs a grant-unblockable-until-turn effect, not this slice — only a static Unblockable keyword exists, #103). **Still blocked, untouched, notes left as-is:** manaform_hellkite and rootha_mastering_the_moment (need base-P/T-**set**-from-Amount for an X/X body, not counters — a different `Effect`/static surface — plus a delayed-exile-at-next-end-step for Manaform Hellkite and a "greatest MV among instants/sorceries cast this turn" `Amount` + begin-combat-if-cast trigger for Rootha); lattice_library (needs study counters, #75, + a first-{X}-spell-each-turn cast trigger, #67/#68); oversimplify (needs a *per-player* token/counters scope — this slice is a single shared `Amount`, not per-player); fractal_harness (judgment call: left entirely as-is rather than partially scripting the counter half — its ETB also needs equipment self-attach-to-minted-token, unbuilt, and the attack-trigger "double the counters," unbuilt; scripting only the counters would leave a non-functional Equipment).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed the base-P/T-**set**-from-Amount slice (the genuine X/X body, distinct from `enters_with`'s counters). New `Effect::CreateToken.set_base_pt: Option<Amount>` (TOML `set_base_pt`, `#[serde(default)]` `None` — behavior-preserving): resolved in the `CreateToken` execute arm (pure `&self`, no game-state dependency like `enters_with` needs) and baked straight into the minted def's `CardKind::Creature { power, toughness, .. }` before any tokens are pushed — a genuine base P/T, so it still differs from `enters_with`'s counters under -1/-1 effects and counter removal. Plus `Effect::CreateToken.exile_at_next_end_step: bool` (TOML, default `false`), which schedules a per-minted-token `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled { fire_at: Step::End, .. }` mirroring `CreateTokenCopy`'s `sacrifice_at_next_end_step` — needed a new `Effect::ExileObject { object: Option<ObjectId> }` (mirrors `SacrificeObject`: guard-returns if the object already left the battlefield, tombstones a token via `TokenCeasedToExist` (CR 111.7) or routes a real permanent through the existing `exile_or_command` choke point otherwise; `label.rs`/`target()` arms added, no schema change since it's card-dsl-only and never wire-visible). Both new `CreateToken` fields are threaded through `fill_cast_mana_value` (the silent-0/0-token bug the brief called out — missed this and the token would've minted 0/0). manaform_hellkite is now fully faithful (note trimmed to the #101 mana-spent-vs-mana-value residual, matching Renegade Bull's precedent). Also landed rootha_mastering_the_moment: its prereq ("greatest mana value among instant/sorcery spells cast this turn") turned out to be a cheap, self-contained per-turn tally, so it's landed too — new `Player::greatest_instant_or_sorcery_mana_value_cast_this_turn: u32` (reset at Untap alongside the other turn tallies, bumped at `Event::SpellCast` alongside the existing `instant_or_sorcery_cast_this_turn` flag, off `def.mana_value()` — the same mana-value-not-mana-spent approximation as `TriggeringSpellManaValue`) and a new `Amount::GreatestInstantOrSorceryManaValueCastThisTurn` (TOML `"greatest_instant_or_sorcery_mana_value_cast_this_turn"`, a live read, no placeholder-fill needed since it isn't `CastSpell`-trigger-contextual). rootha_mastering_the_moment is now fully faithful (`begin_combat` timing + `cast_instant_or_sorcery_this_turn` intervening-if, both already landed, plus this slice's `set_base_pt`; note trimmed to the same #101 residual). **Still blocked:** lattice_library, oversimplify, fractal_harness — unchanged, see the residuals above.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed oversimplify's per-player Fractal-from-exiled-power slice. New `Effect::ExileAll` special case in `Game::resolve_effect` snapshots each exiled creature's controller and power (read off the pre-move object, before `apply_all` moves it) onto a new resolution-scoped `Game::power_exiled_this_way: Vec<state::PowerExiledThisWay>` — the same overwritten-per-call snapshot idiom as `destroyed_this_way`/`nonland_cards_exiled_this_way`, but keyed per player rather than a single shared total. New `Effect::EachPlayerCreatesFractalFromExiledPower { token }` walks `apnap_order()` and mints one `token` per living player, applying each mint before summing that player's own share of the snapshot and routing it through `counters_after_replacements` (CR 614 doublers apply) — no player choice, so unlike `EachPlayerExilesFromGraveyard` it never pauses; a player with no exiled creatures still mints a 0/0 that dies to the SBA sweep (CR 704.5f). oversimplify is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). **#89 stays open (not LANDED):** fractal_harness remains untouched (still needs equipment self-attach-to-minted-token, unbuilt, plus the attack-trigger "double the counters," unbuilt); lattice_library was landed separately via #75/#67/#68 (its note above predates that landing and is stale).
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed fractal_harness, the last open card — **#89 is now LANDED**. Its ETB is `create_token { enters_with = "x" }` (already-landed machinery) followed by new `Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken` (no fields — reads back the just-minted token's `Event::TokenCreated` off this same resolution, the Equipment twin of `AttachSelfToReanimated`). Its attack trigger is new `Effect::DoubleCountersOnAttachedCreature` (no fields — the no-target sibling `DoubleCounters`'s own doc comment already anticipated: "add a self target spec if a card needs the choice actually removed"; pinned to `source`'s `attached_to` instead of a chosen target, factored through a new shared `Game::doubled_counters_event` helper both `DoubleCounters` and this call). Discovered `queue_enchanted_creature_attacks_triggers` already fires off *any* attached permanent (`Game::attachments`, Aura or Equipment — only its doc comment and the TOML tag's own doc line said "Aura only"); no engine widening was needed, just a new `#[serde(alias = "equipped_creature_attacks")]` on the existing `TriggerTag::EnchantedCreatureAttacks` so an Equipment card doesn't read "enchanted" in its own TOML. Also fixed a genuine latent gap this card's ETB surfaced: `Game::ability_source_x` (which threads a permanent's own cast `{X}` into a later-resolving ability, e.g. an ETB trigger's `Amount::X`) read live `plus_counters` as a proxy — correct only when the permanent *also* happens to carry `{X}` +1/+1 counters on itself (every prior consumer, Kinetic Ooze/The Goose Mother, does). Fractal Harness's counters land on a *different* object (the minted token), so the proxy always read 0. Fixed at the root: new `Permanent::entered_with_x: u32`, locked in once from the resolving `Spell.x` at `Event::PermanentEntered` apply time (mirrors the existing `Spell.sacrifice_count`/`.kicked` internal-bookkeeping idiom — never wire-visible, never manifests as a counter), and `ability_source_x` now reads that instead of `plus_counters`. Behavior-preserving for every existing consumer (their counters are set to the same cast X at the same moment) and incidentally closes a `ponytail:` gap that comment used to name (a counter-doubling static in play could previously inflate the proxy above the real cast X). fractal_harness is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).

### 90. `mass-keyword-grant-filters` — 4 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Filter axes on the landed mass until-EOT keyword grant: subtype-filtered ("Spirits you control gain double strike and vigilance" — Quintorius Chaser), attacking/other-filtered ("other attacking creatures get +1/+1" — Martial Impetus's per-attack payoff), a "modified" predicate axis (has counters / your Equipment / your Aura — Silkguard's hexproof grant), and the per-creature has-counters anthem gate ("each creature you control with a counter on it has flying/trample" — Nev). The single-target until-EOT keyword records and the anthem filter machinery both exist — this is filter plumbing at the mass-grant site.
*Cards:* martial_impetus, nev_the_practical_dean, quintorius_history_chaser, silkguard
**Landed:** a `filter: PermanentFilter` (`#[serde(default)]`, matches every creature when absent — behavior-preserving for existing unfiltered consumers) on `Effect::PumpCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn`, AND-ed alongside the existing creature/controller guard at the mass-grant site. Fully faithful (−4 now scripted, note trimmed): quintorius_history_chaser (its "Spirits you control gain double strike and vigilance" −4).
**Still blocked:** silkguard (needs a "modified" predicate axis — equipped/enchanted-by-you/has-counters — not yet in `PermanentFilter`; note untouched); martial_impetus and nev_the_practical_dean not attempted this increment (attacking/other-filtered grant and per-creature has-counters anthem gate respectively).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed the has-counters keyword anthem slice. New `Effect::AnthemStatic.has_counters: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`, behavior-preserving) gated in `Game::matching_anthems` alongside `attacking_only`/`commander_only`/`subtypes`, backed by a new `Game::has_any_counter(id)` (core.rs, near `plus_counters`) reading +1/+1, every named `CounterKind`, and the finality counter — CR 122.1's unqualified "counter" (do not reuse `Game::source_has_counters`, which only checks +1/+1 `at_least` and is the wrong predicate here). nev_the_practical_dean's first ability ("Creatures you control with counters on them have trample") is now faithful — a single `anthem_static { keywords = ["trample"], has_counters = true }` — the anthem is recomputed live off the board, so losing the last counter drops trample the same recompute (regression-tested). Note trimmed to the residual second ability only: the "first {X}-spell each turn: put X +1/+1 counters on Nev" trigger, still blocked on a cast-a-spell-with-{X} trigger (#67/#68). **Still blocked:** silkguard (needs the full "modified" predicate — equipped / your-Aura / has-counters — plus #68 for its X-count clause); martial_impetus (needs an attacking-filtered *per-attack* anthem trigger, a distinct shape from this per-creature static gate — not attempted this slice).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed the attacking/other-filtered per-attack anthem slice. New `Effect::PumpOtherAttackersAttackingYourOpponents { power: i32, toughness: i32 }`, resolved off the already-landed `Trigger::EnchantedCreatureAttacks` (`queue_enchanted_creature_attacks_triggers`, controller = the Aura's own controller): scans the committed `combat.attackers` set, excludes the enchanted host (via `attached_to(source)`) and any attacker whose `defender_of` is the ability's controller (i.e. attacking the Aura's controller directly rather than one of their opponents), and emits one `Event::TempBoost` per qualifying attacker — no new `Event`/schema surface. martial_impetus is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted): both the +1/+1-and-goad static and the per-attack anthem trigger are scripted. **Still blocked:** silkguard (needs the "modified" predicate — equipped / your-Aura / has-counters — plus #68 for its X-count clause; not attempted this slice). #90 stays **PARTIALLY LANDED**.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed the `modified` predicate axis. New `PermanentFilter.modified: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`, behavior-preserving), guarded in `Game::permanent_matches` after the `color` axis, backed by a new `Game::is_modified(id)` (query.rs, next to `is_enchanted`) — CR 701.29: has any counter (`has_any_counter`) OR is enchanted by an Aura OR is equipped (an attachment whose `subtypes` contains `"Equipment"`). Wired into silkguard's rider as a second `[[abilities.effects]]` step on the existing `pump_creatures_you_control_until_end_of_turn` effect: `filter = { modified = true, controller = "you" }`, `keywords = ["hexproof"]`. Trimmed path taken (per this slice's brief): the modified-*creature* half is fully faithful and tested (has-counter, equipped, and Aura-enchanted creatures each gain hexproof; a bare creature doesn't); the "Auras, Equipment you control also gain hexproof" half is dropped — no pool effect targets your own noncreature Auras/Equipment, so it's unobservable — silkguard's note trimmed to name exactly that residual. **Still blocked:** pearl_ear_imperial_advisor's "whenever you cast an Aura spell that targets a modified permanent you control, draw a card" needs a cast-trigger that inspects the cast spell's chosen target, a spell-target-inspection surface not built this slice; the `modified` predicate landed here is the primitive it will consume. #90 stays **PARTIALLY LANDED** (silkguard's noncreature-permanent half and pearl_ear remain).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed pearl_ear_imperial_advisor's cast-trigger draw. New `SpellFilter::AuraTargetsModifiedPermanentYouControl` (TOML `"aura_targets_modified_permanent_you_control"`) — true when the cast spell is an Aura, its chosen target is `Game::is_modified`, and the target's controller is the caster; mirrors the existing single-purpose `SpellsThatTargetACreature` arm rather than a general And-combinator. `Game::spell_matches_filter` gained a `caster: PlayerId` parameter (every other arm ignores it) threaded through its four call sites (`cost_reduction`, `TargetSpec::SpellOnStack` resolution, `queue_cast_spell_triggers`, `queue_prowess_triggers`). pearl_ear_imperial_advisor is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). #90 is now **LANDED** — silkguard's remaining noncreature-Auras/Equipment half stays dropped as an unobservable residual (no pool effect targets your own noncreature permanents), not a live gap.
**Progress (2026-07-16):** Closed silkguard's last residual. New `Effect::GrantKeywordsToPermanentsYouControlUntilEndOfTurn { keywords, filter }` — the keyword-only, no-creature-gate twin of `PumpCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn` (same "you control" scan via `permanent_matches`, but no `is_creature_on_battlefield` filter, so it reaches noncreature permanents). silkguard's rider is now three effects: put-counters, the modified-creature hexproof pump (unchanged), and this new effect over `filter = { subtypes = ["Aura", "Equipment"], controller = "you" }`. silkguard is now fully faithful (`approximates` and both `# ponytail:` lines deleted). ponytail: the grant to your own noncreature Auras/Equipment is still unobservable-in-play — no pool effect targets your own Auras/Equipment with anything hexproof would matter against — but it's a real, verified `TempBoost.keywords` state change (tested via the effective-keywords query, and via the `TempBoost`/cleanup path reaching a noncreature permanent), so the shortcut ceiling is "no pool consumer notices yet," not "unmodeled." #90 stays **LANDED**, now with no residual notes anywhere in the pool.

### 91. `batch-attacker-trigger` — 4 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
The still-open v1 #25 watch scope: batch attack triggers with per-defender attacker counts — "whenever you attack with two or more creatures" (Firemane Commando), "whenever an opponent attacks you with two or more creatures" (Mangara, Tomik), and the per-declared-attacker watch "whenever a creature attacks one of your opponents" with attacker/defender in `TriggerContext` (Martial Impetus's anthem trigger). Declare-attackers already knows the full attacker→defender set; this is a scan over it at the declare event.
*Cards:* firemane_commando, mangara_the_diplomat, martial_impetus, tomik_wielder_of_law
**Landed:** new `Trigger::YouAttackWithCreatures { at_least }` and `Trigger::OpponentAttacksYouWithCreatures { at_least }` (TOML timings `you_attack_with_creatures`/`opponent_attacks_you_with_creatures` with a sibling `at_least` count), fired once per combat by `Game::queue_batch_attack_triggers` — a single scan of the committed attacker set from `declare_attackers`, gated per (attacking player, defender) so counts don't combine across opponents. Plus `Effect::AttackerLosesLifeYouDraw { life_loss }` (the attacking opponent from `TriggerContext` loses life, the ability's controller draws). **Faithful (notes deleted):** mangara_the_diplomat, tomik_wielder_of_law. **Trimmed:** firemane_commando — its first "whenever you attack with two or more creatures, draw" is faithful; residual note is only the second ability (another player's batch attack with a "none attacked you" gate where the *attacker* draws). **Still blocked:** martial_impetus (its per-attack anthem for *other* attacking creatures is a distinct anthem-arming shape, #90, not a batch count). ponytail: the "and/or planeswalkers you control" half of Mangara/Tomik is moot until planeswalkers-as-attack-targets land (`Event::AttackerDeclared.defender` is always a `PlayerId`).
**2026-07-14:** firemane_commando's residual second ability landed — new `Trigger::AnotherPlayerAttacksWithCreatures { at_least }` (TOML `another_player_attacks_with_creatures`) adds the "another player" scope plus a "none attacked you" gate (`against_controller == 0`) onto the existing `queue_batch_attack_triggers` scan, paired with new `Effect::AttackingPlayerDraws { drawer, count }` (the attacking player from `TriggerContext`, not the ability's controller, draws). **Faithful (note deleted):** firemane_commando.

### 92. `additional-cost-sacrifice` — 4 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
The v1 #11 still-open flavor: `[cost.additional] sacrifice = {count|"x"|"one_or_more", filter}` on spells and modes, collected at cast like the landed discard-N slice and recorded in the cast context — so Plumb the Forbidden can copy itself per sacrifice (#83) and Immoral Bargain's X-sacrifice can drive its X (#68). Springbloom's "sacrifice a land" and Witherbloom Charm mode 0 are the fixed-count starters.
*Cards:* immoral_bargain, plumb_the_forbidden, springbloom_druid, witherbloom_charm
**Landed:** new `AdditionalCost.sacrifice: Option<PermanentFilter>` (TOML `[cost.additional] sacrifice = { count = "one_or_more", filter }`, an entirely-optional "sacrifice any number matching filter"), paid pre-stack in `Game::cast` through the normal death events, with the paid count recorded on the resolved `Spell` (`Game::spell_sacrifice_count`) for a future copy-per-sacrifice rider. Plus `Effect::MaySacrifice { filter, then }` — a resolution-time optional single sacrifice (pauses on `PendingChoice::MaySacrifice`, answered by the existing `ChooseSacrifices` wire shape; declining runs nothing) reused by both a spell mode and a triggered ability's rider. **Faithful (notes deleted):** springbloom_druid (ETB "you may sacrifice a land. If you do, search…"), witherbloom_charm (mode 0 "you may sacrifice a permanent. If you do, draw two"). **Trimmed:** plumb_the_forbidden — the sacrifice cost, its recorded count, and the base draw/lose-1-life are faithful; residual note is only the "copy this spell for each creature sacrificed" rider (needs #83's storm-copy-count). **Still blocked:** immoral_bargain (its X-sacrifice must *drive* the spell's X, #68, not just record a count). *(Closed 2026-07-12 by #73's `TargetCount.sacrifice_scaled` — see that section.)*

### 93. `counter-choice-verbs` — 4 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
The v1 #14 deliberately-deferred choice-surface half: `proliferate` (a select-set `PendingChoice` over counter-bearing players/permanents, one more of each kind present — Expansion Algorithm), `move_counters` (remove N/all from one permanent, put on another, with a count choice — Forgotten Ancient, Nexus Mentality), remove-all-counters-then-draw-per-removed (Nexus Mentality, needs the count-and-transfer read), and the mass "remove all counters from all permanents and players" verb (Final Act mode 4). All ride the existing `CountersPlaced` pipeline.
*Cards:* expansion_algorithm, final_act, forgotten_ancient, nexus_mentality
**Landed:** `Effect::Proliferate { times }` pauses once per iteration on a new `PendingChoice::Proliferate` over every battlefield permanent (any controller) that currently has a counter — answered by the existing `ChooseSacrifices` "any subset" wire shape, re-pausing `times - 1` more times (mirroring `SearchLibrary`'s chaining); each chosen permanent gets one more +1/+1 (through the replacement pipeline) and one more of every named kind present (raw). `Effect::MoveCounters { target, to_filter, all_kinds }` moves counters from its own cast/placement-resolved `target` onto a second permanent chosen at *resolution* — mirroring `Fight`'s cast/resolution target split (`to_filter` excludes the source); `all_kinds` (default `false`, +1/+1 only) also moves every named kind. `Effect::RemoveAllCountersThenDraw { target }` removes every counter from `target` and draws one card per counter removed. **Faithful (notes deleted):** expansion_algorithm ("Proliferate X times" is the whole card). **Fully faithful (2026-07-15, `approximates` deleted):** forgotten_ancient — the upkeep "move any number of +1/+1 counters onto other creatures" now distributes a player-chosen number (0..=available) across any number of other target creatures (`move_counters` gained `distributed = true`, pausing on `PendingChoice::DivideMovedCounters` — see the #73 rider note), and its "whenever a player casts a spell" counter clause is scripted (`cast_spell`/`any_player`, #72). nexus_mentality — **fully faithful (2026-07-15, `approximates` deleted):** the "you may choose both if you control a commander" rider is now `choose = 1, choose_max = 2, choose_max_if_commander = true` (new `CardDef::modal_choose_max_if_commander` bool + `Game::modal_choose_max`/`controls_a_commander`, gating the `choose_max` range on a battlefield-commander check at cast, enforced at both the `validate_modes` cast choke and the wire mode-picker prompt). final_act — `choose_max` (an *unconditional* "choose one or more" range, CR 700.2d) was already landed via #105/Casualties of War, and turned out to be the real unlock here rather than #110 (which is specifically per-mode *targets*, not the choose-count mechanism — none of Final Act's modes target anything, so #110 never applied): the card is now `modal, choose = 1, choose_max = 2` over its two expressible modes (destroy all creatures / destroy all planeswalkers), residual note trimmed to the three still-unmodeled modes (destroy all battles — no battle permanent type; exile all graveyards — no mass all-graveyards exile effect; each opponent loses all counters — that's a *player*-level counter wipe, poison/energy/experience/etc., which this pool doesn't track, not a permanent-counter effect).
