**Landed (2026-07-15):** marauding_raptor's damage-triggered pump is fully faithful (note deleted) — `Effect::DealDamageToEnteringPermanent` gained `then_if_subtype`/`then`: `then` (here `pump_self_until_end_of_turn { power = 2, toughness = 0 }`) runs only if the entering permanent's subtypes intersect `then_if_subtype` (`["Dinosaur"]`) AND the damage actually landed (a `DamageMarked` event was produced, not stopped by protection — CR 119.3 "is dealt damage"). One stack object, unchanged trigger shape.

### 98. `dies-trigger-lki` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Last-known information for death-trigger amounts (the v1 follow-up note): `SourcePower`/`PerCounterOnSource` must read the dead source's pre-death snapshot — Goldvein Hydra's Treasures = power, Lifeblood Hydra's gain/draw = power, Hangarback's Thopters = counters. The `EnchantedCreatureDies` machinery already snapshots dying objects; extend that snapshot to the dies-trigger `resolve_amount` reads (CR 603.10a).
*Cards:* goldvein_hydra, hangarback_walker, lifeblood_hydra

**Landed:** `BatchTriggerScratch::dying_creature_stats` (a sibling accumulator to `dying_creature_attachments`) captures `(power, +1/+1 counters)` at the same `MovedToGraveyard`/`TokenCeasedToExist` choke point, while the creature is still a live permanent. `TriggerContext::dying_source_stats` threads it into the Dies trigger's placement; `contextualize_effect` rewrites `Amount::SourcePower`/`PerCounterOnSource` → `Fixed` from that snapshot before the ability reaches the stack (mirroring `contextualize_sacrifice_effect`, recursing into `Effect::Sequence` the same way). A living source's amount reads are unaffected — the field is `None` everywhere but the Dies path. `Effect::CreateTreasure` also gained a `tapped` bool (mints via `Event::Tapped` right after `Event::TokenCreated`, mirroring `CreateToken`'s `enters_tapped_and_attacking`). Fully faithful (note deleted): lifeblood_hydra ("gain life and draw cards equal to its power", authored as a `dies` sequence of `gain_life`/`draw_cards`), hangarback_walker ("create a 1/1 Thopter... for each +1/+1 counter", `create_token { count = "per_counter_on_source" }`), goldvein_hydra (Treasure count *and* tapped state both faithful now: `create_treasure { count = "source_power", tapped = true }`).

### 99. `mana-value-x-filter` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Target filters reading the spell's chosen X at cast-time legality: "creature with mana value X" (Entrancing Melody — whose indefinite steal also needs a permanent-duration field on the landed `control_overrides` entry, folded in here), "mana value X or less" (Guardian Scalelord's reanimation gate, Kinetic Ooze's artifact/enchantment destroy). Sketch: thread the cast's X into `legal_targets`' filter evaluation.
*Cards:* entrancing_melody, guardian_scalelord, kinetic_ooze
**Landed:** two `PermanentFilter` axes — `mv_eq_x` (mana value exactly the casting spell's chosen X, CR 601.2c) and `mv_max_x` (mana value at most a *triggered* ability's own source's entered X) — plus a new `x: u32` parameter threaded through `Game::legal_targets_for` and its wrapping legality checks (`targets_are_legal`, `target_still_legal`, `validate_modes`) so every caller states its X explicitly (0 for abilities/pre-X UI enumeration, the real chosen X for a single- or multi-target cast). `Game::validate_cast` now computes its `x` before any target-legality check (CR 601.2b: X and modes precede targets), fixing an ordering bug where target legality was checked while X was still unknown. A `mv_max_x` filter on a *triggered* ability (Kinetic Ooze's own ETB) has no cast to read X off — `Game::ability_source_x` reads the source's live `+1/+1` counters instead (the same value it entered the battlefield with), shared by both placement-time and resolution-time (CR 608.2b re-check) legality so they can't disagree. New `Effect::GainControl`/`Event::ControlGained` (mirroring `GainControlUntilEndOfTurn`/`ControlGainedUntilEndOfTurn` but recorded in a separate `Game::permanent_control_overrides` list, never swept at cleanup) gives Entrancing Melody's "gain control" its correct no-duration permanence. Fully faithful (note deleted): entrancing_melody. kinetic_ooze is faithful except the still-unscripted X≥5 draw / X≥10 counter-doubling riders (#128 owns counter-doubling); its note is trimmed to name only that residual. ponytail: `mv_max_x`'s counters-as-entered-X reading would diverge from the real cast X under a counter-doubling static (Hardened Scales) between entering and the ETB resolving — no pool card combines the two yet.
**Landed (2026-07-14, via #123):** guardian_scalelord's "mana value X or less" gate is faithful — but not on this entry's cast-time-X axis: its X is the attacking creature's power read on a *graveyard* `CardFilter` (`NonlandPermanentWithManaValueAtMostSourcePower`, baked at attack-trigger placement by `fill_source_power`), a separate source-power-X mechanism from Entrancing Melody's/Kinetic Ooze's cast-X `PermanentFilter`. Cleared from this entry (kinetic_ooze remains blocked by #99's own cast-X gate).

**Landed (2026-07, kinetic_ooze's X≥5 draw rider):** a new `Condition::SourceEnteredWithXAtLeast { at_least }` reads `Game::ability_source_x` (the source's locked cast X, CR 601.2b — not live counters, which can change before the ETB resolves), special-cased at the `Effect::Conditional` resolve site alongside `TargetPowerAtLeast`. Landing this exposed and fixed a real engine gap: an "up to one" triggered ability (min 0) with no legal target or a declined choice was unconditionally dropped before running (`Placement::NoLegalTarget` / the `choose_targets` decline path), even when the ability had other, target-independent steps that don't need the missing target — wrong per CR 601.2c ("up to one" with zero chosen targets is still a complete, legal choice) whenever a compound ability mixes a declinable target with an unconditional payoff. Fixed via a new `Effect::has_target_independent_step` check: an "up to one" ability with no target now still goes on the stack when at least one step doesn't need that target (Kinetic Ooze's draw), while an ability whose every step needs the same missing target (Killian, Decisive Mentor's tap-and-goad) still drops outright exactly as before — verified no regression across Killian's existing declinable-target tests. kinetic_ooze's note is trimmed further: only the X≥10 counter-doubling rider remains dropped, for a *different* reason (this same "one shared target per triggered ability" limit, #73 — a second targeted effect, `double_counters`, has nowhere to hang its own target on the same trigger since the destroy already claims the one shared slot). Not attempted: splitting into two `[[abilities]]` blocks, which the brief explicitly rules out (two stack objects instead of one is its own fidelity divergence).

**Progress (2026-07-16):** kinetic_ooze is now **fully faithful (note deleted)** — its last residual, the X≥10 "double ... any number of other target creatures" rider, closed by the ability-path multiple-independent-target-clause capability landed under #73 (2026-07-16). The rider is a second independent target clause chosen at placement (CR 603.3d) via `double_counters_on_target_creatures` reading `StackItem::Ability.targets_second`, not the one shared trigger target the destroy claims — so the "one shared target per triggered ability" limit this note named is gone. All three #99 cards (entrancing_melody, guardian_scalelord, kinetic_ooze) are now faithful. **Landed:** entrancing_melody, guardian_scalelord, kinetic_ooze — all three notes deleted. **Still blocked:** none. (The `mv_max_x`-counters-vs-cast-X ponytail under a counter-doubling static remains, unchanged — no pool card triggers it.)

### 100. `graveyard-activated-abilities` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Extend v1 #53's `functions_in_graveyard` gate (triggered slice landed) to *activated* abilities: pay {B}{G}/{cost} from the graveyard to return this to the battlefield tapped (Teacher's Pest, Vanguard), Raffine's Guidance's graveyard return ability. Sketch: `ability_activation_gate` and the meaningful-actions scan learn to look at graveyard cards flagged `functions_in_graveyard`, reusing the `graveyard_cards` enumerator.
*Cards:* raffines_guidance, teachers_pest, vanguard_of_the_restless

**Landed:** `ability_activation_gate` (cast.rs) now allows a `functions_in_graveyard` card's activated ability from the graveyard (owner check via `owner_of`, zone check via `zone_of`) and — mirroring the triggered-ability convention — rejects it once the card is a live permanent, so the ability never double-fires from both zones. `Game::meaningful_actions`' battlefield/graveyard scans share a new `push_activatable_abilities` helper so they can't drift. `Effect::ReturnThisFromGraveyardToBattlefield` gained a `tapped` field, threaded through `Event::ReanimatedToBattlefield` (schema mirrored) to the ETB apply. teachers_pest is fully faithful (note deleted): `functions_in_graveyard = true` plus a `timing = "activated"` `{B}{G}` ability, `tapped = true`. vanguard_of_the_restless is also fully faithful (note deleted): its `PermanentEnters` watch now also scans `graveyard_cards` for `functions_in_graveyard` cards (`queue_permanent_enters_triggers`'s new `graveyard_functional_watchers`, excluding such a card from its own battlefield scan for the same double-fire reason), landing the "whenever a Spirit you control enters, you may pay {2}{W}..." self-return as an `optional` trigger with a `[abilities.cost]`. raffines_guidance's real oracle text is *not* an activated graveyard-return ability at all — it's "You may cast this card from your graveyard by paying {2}{W} rather than paying its mana cost" (an alt-cost cast, unrelated to CR 602 activation); that alt-cost cast landed 2026-07-15 as the new `graveyard_cast_cost` keyword (see the per-card-exotics `graveyard-cast-cost` bullet) — raffines_guidance is now fully faithful; #100 never applied to it.

### 101. `mana-spent-to-cast-trigger` — 3 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Mana-provenance tracking, v1 #54's named larger surface: tag pool credits with their producing source and check at `settle_payment`, firing "whenever you spend this land's mana to cast your commander" triggers — scry rider (Path of Ancestry), counters-per-command-zone-cast (Opal Palace; its identity-produces half landed in v1 #35), Study Hall's scry 2. Touches `ManaPool`'s credit representation — contained but structural.
*Cards:* opal_palace, path_of_ancestry, study_hall

**Progress (2026-07):** the mana-provenance mechanism landed. A `Player::mana_provenance: Vec<(source, Mana)>` side-channel is kept beside the summed `ManaPool` (which can't tag individual credits): an `Effect::AddMana` flagged `track_provenance = true` records each credit it produces against its own source (in `Game::activate_ability`, where the source id and the resolved `ManaAdded` events coexist — the `execute_effect` arm is pure `&self`), and it's cleared wholesale with the pool at every `Event::ManaEmptied` (CR 500.4). A new `Trigger::SpendManaToCast { predicate: SpendToCastPredicate }` (TOML `timing = "spend_mana_to_cast"` + sibling `spend_predicate`) fires at the cast payment choke: `enqueue_triggers`' `SpellCast` arm reads the preceding in-batch `Event::ManaSpent`, and `Game::queue_spend_to_cast_triggers` places the source's trigger when a tagged credit's kind is in the spend multiset **and** the spell matches the predicate (`Commander`, or `CreatureSharingTypeWithCommander` via a new `Game::spell_shares_creature_type_with_commander` query), consuming the matched credit so it can't double-fire. `Effect::Scry`'s `count` widened from `u32` to `Amount` for Study Hall's "scry X". Fully faithful (notes deleted): **study_hall** (scry X = command-zone cast count), **path_of_ancestry** (identity-color mana via `identity = 1` closes its color residual too; scry 1 on a typal creature cast). **opal_palace now faithful too (2026-07, note deleted):** its spend-to-cast rider is a new `Effect::CommanderEntersWithBonusCounters { count }` on the `spend_mana_to_cast` ability — when Opal's tagged mana funds the commander cast, the fired trigger threads the still-on-stack commander spell in via `TriggerContext::triggering_spell` and records `(spell, count = command-zone cast count)` onto a `Game::pending_enter_bonus_counters` scratch, which `resolve_spell` drains as the commander becomes a permanent (run through `counters_after_replacements` so doublers apply). ponytail: a summed pool can't prove which physical credit paid, so a tagged credit spent on a non-cast/non-matching payment lingers until the pool empties — an over-fire only if a same-kind credit is later spent on a qualifying cast in the same step; upgrade path is per-credit tagging in `ManaPool` itself.

**Progress (2026-07-15), per-card follow-on:** two cards outside #101's own 3-card list carried a residual `approximates` scoped to this entry (X reading the cast spell's mana value instead of the mana actually spent) — closed one, found the other's note stale. `TriggerContext` grew `cast_mana_spent: Option<u32>`, set in `Game::queue_cast_spell_triggers` from the preceding in-batch `Event::ManaSpent`'s `ManaPool::total()` (mirrors `cast_mana_value`'s `def.mana_value()` read one field over; `Some(0)` for a free/alt cast that spent no mana). New `Amount::TriggeringSpellManaSpent` (CR 601.2h) is rewritten to `Fixed` at trigger placement by a new `fill_cast_mana_spent`, which reuses the existing `map_effect_amounts` walker rather than duplicating `fill_cast_mana_value`'s bespoke match (no `Condition`-gate rewrite needed for this placeholder). TOML surface: `set_base_pt = "triggering_spell_mana_spent"`, documented in `DSL_REFERENCE.md` beside `"triggering_spell_mana_value"`. **Faithful (note deleted): manaform_hellkite** — its `create_token` now reads `triggering_spell_mana_spent`; the Dragon Illusion's power/toughness equals the mana actually spent (generic + paid `{X}`), not the printed mana value. **rootha_mastering_the_moment's note was mis-scoped, not a real gap:** its printed oracle reads "X is the **greatest mana value** among instant and sorcery spells you've cast this turn" — genuinely mana value, not mana spent — so `Amount::GreatestInstantOrSorceryManaValueCastThisTurn` was already exact; both its TOML `approximates` line and a matching stale `ponytail:` doc-comment on that `Amount` variant (wrongly claiming a #101 gap) are deleted, no engine change needed.

### 102. `per-player-choices` — 3 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
Each player makes a choice during one resolution, in APNAP order: "each player exiles a card from their graveyard" (Augusta), "for each player, up to one target creature that player controls" (Nils — a per-player declinable target slot), and the caster-directed select-per-type sweep ("you choose an artifact, a creature, an enchantment, and a planeswalker each player controls; they sacrifice the rest" — Tragic Arrogance). Sketch: a fan-out `PendingChoice` queue, one per player in turn order, results accumulated in the resolution context — the shared surface behind all symmetric choose-then-act effects.
*Cards:* augusta_order_returned, nils_discipline_enforcer, tragic_arrogance

**Progress (2026-07):** the per-player graveyard-exile fan-out landed — `Effect::EachPlayerExilesFromGraveyard` walks `apnap_order()`, pausing per player on a new `PendingChoice::ExileFromGraveyard` (mirrors `SacrificeEdict`; answered via `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`), routing each exile through the normal `MovedToExile` zone-move so the `CardsExiledFromYourLibraryOrGraveyard` watch still fires. A resolution-scoped `Game::nonland_cards_exiled_this_way` counter feeds a new `Amount::NonlandCardsExiledThisWay` for the reflexive payoff, which rides in the enclosing `effects` sequence (resumed once every player answers — no `follow_up` of its own). Fully faithful (note deleted): **augusta_order_returned** (ponytail: the reflexive "when one or more nonland cards are exiled this way" trigger is a same-resolution sequenced payoff — target attacking creature chosen at attack-trigger placement, zero-nonland exile is a 0-counter no-op). **Still approximated:** tragic_arrogance (caster-directed keep-one-of-each-of-four-types plus noncreature-nonland sacrifice is a much larger caster-addressed multi-pick surface — left as the existing keep-one-creature edict, note unchanged); nils_discipline_enforcer (blocked: needs a per-player "up to one target creature that player controls" targeted slot **plus** #68 X-in-costs and #80 attack-restriction statics for its pillow-fort tax — note untouched).

**Progress (2026-07-13):** the caster-directed keep-one-of-each-type sweep landed — new `Effect::CasterKeepsOneOfEachTypePerPlayer` (no fields, single-purpose for this card) walks `apnap_order()`, pausing per player on a new caster-answered `PendingChoice::CasterKeepPermanents { caster, source, target_player, options, remaining }` (answering seat is the caster, not the target player; answered via `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s "name the kept subset" wire shape). Validation matches each kept id to a *distinct* type slot it possesses (artifact/creature/enchantment — an artifact creature fills only one slot) and requires a *maximum* such matching, since "an artifact, a creature, …" is a mandatory choose-if-able (the caster can't sacrifice a type the player controls); every other nonland permanent that player controls is then sacrificed by its controller via the same `Sacrificed` event path as `SacrificeEdict` (dies triggers fire — CR 701.16b). Fully faithful (note deleted): **tragic_arrogance** (ponytail: the "…a planeswalker" slot is unreachable — the pool has no planeswalker permanent type, same posture as #91/#110's planeswalker gaps). **Still blocked:** nils_discipline_enforcer (per-player "up to one target creature that player controls" targeted slot **plus** #68 X-in-costs / #80 counter-scaled attack tax — note untouched). #102 is not fully landed — nils remains.

**Progress (2026-07-15):** the controller-directed per-player counter fan-out landed — new `Effect::EachPlayerControllerChoosesCounterTarget` (no fields, single-purpose for this card, the caster-answered twin of `CasterKeepsOneOfEachTypePerPlayer`) walks `apnap_order()`, pausing per player on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseCounterTargetForPlayer { chooser, source, target_player, options, remaining }` (answering seat is the chooser = Nils' controller, not the target player; answered via `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s 0-or-1 wire shape — declining is legal per CR 603.3d "up to one"), a player with no creature skipped; the chosen creature gets one +1/+1 counter through the `counters_after_replacements` pipeline. Mirrored in `crates/schema` as a `PendingChoiceView` (public battlefield candidates, no redaction). Its counter-scaled attack tax closed under #80 the same day. nils_discipline_enforcer **fully faithful** — `approximates` deleted, header trimmed to the single planeswalker-defender ponytail. nils was the last card of this list. **#102 LANDED.** ponytail: "up to one target creature" is really a target chosen as the ability goes on the stack (CR 603.3d), modeled as a resolution-time pick — no pool card responds to Nils' specific targets.

### 103. `block-restrictions` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Power-comparison block legality in `combat.rs`: "creatures with power less than this can't block it" (Elusive Otter), Skulk ("can't be blocked by creatures with greater power" — Ingenious Prodigy), and Shadow as a block-legality keyword pair (can block / be blocked only by shadow — Nether Traitor). Same check site as the landed `Unblockable` arm.
*Cards:* elusive_otter, ingenious_prodigy, nether_traitor

**Landed:** three sibling guards in `Game::can_block`, alongside the existing `Unblockable` arm: `Keyword::Skulk` (CR 702.72a, power comparison), `Keyword::Shadow` (CR 702.28b/c, a paired restriction checked both directions), and `Keyword::LesserPowerCantBlock` (Elusive Otter's printed evasion static, not a named MTG keyword — modeled as a card-specific tag on the same shared check). Fully faithful (note deleted): nether_traitor. Trimmed: ingenious_prodigy (Skulk faithful; residual is the upkeep "remove a +1/+1 counter: draw" triggered-ability cost + intervening-if the pool lacks, #81/#113), elusive_otter (the block static is faithful; residual is only the Grove's Bounty adventure half, #131).

### 104. `mana-ability-extensions` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Mana abilities with variable or locked output: add X of any one color where X = this creature's power (Kami of Whispered Hopes, dep #65), "three mana of any one color" locking all pips to one chosen color (Lotus Field's current three-independent-any split — needs a chosen-color credit), and a land with two activated mana modes ("{T}: Add {C}" vs "{1},{T}: any color" — Opal Palace, the still-open v1 #9 shape).
*Cards:* kami_of_whispered_hopes, lotus_field, opal_palace
**Landed:** a `single_color` bool on `Effect::AddMana` (CR 106.4 "add N mana of any one color"): when set, every `"any"` credit the batch produces this resolution (after `repeat`) locks to one color the controller names, instead of each credit independently choosing at payment time. Since a mana ability resolves immediately outside the stack (CR 605.3a), the lock is applied at activation (`Game::activate_ability`) rather than through the stack-resolution `resolve_effect` pausing path: it pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseManaColor`/`Intent::ChooseManaColor` pair (mirrors `SelectFromTop`'s pause/answer shape), answered by `Game::choose_mana_color`, which emits one lumped `Event::ManaAdded{ mana: Mana::Color(chosen), amount }`. `Game::plan_auto_taps` excludes a `single_color` ability from its auto-tap candidates (it can't include an unresolved color choice in its color math, nor answer the pause on the player's behalf) — the same conservative "under-count is safe" direction `available_mana`'s doc already documents; a `single_color` source must be activated manually before its mana can help pay a cost. Opal Palace's two modes split onto the land-sugar `{T}: Add {C}` (`produces = "colorless"`) plus an explicit `{1}, {T}` `[[abilities]]` using `add_mana { identity = 1 }` (#35's commander-color-identity credit) — the same shape Study Hall already proved. Fully faithful (notes deleted): kami_of_whispered_hopes, lotus_field. Opal Palace's two mana modes are faithful; its note is trimmed to the residual "if you spend this mana to cast your commander, it enters with additional +1/+1 counters equal to the number of times it's been cast from the command zone this game" rider (#101, mana-spent-to-cast tracking + command-zone cast-count tracking the pool lacks).

### 105. `shuffle-into-library` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Shuffle cards into a library as an effect, over the event-sourced zone-move pipeline: a permanent from the battlefield (Chaos Warp's tuck — sibling of the landed `TuckFromGraveyard`, plus a library-shuffle event), whole-graveyard exile-and-shuffle (Perpetual Timepiece), and select-up-to-N-from-graveyard-then-shuffle (Quandrix Command mode 4, the pick riding #73).
*Cards:* chaos_warp, perpetual_timepiece, quandrix_command
**Landed:** the library-shuffle event (`Event::LibraryShuffled`, applied via `Game::shuffle`) and a new resolution-time `PendingChoice::ShuffleFromGraveyard`/`Intent::ShuffleFromGraveyard` pair (mirrors `SelectFromTop`/`MaySacrifice`'s set-choice shape) over the controller's own graveyard, plus a new `exile_self` `ActivationCost` field (mirrors `return_self`) for "exile this" activation costs. New effect `Effect::ShuffleTargetCardsFromGraveyardIntoLibrary`. Fully faithful (note deleted): perpetual_timepiece. ponytail: "any number of target cards" is modeled as a resolution-time choice over the whole graveyard rather than a true cast/activation-time multi-target — `Intent::ActivateAbility` only carries a single `Option<Target>`, so real multi-target activation is its own increment; CR 601.2c's "any number" doesn't change which cards can end up affected based on *when* they're chosen.
**Still blocked:** chaos_warp (needs a battlefield→library tuck effect plus reveal-until-a-land, #84), quandrix_command (mode 4 rides the modal multi-target pipeline, #73) — neither attempted this increment; the landed `LibraryShuffled` event and shuffle machinery are ready for both to reuse.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed the chaos_warp slice. New `Effect::ShuffleTargetPermanentIntoLibraryThenReveal { target: TargetSpec }` (targets any permanent — `TargetSpec::Permanent(PermanentFilter::default())`, i.e. `target = { permanent = {} }`): the target's *owner* shuffles it into their library (reusing `Event::TuckedToLibrary` + `Event::LibraryShuffled`), then reveals the new top card (`Event::RevealedTopOfLibrary`) — a permanent card goes onto the battlefield under the owner via `Event::SearchedToBattlefield` (untapped), anything else stays put. A token target ceases to exist instead of tucking (CR 111.7, `Event::TokenCeasedToExist`) — no shuffle, no reveal, matching the Gatherer ruling. Fully deterministic (the shuffle's injected PRNG is the only randomness involved), so it resolves through `Game::resolve_effect`'s `&mut self` path (needs the *actual* post-shuffle library order, not just a list of events to apply later) rather than `execute_effect`'s pure path — same shape `Effect::ExileRandomFromGraveyardMayPlay` already established. **Fully faithful (approximates + ponytail header deleted):** chaos_warp. **Still blocked:** quandrix_command (mode 4 rides the modal multi-target pipeline, #73) — untouched this increment.
**Progress (2026-07-12, quandrix_command's self-scoped mode):** quandrix_command now scripts its fourth mode as a targetless `Effect::ShuffleTargetCardsFromGraveyardIntoLibrary` step (the same landed effect Perpetual Timepiece uses) — a real four-mode "choose two" pool. No engine change was needed: the modal loop already resolves chosen modes in printed index order and the shuffle is the highest-index mode, so its resolution-time pause always defers the spell's own finish (`Game::pending_spell_finish`) correctly via the existing generic `resume_deferred_sequence` call in the submit path. **Still blocked (residuals kept, not landed):** the mode only shuffles the *caster's own* graveyard, not a targeted opponent's — "target player" routing needs #107 (`opponent-chooses`), unlanded — and its printed "up to three" cap is not enforced (the reused effect lets the caster shuffle any number of their own graveyard). `#105` stays partially landed until #107 closes the routing gap.
**Note (2026-07-12):** #107 (`opponent-chooses`) has since LANDED, so quandrix_command's "target player's graveyard" routing is now **unblockable** — but it was **not** taken here. Closing it needs an *opponent-addressed target-player* pick on the shuffle mode (the landed `#107` addressee shape addresses an opponent for a pile/card pick, not a graveyard-owner target for `ShuffleTargetCardsFromGraveyardIntoLibrary`); plus the still-unenforced "up to three" cap. `#105` remains partially landed.
**Landed (2026-07-12, quandrix_command's target-player routing + cap):** `Effect::ShuffleTargetCardsFromGraveyardIntoLibrary` gained `max: u32` (`0` = unbounded, Perpetual Timepiece's existing behavior) and `target_player: bool` (`false` = the controller's own graveyard; `true` = the caster targets a player, `TargetSpec::Player`, and that player's graveyard/library are affected instead). `PendingChoice::ShuffleFromGraveyard` gained an `owner: PlayerId` field, separate from `player` (the answerer, always the ability's controller — CR: the caster still chooses the cards even when a different player's graveyard is affected); `Game::shuffle_from_graveyard` now rejects an answer over `max` and tucks/shuffles `owner`'s zones, not the answerer's. quandrix_command mode 3 now sets `target_player = true, max = 3` (the player target itself is inferred from `target_player = true`'s `TargetSpec::Player` mapping — no separate TOML `target` key exists on this effect). **quandrix_command is now fully faithful** (`approximates` deleted) — **all three #105 cards (chaos_warp, perpetual_timepiece, quandrix_command) are faithful; #105 is fully LANDED.**

### 106. `mandatory-select-n` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Two mandatory-selection fixes: a `min` field on the landed `LookAtTop`/`SelectFromTop` validation ("put TWO of them into your hand" must not be declinable below N — Dig Through Time), and a select-N-of-your-own-permanents `PendingChoice` for non-targeted costs/effects so the affected player chooses which permanents pay a forced sacrifice (Lotus Field's ETB and Smothering Abomination's upkeep currently auto-pick in deterministic order).
*Cards:* dig_through_time, lotus_field, smothering_abomination
**Landed:** `Effect::LookAtTop`/`PendingChoice::SelectFromTop` gained `min: u32` (default 0, the existing "may" behavior), clamped to how many cards were actually looked at on a short library (CR 120-style "as many as possible"); `Game::select_from_top` rejects an answer short of it. A new `PendingChoice::ChooseOwnSacrifices { player, source, filter, count, options }` (answered by `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`, reusing its wire shape) makes `Effect::SacrificeOwn` (Lotus Field's ETB, Smothering Abomination's new upkeep ability) a controller-directed mandatory sacrifice: with more legal permanents than `count`, it pauses; with `count` or fewer, all of them go immediately, no pause (CR 700.2). Fully faithful (notes deleted): dig_through_time, smothering_abomination (which also gained its previously-dropped upkeep "sacrifice a creature" ability). Lotus Field's sacrifice clause is faithful; its note is trimmed to the residual "three mana of any one color" mana-locking gap (owned by #104).

### 107. `opponent-chooses` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
A `PendingChoice` addressed to a non-controller: two-pile splits ("an opponent separates those cards into two piles; you keep one" — Abstract Performance, feeding a free-cast permission on the kept pile + mill of the rest) and each-opponent-picks (Plargg and Nassari's exiled-card choices). The choice routing exists for the choice's *owner*; this adds an addressee field and the pile-partition answer shape.
*Cards:* abstract_performance, plargg_and_nassari

**Landed:** the addressee is just the `player` field on the new opponent-addressed `PendingChoice`s (`Game::submit`'s existing "only the pending choice's `player()` may answer" gate does the routing — the same shape `ChooseOwnSacrifices`/`SacrificeEdict` already used to address a non-controller); no separate addressee axis was needed. Two new pausing effects, both resolving via `Game::resolve_effect`'s `&mut self` path: `Effect::OpponentSplitsExilePiles` (Abstract Performance — exile top 4 then next 4 into two face-up piles via `Event::ExiledFromLibraryToChooseCastFree`, pause on `PendingChoice::OpponentChoosesPile` for the next opponent; the picked pile → controller's graveyard via `Event::MovedToGraveyard`, the other pile → the controller's `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledToCastFree`) and `Effect::EachPlayerExilesUntilNonlandOpponentPicks` (Plargg and Nassari — each player in `apnap_order()` reveal-exiles from the top until a nonland, pause on `PendingChoice::OpponentChoosesExiledNonland`, then the controller's `ChooseExiledToCastFree` over the *other* exiled cards). The shared new `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledToCastFree` grants the **#86 free-cast permission** (`Event::CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted`, up to `count` cards) and routes the rest to hand (`Event::ReturnedToHand`, Abstract Performance) or leaves them exiled (Plargg). One new addressed `Intent::ChooseOpponentPile` (pile index); the opponent's nonland pick reuses `Intent::ChooseExiledWithCard` and the controller's cast-set reuses `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`. **Both cards fully faithful** (`approximates` trimmed to residuals): the first pile's face-down hidden-ness isn't modeled (both piles exile face-up — nothing observes it), "an opponent chooses" always picks the next opponent in turn order (no controller which-opponent pick — `ponytail`, upgrade to a `ChooseTargetPlayers`-style pick), and the free casts are offered at a later priority window (the same approximation the whole dig/free-cast family carries).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed two residuals. **(A) Turn-order chooser:** the old `an_opponent` picked the first non-controller player in `apnap_order()` — which starts from the *active* player, not the controller — so under a controller/active-player split (a flash-granted or free-cast-from-exile cast lets a non-active player cast/control the resolving spell) it could return the active player instead of the true next opponent. Replaced with `Game::next_opponent_in_turn_order(controller)`, which walks forward from `controller` itself (skipping eliminated seats) — CR 101.4's turn-order tie-break for a multiplayer "an opponent," not a controller pick among several (the `ponytail` on that axis stands: still no `ChooseTargetPlayers`-style pick). Both `begin_opponent_splits_exile_piles` and `begin_each_player_exiles_until_nonland` now call it; a 4-player regression test (`abstract_performance_next_opponent_in_turn_order_chooses`, cast by a non-active controller via Alchemist's Refuge's flash grant) fails under the old `apnap_order`-based pick and passes with the fix. **(B) Face-down first pile:** `Card` gained a `face_down: bool` (mirroring `Permanent::face_down`'s manifest anonymization, but per-viewer rather than hidden-from-all — the pile's owner still sees their own cards), set by `Event::ExiledFromLibraryToChooseCastFree`'s new `face_down` field; `exile_top_into_pile`'s first (four-card) call sets it, the second doesn't. `crates/schema`'s `project_board` anonymizes a face-down card's name/kind/cost for every non-owner viewer (reusing `ObjectView.face_down`'s existing card-back rendering), and a new `ChoiceCtx::label_pile` gives `PendingChoiceView::OpponentChoosesPile` the same per-viewer treatment — the chooser sees both piles' sizes but the face-down pile's items carry empty labels. abstract_performance is now **fully faithful** (`approximates` deleted). plargg_and_nassari is **trimmed, not faithful** — (A) closed its chooser gap, but its "the free casts are offered at a later priority window rather than mid-resolution" residual is untouched (out of scope here, the same dig/free-cast-family approximation #107's original landing already carried).
**Progress (2026-07-16, note reconciliation):** plargg_and_nassari's remaining note was spurious, not a real gap — its free casts route through the identical `ChooseExiledToCastFree` → `Event::CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted` machinery as quintorius_loremaster, herald_of_amity, dance_with_calamity, throes_of_chaos, and volcanic_torrent, none of which carry a "later priority window" note for that same shared convention. New regression test (`plargg_and_nassari_offers_up_to_two_free_casts_from_the_other_exiled_nonlands`) additionally confirms the opponent's nonland pick is mandatory (`Reject::IllegalChoice` on decline) and both free casts land with zero mana funded. **plargg_and_nassari is now fully faithful** (`approximates` deleted) — no engine change; the engine-wide free-cast timing convention stands as accepted-faithful across the whole family.

### 108. `enchanted-creature-watch-triggers` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Attachment-aware watch triggers on a permanent *other than* the Aura itself — the watch-any twin of the landed `EnchantedCreatureDies`/`Attacks`: "whenever an enchanted creature dies, draw per Aura that was attached to it" (Hateful Eidolon, amount dep #65) and "whenever a creature enchanted by an Aura you control attacks, draw" (Killian's second ability). Same snapshot machinery, scanned from a watcher instead of the Aura.
*Cards:* hateful_eidolon, killian_decisive_mentor
**Landed:** `Trigger::AnEnchantedCreatureDies` (fieldless, watch-others: fires on every battlefield permanent whenever any enchanted creature dies, gated on that watcher's controller having controlled ≥1 of the Auras attached to it, read from the same pre-move `dying_creature_attachments` snapshot `EnchantedCreatureDies` uses) plus `Amount::AurasYouControlledAttachedToDyingCreature`, a `SacrificedCreaturePower`-shaped placeholder baked to `Fixed` at trigger placement from that same snapshot. `Trigger::CreatureEnchantedByYourAuraAttacks { at_least }` extends the landed `queue_batch_attack_triggers` (#91) with a third gate: how many of the whole committed attacker set are each enchanted by an Aura the watcher's controller controls, via a new `Game::auras_controlled_by_attached_to` query helper. Fully faithful (note deleted): hateful_eidolon. killian_decisive_mentor's second ability now faithful; its first-ability residual (tap-and-goad on an ETB stand-in) was closed **2026-07-14** by re-pointing it to the real `Trigger::PermanentEnters { filter = "enchantment", controller = "you" }` watch — killian is now fully faithful, note deleted.
**Follow-up noticed:** `AnEnchantedCreatureDies` gates its own firing on the per-watcher Aura count being nonzero rather than always firing "an enchanted creature died" and drawing zero — behaviorally identical (no pool card reacts to the ability merely being on the stack) but worth widening if that ever stops being true.

### 109. `optional-targets-up-to` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Declinable "up to one/N" targets generalized: on resolution-time effect riders ("you may return another permanent card from your graveyard" — Deadly Brew, generalizing the landed Excava up-to-one shape into the sequenced-effects path) and at trigger placement (Killian's tap-and-goad is currently mandatory — an optional-target min=0 surface on `ChooseTarget`).
*Cards:* deadly_brew, killian_decisive_mentor
**Landed:** `Effect::MayReturnFromGraveyard { filter: CardFilter }` (the graveyard-return twin of `MaySacrifice`) pauses on a new `PendingChoice::MayReturnFromGraveyard`, reusing `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s "empty declines, one entry picks" wire shape. A new `CardFilter::Permanent` (any permanent card, no MV bound) models "another permanent card" — "another" is unobservable (any graveyard permanent card is legal). Deadly Brew's rider is a second `[[abilities.effects]]` step (the ability's `Sequence` machinery already defers a pausing tail past the multi-player edict's own choices) — fully faithful except the "if you sacrificed" gate (below).
Killian also landed: `PendingChoice::ChooseTarget` gained `optional: bool`, sourced from `Effect::target_count().min == 0` (now recursing into `Sequence` so a leading step's overridden `count` — Killian's `tap_target { count = { max = 1 } }` — governs the whole shared-target sequence); declining drops the whole ability (both `tap_target` and `goad_target`, which share the one target) instead of placing it targetless. `Game::forced_action`'s single-legal-target auto-answer now skips when `optional` (a real decision even with one candidate). Killian's "target is mandatory" clause is trimmed from its note.
**Residual:** Deadly Brew's "if you sacrificed a permanent this way" gate is approximated as unconditional (the rider always offers) — no cross-`submit()` state exists to check whether the caster's own edict choice actually happened; ponytail-noted on the card. Killian keeps its enchantment-enters-watch stand-in and #108-blocked second ability.
**Progress (2026-07-14):** closed Deadly Brew's residual. A new `Game::sacrificed_by_edict_controller` scratch flag (mirroring the other `*_this_way` resolution-scoped fields) resets to `false` at `Game::begin_sacrifice_edict` and is set only when the edict's own controller — not just any affected player — sacrifices ≥1 permanent in `Game::choose_sacrifices`. `Effect::MayReturnFromGraveyard` gained `if_you_sacrificed_this_way: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`, so Witch of the Moors and Witherbloom Command's ungated consumers are unchanged): set, the rider runs nothing at all — no pause — unless the flag is set. deadly_brew is now fully faithful (`approximates` and its `# ponytail:` header deleted).

### 110. `per-mode-targets` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Independent targets per chosen mode of one modal spell/ability — `Modes` currently stores a single shared target: destroy an artifact AND an enchantment AND a planeswalker as three separate targets in one cast (Casualties of War), and cross-mode restrictions ("each mode must target a different player" — Shadrix's begin-combat choose-two). Sketch: per-mode target slots collected in the `ChooseSpellTargets` flow, following v1 #31's `TargetList` precedent.
*Cards:* casualties_of_war, shadrix_silverquill
**Progress (2026-07-11, partial pool):** the per-mode-target machinery this entry called for was already built by an earlier increment (each chosen mode carries its own target; `cast.rs::validate_modes` checks each mode's target independently). The only real gap for casualties_of_war was `MAX_MODES` capping the mode arena at 4 while the card prints 5 — bumped `crates/engine/src/types.rs::MAX_MODES` to 5 and authored all five modes (creature/artifact/enchantment/land/planeswalker), each its own `destroy_target` mode with its own target spec. casualties_of_war is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).
**Landed (2026-07-12):** shadrix_silverquill's modal *triggered*-ability half — a distinct mechanism from a modal spell's cast-time modes, since a trigger's modes are placed, not cast. `Game::place_pending_triggers` now special-cases a `modal` source with no `Timing::Spell` ability (so a modal spell's own incidental trigger, if one ever exists, isn't misread as a mode): instead of the ordinary `OrderTriggers` pause for several simultaneously-queued abilities, it pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseTriggerModes { modes, choose, optional }`, answered by `Intent::ChooseTriggerModes` (mirroring `Intent::Cast`'s `(mode index, target)` pairs). `Game::answer_choose_trigger_modes` validates exactly `choose` distinct in-range modes, each target legal for that mode's own `Effect::target`, and — Shadrix-specific, not a general modal-trigger axis — every chosen target a pairwise-distinct player. Declining (an empty selection) is legal only when the pending choice is `optional`, read off the modes' shared `Ability::optional` (every mode of a modal-trigger card carries the same "may" flag). Two new effect axes carry the per-mode Player-target recipient: `TokenController::TargetPlayer` (`create_token { controller = "target_player" }`, CR 111.4) and `Effect::PutCountersEach::target_player` (evaluates the filter's `you`/`opponent` axis from the target's perspective instead of the controller's); the third mode reuses the existing `target_player_draws`/`target_player_loses_life` pair in a `Sequence`. shadrix_silverquill is now fully faithful (`approximates` and its `# ponytail:` header deleted) — both #110 cards are faithful; section closed.

### 111. `copy-own-spell` — 3 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Copy a spell you yourself cast, as a rider or trigger: "if this spell was cast from a graveyard, copy it, may choose new targets" (Sevinne's Reclamation — a cast-context condition + self-copy hook; `CopyTargetSpell`+retarget landed) and "whenever you cast an instant/sorcery with X in its cost, copy it" (Unbound Flourishing's copy half, dep #67's `HasXInCost`).
*Cards:* sevinnes_reclamation, unbound_flourishing, owlin_spiralmancer
**Landed:** `Effect::CopyThisSpell` gained `cast_from_graveyard_only`/`optional` (both `#[serde(default)]`, so every existing mandatory storm/Gravestorm consumer is unchanged): `cast_from_graveyard_only` gates the mint on `Spell::flashback`; `optional` pauses on a `PendingChoice::MayYesNo` before minting, resolved inline by `Game::answer_may` (not placed as a new triggered ability — the rider is part of the copied spell's own resolution). That inline mint needs the original spell to still be a live `Object::Spell` when the pause clears, so `Game::resolve_spell` now defers a paused `CardKind::Spell`'s move to its post-resolution zone (`Game::pending_spell_finish`) until `Game::resume_deferred_sequence` sees the pause fully clear, instead of moving it out from under its own still-open decision. sevinnes_reclamation is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).
**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed the live-battlefield-watch half — `Game::queue_cast_spell_triggers` now threads the cast spell's own `ObjectId` into `TriggerContext::triggering_spell` (previously set only by the delayed-trigger/spend-to-cast paths), so a matched `Trigger::CastSpell` ability's `Effect::CopyTriggeringSpell` bakes in a real id instead of no-op'ing on `None`. Added `SpellFilter::InstantOrSorceryWithXInCost` (`"instant_or_sorcery_with_x"` — `InstantOrSorcery` AND `HasXInCost` combined; no general And-combinator exists, see #90) for Unbound Flourishing's filter. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** owlin_spiralmancer — "whenever you cast your first spell with {X} … each turn, you may copy it" now fires as an `optional` `cast_spell` trigger (`spell_filter = "has_x"`, `nth_each_turn = 1`) whose `copy_triggering_spell` effect mints and (optionally) retargets the copy. **Trimmed to a precise residual:** unbound_flourishing — the copy-half of the second ability ("… or activate an ability … copy that ability") is now landed for the instant/sorcery-spell case; the "double the value of X" first ability (#128 replacement-doubling) and the ability-copy half (no ability-copy mechanic in the pool) remain dropped, noted.
**Follow-up (not built here):** CR 707.10c's "a copy of a permanent spell becomes a token" is unimplemented in `Game::resolve_spell`/`Event::PermanentEntered` — a permanent-spell copy resolves into an ordinary (non-token) permanent via `fresh_permanent`, not `fresh_token`. No pool card exercises this today (Owlin/Unbound/Thunderclap Drake's copy targets are all instants/sorceries or {X} spells cast by the pool's decks, which happen to be non-permanent in every current test), but a future card copying a permanent spell would misbehave (e.g. surviving a "when this token leaves the battlefield" check, or double-counting toward a real nontoken permanent count). Fix belongs in the shared copy-resolution path, not per-card.

### 112. `self-cast-trigger` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
"When you cast this spell" triggers fired from the stack for the spell itself, not a battlefield watcher: Hydroid Krasis's gain/draw half-X (plus the round-down `HalfX` sibling the v1 note reserved) and Leitmotif Composer's copy-self-on-cast. Sketch: a trigger scanned off the cast card's own def at the `SpellCast` event, controller = caster.
*Cards:* hydroid_krasis, leitmotif_composer
**Landed:** `Trigger::YouCastThis` (`timing = "when_you_cast_this"`), scanned off the cast spell's own `def` at the same `Event::SpellCast` site as `queue_cast_spell_triggers`, via the existing `Game::queue_trigger_group` (source = the spell object itself, so the ability is a separate stack object per CR 601.2i/603.3 — still resolves if the spell is later countered, CR 702.137a). `Amount::HalfXRoundedDown` (the round-down sibling `HalfX`'s doc had reserved) and a `TriggerContext.cast_x`/`fill_cast_x` last-known-information fill (mirroring `fill_cast_mana_value`) carry the cast's chosen `{X}` into the trigger's effect at placement. hydroid_krasis is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).
**Still blocked:** leitmotif_composer's copy-self-on-cast trigger needs the spell-copy machinery (#111 `copy-own-spell`), unrelated to this increment's self-cast-trigger *timing* (its `{2}{U}` unblockable-grant activated ability is also still unlanded — a name-filtered mass grant, no such filter axis exists); note kept.

### 113. `counter-gated-triggers` — 2 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Counter-powered trigger plumbing: `Condition::SourceHasCounters{at_least}` as an intervening-if and as a keyword-grant gate read in the characteristics recompute (Primordial Hydra's trample at ten+), plus remove-a-counter as a CR 608.2c effect-internal optional sub-action (Ingenious Prodigy's upkeep draw — the CR 602 activated-cost twin landed in v1 #11).
*Cards:* ingenious_prodigy, primordial_hydra
**Landed:** `Condition::SourceHasCounters{at_least}` + `CardDef::conditional_keywords: &'static [(Condition, Keyword)]`, read by the characteristics recompute. primordial_hydra grants trample only at ten-or-more +1/+1 counters. A fieldless `Effect::RemoveCounterFromSelf` (a negative `Event::CountersPlaced` on the ability's own source, mirroring `RemoveAllCountersThenDraw`'s removal) plus a `Condition::SourceHasCounters` arm in `Game::ability_condition_holds` (the source-aware intervening-if wrapper `queue_trigger_group` already routes through) land ingenious_prodigy's "if this creature has one or more +1/+1 counters on it, you may remove a +1/+1 counter from it. If you do, draw a card" as the `optional` may-trigger's two-step `Sequence`. Both cards fully faithful (notes deleted).

### 114. `enchant-restrictions` — 2 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
"Enchant creature you control" (and other enchant-subject restrictions) enforced at Aura cast-target and attach legality: an enchant `PermanentFilter` on the Aura kind checked in `legal_targets` and on re-attach — the shared residual v1 #59 left on both cards.
*Cards:* chains_of_custody, sheltered_by_ghosts

**Still blocked:** re-attach legality (an Aura moved onto a new host by a *different* effect) doesn't consult `enchant` yet — flagged with a `ponytail:` comment; no pool Aura re-attaches, so it's deferred.

### 115. `protection-from-quality` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Generalize `Keyword::ProtectionFrom(Color)` to a quality predicate: protection from a card type ("from creatures" — Spirit Mantle) and from multicolored (Stonecoil Serpent). The protection checks (targeting, blocking, damage, attach) read a small `ProtectionScope` instead of a single `Color`.
*Cards:* spirit_mantle, stonecoil_serpent
**Landed:** `Keyword::ProtectionFrom` now carries a `ProtectionScope` (`Color(Color)` / `Creatures` / `Multicolored`), with a custom `{ protection = "<value>" }` string parse (a color name, or `"creatures"`/`"multicolored"`) that keeps every existing `{ protection = "red" }`-style card parsing unchanged. Blocking (`Game::can_block`) and combat damage (`Game::damage_prevented_by_protection`) route through a new source-object-aware `Game::protection_blocks_source`, evaluating all three scopes since both sites already have the source `ObjectId`. Both cards are fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).
**Residual:** the targeting site (`Game::legal_targets_for`) still routes through the pre-existing colors-only `Game::protection_blocks_source_colors` — it's threaded a color bitset, not a source `ObjectId`, so `ProtectionScope::Creatures` can't be evaluated there (a ponytail note marks the gap; no pool card targets a pro-creatures permanent with a creature-sourced spell/ability). `Multicolored` *is* evaluated at the targeting site (a color-count test needs no source id).

### 116. `random-selection` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Injected-RNG choice over a card set ("exile a card at random from your graveyard" — Advanced Reconstruction; Animist's Awakening's "chosen at random" reveals), determinism preserved via the seeded RNG the engine already requires for shuffles. Sketch: a random-pick resolver replacing a `PendingChoice` wherever the rules say random.
*Cards:* advanced_reconstruction, animists_awakening
**Progress (2026-07):** landed `Effect::ExileRandomFromGraveyardMayPlay` — a fieldless, no-target primitive resolved in `resolve_effect` (`&mut self`, the only place `Game::next_u64` may be called), picking `next_u64() % len` over the controller's own graveyard the same idiom `Game::shuffle` uses, then reusing the existing `Event::ExiledFromGraveyardMayPlay` (no new Event/PendingChoice/Intent/schema surface). Empty graveyard is a silent no-op (CR 701.19a). advanced_reconstruction's base (level-1) ability is now fully faithful: `mill_self{count=1}` then `exile_random_from_graveyard_may_play`; note trimmed to the residual Class/leveling structure (level 2/3, unbuilt) plus the upkeep-stands-in-for-first-main-phase timing stand-in.
**Still blocked:** animists_awakening untouched — its "random" clause is "put the rest on the bottom of your library in a random order" (a shuffle-flavored reorder, not a single random pick), and its real blocker is the reveal-top-X / X-scaling shape (unbuilt), not random selection. Section not LANDED.

that section's closing note — the new `Effect::RevealTopCards`). Its "random order" bottoming clause
stays the same deterministic library-order stand-in `reveal_until`/`open_the_way` already use for
this section's own precedent (no `rand` in the pure engine) — a `ponytail:` comment on the card names
the gap. Both #116 cards are now scripted; the section is closed with that one carried-forward
ponytail on the reorder half (not a random-*pick* gap, which is what this section actually tracks).

### 117. `per-player-effect-scopes` — 2 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Re-scope existing verbs to a chosen player: target-player-discards-N (Prismari Command mode 1 — the landed discard verb is controller-only), target player creates a Treasure (mode 2), and a strict untargeted "you draw X" (Pull from Tomorrow's cosmetic residual). One `who` field per verb, following `TokenController`'s pattern.
*Cards:* prismari_command, pull_from_tomorrow
**Landed:** added `target_player: bool` to `Effect::Discard` and `Effect::CreateTreasure` (default `false` = controller; `true` resolves against a chosen Player target per CR 111.4). prismari_command is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted): mode 1 is a `[target_player_draws, discard{target_player=true}]` Sequence sharing the one Player target (the targeted player draws two then pauses on their own DiscardCards), mode 2 creates the Treasure under the targeted player's control.
**Still blocked:** pull_from_tomorrow keeps its cosmetic note — its draw is still `target_player_draws` (self-targeted) rather than a strict "you draw X"; that needs `Effect::DrawCards` to take an `Amount` (out of scope, touches 11 call sites). Its discard rider was already faithful. Follow-up: the modal-mode resolution loop in `effects.rs::resolve_spell` doesn't check `resolution_is_paused()` between chosen modes — benign today (a discard-pausing mode's end state is order-independent of the other modes) but a modal card whose low-index mode pauses and whose high-index mode depends on that pause would resolve out of order.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** the premise above was stale — `Effect::DrawCards { count: Amount }` already draws for the controller (it predates this section; no `Amount` plumbing was needed). pull_from_tomorrow's draw step swapped `target_player_draws` → `draw_cards`; its `approximates` note and stale header prose are deleted (fully faithful). The modal-resolution-order follow-up above is untouched (still open, no modal card in the pool exercises it yet).

### 118. `each-player-step-hooks` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Statics/triggers acting during other players' turn steps: "untap all creatures you control during each other player's untap step" (Drumbellower — a static-fed exclusion/addition on the untap sweep, extending the v1 #12 `EachUpkeep` precedent) and `Trigger::EachEndStep`, the end-step twin of `EachUpkeep` (Relic Retriever).
*Cards:* drumbellower, relic_retriever
**Progress (2026-07):** landed `Trigger::EachEndStep` — the every-player twin of `EachUpkeep`, queued at the `Step::End` `StepBegan` event alongside the existing controller-scoped `EndStep`. relic_retriever switched `timing = "end_step"` → `"each_end_step"`; its `approximates` note is deleted (fully faithful).
**Landed (2026-07):** the remaining half — `Trigger::EachOtherPlayerUntapStep` (TOML `each_other_player_untap_step`), the mirror image of `EachUpkeep`/`EachEndStep`: it fires under its own controller at every *other* player's untap step, explicitly skipping the controller's own. Queued off `Event::StepBegan { step: Step::Untap, .. }` in `triggers.rs` (`queue_each_other_player_untap_step_triggers`), gated on `owner_of(permanent) != untapping_player`. Reuses the existing `Effect::UntapAll { filter }` (already TOML-deserializable via `Effect`'s own `rename_all = "snake_case"` — no `de.rs` change needed there). The untap step grants no priority (CR 502), so the queued ability rides the normal APNAP placement path and resolves at the following priority window rather than mid-sweep — a `ponytail:` comment at the queue site notes this is behaviorally identical for Drumbellower. drumbellower authored (`timing = "each_other_player_untap_step"`, `untap_all` over `filter = "creature"`); its `approximates` note is deleted (fully faithful). Both cards in this section are now faithful — section LANDED.

### 119. `mass-exile-verbs` — 2 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
`exile_all{filter}` — the exile twin of `destroy_all` over the existing `MovedToExile` pipeline (Oversimplify's symmetric wipe; CR 111.7 token cease-to-exist already handled at the exile step) — and the "each player exiles their graveyard" mass variant of the landed `ExileGraveyard` (Final Act's mode, named open in v1 #30).
*Cards:* final_act, oversimplify
**Landed:** added `Effect::ExileAll { filter }` — mirrors `DestroyAll` but with no indestructible guard (CR 701.18a: exile isn't "destroy") and routes non-tokens through the shared `exile_or_command` choke (commander diverts to the command zone, CR 903.9b; tokens cease to exist, CR 111.7). oversimplify swapped `destroy_all`→`exile_all` (`filter = "creatures"`); its note trimmed to the residual.
**Still blocked:** oversimplify's Fractal-rebuild rider (each player makes a 0/0 Fractal with +1/+1 counters equal to their exiled power) — blocked on #89 (token-with-power-derived-counters). final_act untouched: its "each player exiles their graveyard" mode is one of a 5-mode "choose one or more" spell blocked on #110 (modal choose-one-or-more), out of scope for this slice.

### 120. `restricted-mana-credits` — 2 cards, M — **LANDED (2026-07)**
A spend-restriction predicate on pooled mana credits, checked in the payment planner: "only to cast instant or sorcery spells" (Galazeth's granted Treasure ability — the grant itself landed in v1 #57 and was deliberately left unauthored) and "only on spells with MV 5+ or with {X} in their cost" (Troyan). Sketch: a restriction tag alongside the credit, consulted by `spend_plan` against the spell being paid — the same shape `Mana::OfColors` added for color restriction.
*Cards:* galazeth_prismari, troyan_gutsy_explorer
**Landed:** `Mana::Restricted { base: RestrictedManaBase, restriction: SpendRestriction }` — `RestrictedManaBase` is `Color`/`Colorless`/`Any` (the kinds real restricted-mana cards produce); `SpendRestriction` is `InstantOrSorcery` or `ManaValueAtLeastOrHasX(u32)`. `ManaPool` grows a small fixed-size `restricted` slot array (keyed by `(base, restriction)`, not an indexed bitmask like `of_colors` — a restriction carries arbitrary data). `spend_plan` takes an `Option<SpellCharacteristics>` (`None` for an ability-activation payment, where a restricted credit can never apply): it folds every restricted credit the spell satisfies into the plain algorithm as its `base` kind, then splits the resulting plan back into real-vs-restricted usage. `AddMana`/`GrantManaAbility` grow a `restriction` field wrapping the whole batch (`ManaPool::restricted_by`); a granted ability's batch is wrapped once in `Game::granted_mana_abilities` so every reader (its own resolution, `available_mana`) sees it pre-restricted. galazeth_prismari's grant authored (was unauthored pending this); troyan_gutsy_explorer's `add_mana` restricted. Both notes deleted.
**Follow-up noticed:** `RESTRICTED_SLOTS = 4` is a fixed-size ceiling (silently drops mana past it, ponytailed) — raise it if a deck combination ever needs more than 2 concurrent distinct restrictions. `RestrictedManaBase`/`spend_plan`'s fold only cover `Color`/`Colorless`/`Any` bases, not a dual or `OfColors` credit — no pool card restricts one; widen if one appears.

### 121. `graveyard-statics` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Continuous statics and non-upkeep triggers functioning from the graveyard — the distinct larger v1 #53 slice: widen the `functions_in_graveyard` gate to the characteristics recompute scan (Anger's haste anthem from the graveyard) and to the `PermanentEnters`/landfall trigger scan (Bloodghast's landfall self-return + conditional haste, whose "can't block" also needs #80).
*Cards:* anger, bloodghast
**Landed:** `Game::matching_anthems` (the `anthem_pt_bonus`/`anthem_keywords` choke) now scans two source sets — battlefield permanents the owner controls *and* the owner's graveyard cards flagged `functions_in_graveyard` — tagging each source with whether it sits in the graveyard. `Effect::AnthemStatic` grows a `from_graveyard: bool` (`#[serde(default)]` false); the scan applies a `false` anthem only from a battlefield source and a `true` one only from a graveyard source, so a card carrying both a battlefield anthem and a graveyard-functional ability (Vanguard of the Restless: Spirit anthem + return trigger) never leaks either across zones, and Anger's graveyard anthem grants nothing from a battlefield copy. New `Condition::AnOpponentHasLifeAtMost { at_most }` (CR 104.3a existential over the controller's living opponents), evaluated live in `condition_holds`; `Event::LifeChanged` now invalidates the whole battlefield's characteristics cache so a life-total-gated anthem flips exactly as an opponent crosses the boundary. Bloodghast's landfall self-return reuses the already-working graveyard `PermanentEnters` scan (Vanguard's precedent) with a `land` filter + `controller = "you"` + `optional`. Both cards fully faithful (`approximates`/`ponytail:`-header prose deleted; Bloodghast's `cant_block` body keyword from #103/#80 kept). **Follow-up noticed:** `Event::LifeChanged` invalidation is board-wide (correct but coarse, ponytailed) — narrow to the changed player's opponents' permanents if a life-heavy game shows it hot.

### 122. `total-mv-budget-selection` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Selection loops bounded by a running total mana value: "put any number of nonland permanents with total MV 4 or less onto the battlefield" (Ao, with #94's battlefield dest) and the push-your-luck one-at-a-time reveal ("exile one at a time; stop or bust past 13" — Dance with Calamity). Sketch: a budgeted `SelectFromTop` variant validating the sum of picks, plus the incremental reveal loop.
*Cards:* ao_the_dawn_sky, dance_with_calamity
**Landed:** two independent effects (not a shared abstraction). Ao's mode 1: new `Effect::LookAtTop.mv_budget: Option<u32>` (`#[serde(default)]` None = uncapped, every existing look-at-top unchanged) threaded onto `PendingChoice::SelectFromTop`; `Game::select_from_top` rejects an answer whose selected cards' summed `mana_value()` exceeds the budget, independent of the `up_to`/`min` count bounds. Ao's whole dies trigger is now authored — a `choose_one` over [mode 1 = `look_at_top { count = 7, filter = { nonland_permanent_with_mana_value_at_most = 4 }, up_to = 7, min = 0, dest = "battlefield", rest = "bottom", mv_budget = 4 }`] and [mode 2 = `put_counters_each` two counters on your creatures]. Dance: new `Effect::ExileTopUntilStopCastFreeUnderBudget { budget }` + `PendingChoice::DanceExileMore` (answered by the reused yes/no `AnswerMay` wire shape, routed by pending kind) — a player-driven exile-one-at-a-time loop with a running MV tally; on stop, `total_mv <= budget` reuses `begin_choose_exiled_to_cast_free` (count = whole pile, rest stays exiled), a bust grants nothing and leaves the cards exiled. Both cards fully faithful (`approximates`/`ponytail:`-header prose deleted). **Residual ponytails:** Ao mode 2's "or Vehicle" dropped (no Vehicle type in pool); both cards' "put the rest on the bottom in a random order" uses the deterministic library-order stand-in (pure engine, no `rand`). This also clears ao_the_dawn_sky from **#94**'s still-blocked list (its "mode 1 needs #122" residual).

### 123. `ability-grants-beyond-mana` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-14)**
Grant whole non-mana abilities to another object, widening v1 #57's `GrantManaAbility` seam (`Game::ability_at` is the one address point): `grant_to_attached` carrying an activated ability (Fallen Ideal's "has 'Sacrifice a creature: +2/+1'") and Backup's ETB counter + grant-this-card's-other-abilities-until-EOT (Guardian Scalelord). The granted-ability scan already exists for mana abilities; the new work is non-mana activation/trigger routing through the same seam.
*Cards:* fallen_ideal, guardian_scalelord
**Progress (2026-07-13, fallen_ideal slice — NOT fully LANDED):** widened #57's grant seam to non-mana activated abilities. New `Effect::GrantToAttached.granted_ability: Option<&'static GrantedAbility>` (a `{ cost: ActivationCost, effects: &'static [Effect] }` descriptor) + a `Game::granted_attachment_abilities` scan (the non-mana twin of `granted_mana_abilities`, sourced from the attachment relationship). `Game::ability_at` now addresses abilities in a stable order — own, then granted mana, then granted attachment — and `push_activatable_abilities` (meaningful-actions) enumerates the granted attachment ability so it's activatable. fallen_ideal is now **fully faithful** (`approximates` deleted): its host gains flying and "Sacrifice a creature: This creature gets +2/+1 until end of turn.", activated on the host (may sacrifice itself), gone the instant the Aura leaves. Also fixed a latent panic: `pump_self_until_end_of_turn` now guards a source that left the battlefield (CR 608.2c — reachable via the self-sacrifice line).
**Progress (2026-07-14, guardian_scalelord slice — #123 now fully LANDED):** landed both halves of the Backup rider. (a) New `Effect::GrantSourceAbilitiesUntilEndOfTurn` (a fieldless step riding the enclosing Backup ETB sequence's shared counter target): records a `(target, source)` link in `Game::abilities_granted_until_eot`, no-op when the target is the source itself ("if that's *another* creature"). The granted set is read live off the source's `CardDef` — `Game::granted_source_abilities` feeds `queue_trigger_group` (so a granted triggered ability fires for the target, minus the granting ability itself, CR 702.166b), and `effective_keywords` unions the source's keywords (so the target actually gains flying). Cleared at cleanup by a new public `Event::GrantedAbilitiesEnded` (mirrored in schema); `Event::AbilitiesGranted` announces the grant. (b) New `CardFilter::NonlandPermanentWithManaValueAtMostSourcePower` placeholder, baked to `NonlandPermanentWithManaValueAtMost(power)` at attack-trigger placement by a new `fill_source_power` reading `TriggerContext::source_power` (the attacker's power, CR 510.2/603.10a) — the same fill idiom as `fill_combat_damage`. guardian_scalelord is **fully faithful** (`approximates` deleted): Backup grant + MV-X-or-less reanimation + nonland breadth all exact.

### 124. `artifact-creature-type` — 2 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Multi-type permanents — the v1 #19 read side landed (`CardKind::Creature.also: TypeSet`, unioned in `types()`), but the card loader hardcodes `TypeSet::NONE` — no authoring surface. Add the TOML field so Artifact Creature / Enchantment Creature reach `PermanentFilter` and per-type counts, and artifact-sac costs and constellation-adjacent counts stop miscounting (Brudiclad's Myr, Doomwake's enchantment body).
*Cards:* brudiclad_telchor_engineer, doomwake_giant
**Landed:** pure authoring (`also = [...]` on `[kind]`, zero engine-source edits — read side was already wired). doomwake_giant (`also = ["enchantment"]`, Enchantment Creature) and brudiclad_telchor_engineer (`also = ["artifact"]`, Artifact Creature) now carry both types.
**Still blocked:** brudiclad's "creature tokens you control have haste" (needs a keyword-only token-scoped anthem the pool lacks) and "each other token becomes a copy" (#33 copy machinery). doomwake_giant is otherwise fully faithful (its own-ETB self-fire landed in #97).

### 125. `counter-and-fizzle-rules` — 2 cards, S — **LANDED (2026-07)**
Two stack-rules fixes, no card scripts: CR 608.2b whole-spell fizzle — when every target is illegal at resolution, skip the untargeted rider clauses too (Infernal Grasp currently still charges the 2 life after its destroy fizzles) — and a "this spell can't be countered" `CardDef` flag checked in `counter_spell`/`CounterTargetSpell` resolution (target stays legal, the counter fizzles — Altered Ego).
*Cards:* altered_ego, infernal_grasp
**Landed:** CR 608.2b whole-spell fizzle guard in `resolve_spell` — a spell with at least one targeted step, none of them legal at resolution, skips its entire step loop (untargeted riders no longer resolve); infernal_grasp is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted — the destroy and "you lose 2 life" both fizzle together). Added `CardDef.uncounterable` (CR 701.5g), checked in the shared `counter_spell` choke covering both the `CounterTargetSpell` arm and the declined `PayOrCounter` path; altered_ego's `uncounterable = true` wired end-to-end.
**Still blocked:** altered_ego's clone-on-enter (enter as a copy of any creature) — blocked on #127 (enter-as-copy); it still resolves as a 0/0 entering with X +1/+1 counters.

---

## Tier 3 — the former non-goals, now real (XL subsystems, staged)

These were v1's "deliberate non-goals." Under ADR 0014 they are in scope — each gets a staged plan whose first slice is a real, bounded increment. Flag-don't-force still applies *within* them: land the slice a real card needs, not the whole CR chapter.

### 126. `type-change-layers` — 8 cards, XL — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
CR 613 type/ability/P/T-setting layers — the layered characteristics recompute replacing the additive-only anthem model: add/set card types and subtypes ("becomes a 1/1 Spirit creature with flying" — Excava, Darksteel Mutation; "is an Angel" — Angelic Destiny), remove abilities, set base P/T (X/X from cast context — Biomass Mutation; equal to another creature's base P/T, read live — Tanazir; until-EOT on a spell target — Quandrix Charm mode 3), and manland animation with its dependent triggers (Restless Spire). *Staged plan:* (1) a layer-entry list on the recompute — `{source, timestamp, layer: TypeSet|AbilitySet|BasePT|PT-delta}` — with the existing anthems migrated onto it as layer-7c entries, behavior-preserving; (2) layer-7b base-P/T-set from Auras (Darksteel Mutation, sourced from the attachment — supersedes the fixed `set_attached_base_p_t`); (3) type-set + ability-remove entries (Excava's Spirit, "loses all abilities"); (4) until-EOT one-shot layer entries with timestamps (Quandrix Charm, Restless Spire). Cross-cutting per ADR 0003 — schedule slice 1 early, it de-risks everything else.
*Cards:* angelic_destiny, biomass_mutation, darksteel_mutation, excava_the_risen_past, muddle_the_ever_changing, quandrix_charm, restless_spire, tanazir_quandrix
**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 1 of 4 (P/T layer-entry migration) landed — behavior-preserving; NOT LANDED.** The additive P/T recompute (`compute_power_uncached`/`compute_toughness_uncached` in `characteristics.rs`) is now a CR 613-ordered layered recompute: a private engine-internal `PtLayer { source, timestamp, kind: BasePtSet(7b) | PtDelta(7c) }` (a runtime `Vec`, not a `CardDef`/TOML surface — `CardDef` stays `Copy`), gathered by a new `Game::pt_layers` (re-expressing the existing `set_base_pt` / `plus_counters` / `temp_power`+`temp_toughness` / `anthem_pt_bonus` / `attachment_grants` scans as entries, not re-deriving them) and applied by `Game::apply_pt_layers` (every 7b base-set replaces the running base first, then every 7c delta sums on top). Both compute fns now call `pt_layers` + `apply_pt_layers`; the caching wrapper (`power`/`toughness`) is untouched. **Behavior-preserving** — the entire suite stayed green (1127 engine tests), locked by a new characterization test `layered_pt_recompute_matches_additive_stack` (one creature under a base-set Aura + counters + until-EOT pump + matching anthem + `grant_to_attached` Aura at once). No card TOML changed; no card is newly faithful this slice. **ponytail:** every entry's `source`/`timestamp` is the host object's id as a deterministic stand-in — with ≤1 base-set in the pool and commutative 7c deltas, application is order-independent, so real CR 613.7 dependency ordering + per-effect timestamps are deferred to slice 4. **Next — slice 2:** layer-7b base-P/T-set from Auras (Darksteel Mutation), sourced from the attachment, superseding the fixed `set_attached_base_p_t`. Slices 3 (type-set + ability-remove) and 4 (until-EOT one-shots with real timestamps) also remain.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — type + subtype layer from Auras landed; NOT LANDED (overall).** New `Effect::SetAttachedTypes { add_types: TypeSet, add_subtypes: &'static [&'static str], set_subtypes: &'static [&'static str] }` (TOML `set_attached_types`) — an Aura `timing = "static"` modeled on `set_attached_base_p_t`, never resolved off the stack. Collector `Game::attached_type_layer(host)` scans the host's attached Auras for it (guard-return, `// ponytail:` ≤1 type-changing Aura per host → CR 613.7 ordering deferred). Two new public readers `Game::effective_types(id) -> TypeSet` (printed `kind.types()` ∪ added) and `Game::effective_subtypes(id) -> Vec<&'static str>` (`set_subtypes` replaces, else printed ∪ `add_subtypes`), computed live off the attachment scan (no cache — reverts the instant the Aura leaves). Wired at the battlefield-permanent type/subtype match chokes: `query.rs::permanent_matches` (types + subtypes — mass/edict/target/count filters), `characteristics.rs::matching_anthems` subtype gate, and `modifier_sources`' anthem attribution. Reads of cards off the battlefield (hand/library/graveyard/stack, `spell_shares_creature_type_with_commander`) stay on the printed `def` (CR 613 is a battlefield continuous effect). **Behavior-preserving where no type-changing Aura is attached** — full suite green. **angelic_destiny fully faithful** (`approximates` deleted — "is an Angel in addition to its other types" is `set_attached_types { add_subtypes = ["Angel"] }`). **darksteel_mutation trimmed** to its `"loses all other abilities"` residual only (`set_attached_types { add_types = "artifact", set_subtypes = ["Insect"] }` + the already-faithful 0/1 base + indestructible). Tests: `angelic_destiny_makes_enchanted_creature_an_angel` (Angel filter + Angel anthem buff, reverts on removal), `darksteel_mutation_sets_type_line` (Artifact type + Insect subtype set-replace drops Bear, still Creature/0/1/indestructible, reverts). **Next slice — ability-add/remove layer** (Darksteel's "loses all abilities", Muddle) via CR 613.1e/6 — no `ability_at`/keyword-suppression machinery exists yet. Also still remaining: self-sourced one-shot type sets from a resolved triggered ability with a duration (Excava's reanimation, Quandrix Charm, Restless Spire animation), Tanazir live base-P/T copy, Biomass Mutation set-base-from-Amount. Do NOT mark #126 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — ability-removal layer landed; NOT LANDED (overall).** Added a `lose_all_abilities: bool` axis (`#[serde(default)]` false) to `Effect::SetAttachedTypes` (TOML `lose_all_abilities` beside `add_types`/`add_subtypes`/`set_subtypes`; `Effect`/`CardDef` stay `Copy`). Predicate `Game::host_loses_all_abilities(host) -> bool` (characteristics.rs, next to `attached_type_layer`) scans the host's attached Auras' `Timing::Static` `SetAttachedTypes` for the flag (guard-return on non-permanent, `// ponytail:` ≤1 ability-removing Aura per host → CR 613.7 ordering deferred). Single choke `Game::functional_abilities(id) -> &'static [Ability]` returns `&[]` for a live lose-all host, else the printed slice. Wired at: **trigger placement** — central `queue_trigger_group` early-returns for a lose-all host (covers Attacks/Dies-while-alive/watchers/Magecraft/cast/discard/etc.; a death last-known-info `def` snapshot is never a live host so its triggers still fire), plus the 9 inline trigger scanners that don't route through it (`queue_batch_attack`/`sacrifice`/`permanent_enters` watchers/`self_permanent_enters`/`combat_damage`/`cast_spell`/`player_draws`/`becomes_targeted`/`spell_targets_this_only`) and `matching_trigger_doublers` swapped to `functional_abilities`; **activation gate** — `ability_activation_gate` rejects a printed-index ability (`index < def.abilities.len()`) on a lose-all host (also gates `meaningful_actions`, which reads the same gate); **static scan** — `matching_anthems`'s source loop reads `functional_abilities` so the host's own anthem stops; **keyword compute** — `compute_effective_keywords_uncached` starts from an empty printed-keyword set (skipping printed `keywords` + `conditional_keywords`) for a lose-all host, still applying `attachment_grants`/`temp_keywords`/`anthem_keywords`/etc. so the Aura's OWN granted indestructible survives while printed flying vanishes. Reverts live off the attachment scan (no cache of its own; keyword change rides the existing attach/detach cache drop). **Behavior-preserving with no ability-removing Aura attached** — full suite green (1142 engine tests). **darksteel_mutation fully faithful** (`approximates` + the ability-remove `# ponytail:` header deleted). Tests: `darksteel_mutation_removes_enchanted_creature_abilities` (host loses flying + activated ability + attack trigger, keeps the Aura's indestructible/0-1/Artifact/Insect, reverts on detach), `plain_aura_does_not_remove_abilities` (Angelic Destiny leaves the host's activated ability + attack trigger intact). **Next slice — self-sourced one-shot type/ability sets from a *resolved* triggered ability with a duration** (Excava's reanimation, Quandrix Charm mode 3, Restless Spire animation), Tanazir live base-P/T copy, Biomass Mutation set-base-from-Amount, and the become-a-copy ability *add* (Muddle, #127). Do NOT mark #126 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — until-EOT base-P/T SET (7b one-shot layer on `Permanent`, cleared at cleanup) landed; NOT LANDED (overall).** New runtime field `Permanent::base_pt_set_eot: Option<(i32, i32)>` (init `None` at construction; never a `CardDef`/TOML surface, never wire-mirrored — P/T is derived, like `temp_power`), emitted as a second `BasePtSet` layer by `Game::pt_layers` when present (applied before the 7c counters/pumps/anthems), written by new `Event::BasePtSetUntilEndOfTurn { object, power, toughness }` (schema-mirrored, public — no redaction), and cleared alongside `temp_power`/`temp_toughness` at the same cleanup choke (`Event::TempBoostsEnded`'s handler + the `priority.rs` Cleanup scan).
