Two new effects both resolve their `Amount` off the spell/effect controller: `Effect::SetBasePtCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn { power, toughness }` (TOML `set_base_pt_creatures_you_control_until_end_of_turn` — the "you control" mass scan, mirroring `PumpCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn`) and `Effect::SetBasePtTargetUntilEndOfTurn { power, toughness, target }` (TOML `set_base_pt_target_until_end_of_turn` — single-target, mirroring `PumpUntilEndOfTurn`). **Behavior-preserving with no until-EOT base-set active** — full suite green. **biomass_mutation trimmed** to its `{G/U}{G/U}` hybrid-mana residual only (`set_base_pt_creatures_you_control_until_end_of_turn` with `power`/`toughness` `= "x"`; the "no set-base effect / ability dropped" clause deleted). **quandrix_charm fully faithful** (mode 3 authored as `set_base_pt_target_until_end_of_turn` 5/5 on `target = "creature"`; `approximates` deleted, all three modes present). Tests: `biomass_mutation_sets_your_creatures_base_pt_to_x` (two creatures of different printed P/T both set to X/X, a +1/+1 counter stacks on the set base, reverts at cleanup), `quandrix_charm_mode_three_sets_target_base_pt_5_5` (target set to 5/5, counter delta layers on top, reverts). **ponytail:** `pt_layers` can now push TWO `BasePtSet` layers on one host (a `SetAttachedBasePT` Aura + an until-EOT set), but no pool card combines them, so CR 613.7 timestamp/dependency ordering stays deferred to the slice that stacks two base-sets. **Next slice — manland animation** (Restless Spire — add a creature type + base P/T to a *noncreature* land as a one-shot self-effect, plus its dependent attack-triggered scry) *or* Excava's self-sourced type-SET + subtype-ADD on a reanimated creature; also remaining: Tanazir live base-P/T copy, Muddle become-a-copy (#127). Do NOT mark #126 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — manland animation (Restless Spire) landed; NOT LANDED (overall).** New `Effect::AnimateSelfUntilEndOfTurn { add_types: TypeSet, add_subtypes, base_power, base_toughness, keywords }` (TOML `animate_self_until_end_of_turn`) resolves on its own source into three until-EOT writes: `Event::TypesAddedUntilEndOfTurn { object, types, subtypes }` (new; schema-mirrored public, types/subtypes dropped from the wire like `KeywordsStripped`), the existing `Event::BasePtSetUntilEndOfTurn` (base P/T SET), and the existing `Event::TempBoost` (first-strike keyword). Two new runtime `Permanent` fields `added_types_eot: TypeSet` / `added_subtypes_eot: &'static [&'static str]` (init empty; never `CardDef`/TOML/wire), unioned in by `Game::effective_types`/`effective_subtypes` and cleared alongside `base_pt_set_eot` at the same cleanup choke (`Event::TempBoostsEnded` handler + the `priority.rs` Cleanup scan + `clear_modifier_provenance`). **Creature-ness rerouted through `effective_types`:** `Game::is_creature_on_battlefield` (`priority.rs`, the shared choke — trigger placement, activation gates, mass scans), and `can_attack`/`can_block`'s direct `def.kind` reads (`combat.rs`) now test `effective_types(id).intersects(TypeSet::CREATURE)` instead of the printed kind, so an animated land can be declared as an attacker/blocker. `compute_power_uncached`/`compute_toughness_uncached` factored into a `pt_base` helper: an animated noncreature has printed base 0/0, replaced by its `BasePtSet` layer → 2/1 (counters/pumps still layer 7c on top). **Behavior-preserving** — no pool card adds "creature" via a type layer today, so every combat/anthem/SBA test stayed green (1154 engine tests); regression caught by `pt_base`'s `as_permanent` guard (`effective_types` reads `def_of`, which panics on a Removed object queried through the P/T cache). **restless_spire faithful** (`approximates` trimmed to two residuals: the "blue and red" added colors are dropped — unobservable, no color-layer subsystem; and "During your turn" on first strike is approximated as unconditional-until-EOT — diverges only if animated on an opponent's turn to block). Tests: `restless_spire_animates_into_a_creature_until_end_of_turn` (land → 2/1 Elemental creature that's still a land, +1/+1 counter → 3/2, reverts at cleanup), `restless_spire_scries_when_it_attacks` (animated land declared as attacker, `timing = "attacks"` scry-1 fires). **Remaining #126:** excava (self-sourced type-SET + subtype-ADD on a *reanimated other* creature, indefinite duration), tanazir (live base-P/T copy), muddle (become-a-copy — #127). Do NOT mark #126 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — Excava's indefinite reanimated-creature set landed; NOT LANDED (overall).** `Effect::ReanimateToBattlefield` grew an optional `becomes: Option<&'static ReanimateBecomes>` rider (new `ReanimateBecomes { add_types: TypeSet, add_subtypes, base_power, base_toughness, keywords }` — `#[serde(default)]` `None`, leaked to `'static` like `GrantedAbility`; TOML inline `becomes = { … }`). When `Some`, the reanimate execute arm follows its `ReanimatedToBattlefield` event with a new public `Event::ReanimatedCreatureBecame { object, add_types, add_subtypes, base_power, base_toughness, keywords }` (schema-mirrored, characteristics dropped from the wire like `TypesAddedUntilEndOfTurn`) written onto the just-entered permanent. Four **indefinite** runtime `Permanent` fields — `set_base_pt: Option<(i32,i32)>` / `added_types: TypeSet` / `added_subtypes: &'static [&'static str]` / `granted_keywords: &'static [Keyword]` (init empty at `fresh_permanent`; never `CardDef`/TOML/wire) — the indefinite twins of slice 5's until-EOT fields, but **NOT cleared at cleanup** (they reset only when the object leaves the battlefield and becomes a new object, CR 611.2c/400.7). Unioned into the SAME read sites slice 5 touched: `effective_types` (∪ `added_types`), `effective_subtypes` (∪ `added_subtypes`), `pt_layers` (a second 7b `BasePtSet` from `set_base_pt`, before the 7c counter/pump deltas), `compute_effective_keywords_uncached` (∪ `granted_keywords`). **Behavior-preserving** — nothing sets these until Excava reanimates; full suite green (1162 engine tests). **excava_the_risen_past fully faithful** (`approximates` + the type-change `# ponytail:` header deleted; `becomes = { add_types = "creature", add_subtypes = ["Spirit"], base_power = 1, base_toughness = 1, keywords = ["flying"] }`). Tests: `excava_reanimates_a_creature_as_a_1_1_spirit_flyer` (vanilla 4/4 → base-SET 1/1 Spirit flyer that's still a creature, finality counter intact, +1/+1 counter → 2/2), `excava_reanimates_a_noncreature_as_a_creature` (artifact → 1/1 Spirit flyer that's now a creature AND still an artifact), `plain_reanimate_does_not_set_type` (Reanimate leaves printed P/T/types untouched). **Remaining #126:** tanazir (live base-P/T *copy* — read another creature's P/T live, a separate slice), muddle (become-a-copy — #127). Do NOT mark #126 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — Tanazir base-P/T "become equal to" landed — #126 LANDED.** Despite the backlog phrasing "live base-P/T copy," CR reads "become equal to Tanazir's power and toughness" as a **one-shot snapshot** at resolution — it does NOT keep tracking Tanazir's P/T afterward — so this is the existing until-EOT 7b base SET, not a continuous copy layer. Two small additions: `Amount::SourceToughness` (the toughness twin of `SourcePower`; de tag `"source_toughness"`, `resolve_amount` → `self.toughness(source)`, label "its toughness"), and an `other: bool` (`#[serde(default)]` false) axis on `Effect::SetBasePtCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn` — when true the "you control" scan also requires `id != source`, excluding Tanazir itself. The attack ability is authored `optional = true` (`timing = "attacks"`) with `power = "source_power"` / `toughness = "source_toughness"` / `other = true`, so it resolves Tanazir's CURRENT P/T once and bakes fixed numbers into each other creature's `base_pt_set_eot` (7b), with counters/pumps layering 7c on top and reverting at cleanup. **Behavior-preserving when `other` is absent/false** — full suite green (1167 engine tests). **tanazir_quandrix fully faithful** (`approximates` + the attack-copy-dropped `# ponytail:` header deleted). Tests: `tanazir_attack_sets_other_creatures_base_pt_to_its_own` (a 6/6 Tanazir — base 4/4 + two counters — snapshots 6/6 onto a 1/1 and a 3/2, excludes itself, 7c counter → 7/7, reverts at cleanup), `tanazir_attack_snapshot_does_not_track_later_pt` (pumping Tanazir after resolution does NOT move the snapshotted others). **#126 LANDED** — muddle's become-a-copy belongs to #127.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — restless_spire's last two card-visible residuals closed; #126 stays LANDED.** `Effect::AnimateSelfUntilEndOfTurn` gained an `add_colors: &'static [Color]` axis (`#[serde(default)]`), threaded through the existing `Event::TypesAddedUntilEndOfTurn` (widened with a `colors` field) onto a new runtime `Permanent::added_colors_eot: &'static [Color]` (init empty, cleared alongside `added_types_eot`/`added_subtypes_eot` at the same `TempBoostsEnded` cleanup choke) — unioned into `Game::colors_of` (promoted `pub(crate)` → `pub`) alongside the printed cost-pip `color_identity`. Separately, a new `Condition::DuringYourTurn` (holds iff `Game::active_player == ctx.controller`, evaluated live) reuses the existing `AnthemStatic` conditional-anthem axis (`condition: Option<Condition>`) rather than inventing a new keyword-grant flag: Restless Spire's "During your turn, this creature has first strike" is now a second `[[abilities]]` (`timing = "static"`, `anthem_static { self_only = true, keywords = ["first_strike"], condition = { type = "during_your_turn" } }`) instead of an unconditional keyword riding the animation effect's own `keywords` list — first strike now only applies while the land's controller is the active player, correctly withholding it if animated on an opponent's turn to block. **restless_spire is now fully faithful** (`approximates` + the multi-line `# ponytail:` header deleted). Tests: `restless_spire_animated_form_is_blue_and_red` (colorless before animation, exactly {blue, red} while animated, colorless again after cleanup), `restless_spire_first_strike_only_during_your_turn` (first strike present when animated on its controller's own turn, absent when animated on an opponent's turn — still a creature either way). Reusable primitives: `Condition::DuringYourTurn` (any future your-turn-conditional static/anthem) and `Permanent::added_colors_eot` (any future type-change-layer color grant).

### 127. `enter-as-copy` — 7 cards, XL — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
CR 707 copyable values — the copy half of v1 #33 that never landed: a copyable-values snapshot (printed `CardDef` + copy-layer modifications, nothing else) applied at the enter event before ETB triggers, with riders (extra +1/+1 counters — Altered Ego; gains haste, revert/sacrifice at end of turn — Cursed Mirror). *Staged plan:* (1) the snapshot type + token-copy mint ("create a token that's a copy of…" — Hofri's Spirit rider, Inspired Skypainter's back face, Angel of Indemnity's Encore-style copies, feeding #88's entry riders); (2) enter-as-copy replacement on a real permanent (Altered Ego, Cursed Mirror); (3) "becomes a copy" of an existing object — Brudiclad's mass token conversion, Spirit of Resilience's become-a-copy-of-a-leaving-card (needs the leave-batch's card list in trigger context) — which layers on #126's copy layer. Depends on: #126 slice 1 for the layer bookkeeping.
*Cards:* altered_ego, angel_of_indemnity, brudiclad_telchor_engineer, cursed_mirror, hofri_ghostforge, inspired_skypainter, spirit_of_resilience
**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 1 of 3 (token-copy mint of a specific creature):** `Effect::ExileDeadCreatureCreateCopyWithSubtype { dead: Option<ObjectId> (#[serde(skip)], baked at placement), add_subtypes: &'static [&'static str], leaves_returns_exiled: bool }` — a no-target `creature_you_control_dies*` payoff. The dead creature's id is threaded through the new `TriggerContext::dead_creature` (set in `Game::queue_death_watcher`, CR 603.10a last-known information) and baked in by the new `fill_dead_creature` walker in `contextualize_effect` (mirrors `fill_dying_enchanted_creature`). Resolution (`effects.rs`) exiles the card off its graveyard object (reusing `exile_or_command`), mints a token copy of its printed `def` via the landed `Event::TokenCreated` (CR 707.2 — ponytail: printed def, not full copyable values), and unions `add_subtypes` onto the token indefinitely via the new minimal `Event::AddedSubtypes { object, subtypes }` (writes `Permanent::added_subtypes`, #126's subtype-add primitive already unioned by `effective_subtypes`; a subtype-only sibling of `ReanimatedCreatureBecame` that leaves base P/T untouched — Hofri's copy keeps the original's P/T). `Event::AddedSubtypes` mirrored in `crates/schema` (public battlefield status). **hofri_ghostforge trimmed to the leaves-rider residual only:** its second ability is now scripted (dies-nontoken timing, self-excluded, token-death-excluded); the exile + Spirit-copy body is faithful. `leaves_returns_exiled` parses but is NOT wired — the token's granted "When this token leaves the battlefield, return the exiled card to its owner's graveyard" rider needs a per-object granted leaves trigger baking the exiled id (heavier than the rest of the slice); `approximates` trimmed to name exactly that rider. Reusable primitive: `Effect::ExileDeadCreatureCreateCopyWithSubtype` + `TriggerContext::dead_creature` + `Event::AddedSubtypes`. No other #127 card touched. Slices **2 (enter-as-copy replacement on a real permanent — altered_ego, cursed_mirror)** and **3 (becomes-a-copy — brudiclad, spirit_of_resilience)** remain; angel_of_indemnity Encore (per-opponent token copies + haste + end-step sac; different subject/rider — Hofri's primitive doesn't drop in) + inspired_skypainter (blocked on prepare/DFC) still blocked. NOT LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 2 of 3 (enter-as-copy replacement on a real permanent):** the copy primitive is a wholesale `Permanent::def` overwrite (CR 613 layer 1 / 707.2 copyable values) via the new `Event::BecameCopy { object, def, until_eot }` — every characteristics choke already reads `p.def.*`, and #126's layer fields (`plus_counters`, `added_subtypes`, `temp_power`, …) compose on top unchanged, so a clone + its own counters + anthems all layer with no change to the characteristics chokes. Authored as a rules-keyword marker `CardDef::enter_as_copy: Option<EnterAsCopy { until_eot, extra_counters, gains_haste }>` (all `Copy`, all scalars/`Amount`), paused at the `begin_devour` seam in `resolve_spell` (before ETB/counters, CR 616) on the new `PendingChoice::ChooseCopyTarget` over every *other* battlefield creature — a "you may," declinable, answered by the new `Intent::ChooseCopyTarget { copy: Option<ObjectId> }`; no candidate ⇒ no pause. The answer handler (`begin_/answer_enter_as_copy` in `pending/handlers.rs`) overwrites `def`, places `extra_counters` through `counters_after_replacements`, and grants haste via the same until-EOT `Event::TempBoost { Keyword::Haste }` `create_token_copy` uses. Until-EOT copies stash the printed def on the new runtime `Permanent::reverts_to_def_eot: Option<&'static CardDef>` (leaked at the copy step, like `CardDef::back`, to keep `Permanent: Copy` small — the `Option<CardDef>`-by-value form bloated the `Object` enum into a new `large_enum_variant`) and restore it at cleanup alongside the `_eot` layer resets (`Event::TempBoostsEnded`, CR 514.2). **SBA gate fix (CR 704.3):** `sweep_state_based_actions` now returns early while a choice is pending — Altered Ego enters a printed 0/0 and would die to the 0-toughness SBA in the gap before the copy is chosen; SBAs correctly run only on the answer that clears the choice. New wire surface (`ChooseCopyTarget` `PendingChoice`/`Intent`/`Answer`, `BecameCopy` event) mirrored in `crates/schema` (a copy is public). **altered_ego + cursed_mirror both faithful** (`approximates` + Cursed Mirror's `# ponytail:` header prose deleted). ponytail: printed `CardDef` copyable values, not full CR 707.2 copy-layer read (exact for the pool); a copied creature's own ETB trigger doesn't fire (`def` overwritten after the enter event — neither card copies an ETB creature). Reusable primitive: `Event::BecameCopy` + `CardDef::enter_as_copy` marker + `PendingChoice::ChooseCopyTarget` + `Permanent::reverts_to_def_eot`. Slice **3 (becomes-a-copy of an *existing* object via an activated/triggered ability or mass conversion — brudiclad_telchor_engineer, spirit_of_resilience — the latter needs the leave-batch's card list in trigger context)** remains; angel_of_indemnity Encore + inspired_skypainter (prepare/DFC) still blocked. NOT LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 3a of 3 (becomes-a-copy of an existing object — mass token conversion):** the new no-target `Effect::EachOtherTokenBecomesCopyOfChosen` (TOML `each_other_token_becomes_copy_of_chosen`, no fields, `CardDef: Copy` preserved) is the mass "becomes a copy of a chosen object" entry point, reusing slice 2's `Event::BecameCopy` primitive wholesale. Resolution (`effects.rs → begin_each_other_token_becomes_copy`) enumerates the controller's tokens (`permanent_ids` filtered by `token` flag + `controller_of`) and pauses on the new `PendingChoice::ChooseTokenToCopy { player, source, candidates }` — an up-to-one, declinable pick ("you may choose a token you control"); no token ⇒ no pause. The answer reuses `Intent::ChooseCopyTarget` (the answer shape is identical — one optional chosen object; dispatch in `pending/mod.rs` routes by which pending choice is live, the `CastVote` guard pattern), and `answer_each_other_token_becomes_copy` emits an **indefinite** `Event::BecameCopy { until_eot: false }` (permanent, CR 400.7) for every *other* token the controller controls — only tokens, only the controller's own. `ChooseTokenToCopy` projects onto the existing `PendingChoiceView::ChooseCopyTarget` wire shape (identical client view — "choose one of these objects"), so **no new schema variant**. **brudiclad_telchor_engineer's copy clause is faithful** — authored as effect[1] of the begin-combat ability, right after the Myr `create_token` (so the fresh Myr is a legal choice/target); `approximates` + `# ponytail:` header trimmed to the sole residual: "creature tokens you control have haste" (a token-scoped keyword-only anthem — `AnthemStatic` is P/T-only, a separate unlanded surface). ponytail: chosen token's `CardDef` copyable values, not a full CR 707.2 copy-layer read (inherits slice 2's note). Reusable primitive: `Effect::EachOtherTokenBecomesCopyOfChosen` + `PendingChoice::ChooseTokenToCopy`. Slice **3b (spirit_of_resilience — become-a-copy of an artifact/creature from among the cards that left your graveyard this turn, needs the leave-batch's card list threaded into trigger context — a new `TriggerContext` field + fill walker + a choose-from-that-list pause)** remains; angel_of_indemnity Encore + inspired_skypainter (DFC) still blocked. NOT LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 3b of 3 (become-a-copy of a card that left your graveyard):** the last become-a-copy shape. **Context threading:** `BatchTriggerScratch::graveyard_exits_this_batch` widened `Vec<PlayerId>` → `Vec<(PlayerId, ObjectId)>` (the graveyard-object id that left, pushed at `create_object`'s graveyard-exit choke, CR 603.10a last-known info); `enqueue_triggers`'s drain now groups each owner's leaving-card ids and threads them through the new `TriggerContext::cards_left_graveyard: &'static [ObjectId]` (interned via one `Box::leak` per fire so `TriggerContext` stays `Copy` — ponytail: bounded per-fire leak, upgrade to a runtime carrier if repeated fires matter), set by the new bespoke `Game::queue_cards_leave_graveyard_triggers` (mirrors `queue_magecraft_triggers`, replacing the old context-less `queue_controller_triggers(.., None)` call). The new `fill_cards_left_graveyard` walker in `contextualize_effect` bakes the slice into the effect. **The effect:** no-target `Effect::PutCounterThenMayBecomeCopyOfCardFromList { cards: &'static [ObjectId] (#[serde(skip)]) }` (TOML `put_counter_then_may_become_copy_of_card_from_list`, `CardDef: Copy` preserved). Resolution (`effects.rs → begin_put_counter_then_may_become_copy`) places one +1/+1 counter on the ability's own source (via `counters_after_replacements` + `Event::CountersPlaced`), filters `cards` to artifact/creature cards (`def.kind.types().intersects(CREATURE|ARTIFACT)`), and — if any remain — pauses on the new `PendingChoice::ChooseCopyCardFromList { player, source, candidates }`, an up-to-one declinable pick; no copyable card ⇒ counter only, no pause. The answer reuses `Intent::ChooseCopyTarget` (dispatch guard in `pending/mod.rs` alongside `ChooseTokenToCopy`) and `answer_choose_copy_card_from_list` emits slice 2's `Event::BecameCopy { until_eot: true }` (reverts at cleanup via the existing `reverts_to_def_eot` sweep, CR 706/707.2/514.2); the counter rides on top of the copy's base P/T and survives the revert. `ChooseCopyCardFromList` projects onto the existing `PendingChoiceView::ChooseCopyTarget` wire shape — **no new schema variant**. **spirit_of_resilience is now faithful** — triggered ability authored (`cards_leave_your_graveyard` timing); `# ponytail:` "body only" header + `approximates` deleted, replaced by the sole inherited residual (chosen card's printed `CardDef` copyable values, not a full CR 707.2 copy-layer read — a `# ponytail:` note). Reusable primitive: `TriggerContext::cards_left_graveyard` + `fill_cards_left_graveyard` + `Effect::PutCounterThenMayBecomeCopyOfCardFromList` + `PendingChoice::ChooseCopyCardFromList`. **#127's become-a-copy/copy machinery is complete** across slices 1–3b; only **angel_of_indemnity** (Encore keyword) and **inspired_skypainter** (prepare/DFC) remain, each blocked on an unrelated unlanded subsystem, not on further copy work. NOT LANDED (2 of 7 cards still blocked).

**Progress (2026-07-15) — Encore keyword landed, angel_of_indemnity faithful.** New rules-keyword `CardDef::encore: Option<&'static Cost>` (the encore **mana** cost; `[encore]` TOML table, leaked to `'static` like `suspend`'s cost, `CardDef: Copy` preserved) plus a graveyard special-action mirroring suspend: `Intent::Encore` / `MeaningfulAction::Encore`, `encore_listable` (owner's graveyard, sorcery timing CR 702.140b, affordable), offered in `meaningful_actions`' graveyard scan; `Game::encore` (`cast.rs`) settles the encore mana cost (rejects before any exile if unpayable), `Event::MovedToExile`s the card (CR 702.140a), then **for each opponent** mints a token copy of the card's printed `def` under the encoring player with `Event::MustAttackDeclared` (CR 702.140c), an until-EOT `Event::TempBoost { Keyword::Haste }`, and a `Step::End` `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled { Effect::SacrificeObject }` — all pre-existing events (no new schema `Event`; `Intent::Encore` is the only wire-mirror added). Token count runs through `token_count_after_replacements` (CR 614). **angel_of_indemnity is now faithful** (`approximates` deleted). The per-opponent must-attack haste-copy body is the reusable substrate for **myriad** (muddle_the_ever_changing, #74/#88 — same shape; a `// ponytail:` on `Game::encore` notes it). #127's **only remaining card is inspired_skypainter** (blocked on prepare/DFC, an unrelated unlanded subsystem). NOT LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15) — brudiclad's token-haste anthem residual closed.** `Effect::AnthemStatic` gained a `tokens_only: bool` axis (`#[serde(default)]`, TOML `tokens_only`), enforced at the single anthem choke `Game::matching_anthems` (`crates/engine/src/characteristics.rs`) via `if tokens_only && !self.as_permanent(candidate).is_some_and(|p| p.token) { continue; }`. brudiclad_telchor_engineer's first ability ("Creature tokens you control have haste") is now authored as a `timing = "static"` `anthem_static` ability (`tokens_only = true`, `keywords = ["haste"]`); its `approximates` and stale `# ponytail:` header (which claimed `AnthemStatic` was P/T-only — it already granted keywords, only the token-scoping axis was missing) are both deleted. **brudiclad_telchor_engineer is now fully faithful.** #127 overall still NOT LANDED — angel_of_indemnity (Encore) and inspired_skypainter (DFC/prepare) remain blocked on unrelated unlanded subsystems, unrelated to this anthem axis.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — inspired_skypainter faithful; #127 now LANDED (all 7 cards).** Pure card authoring onto already-landed machinery — **no engine change**. Its stale `approximates`/`# ponytail:` header (claiming "no DFC/prepare") predated #77 `prepare-back-face-authoring` and #46's `CardDef::back`/`Intent::CastPrepared` machinery. Front face: the printed "When this creature enters and whenever one or more creature tokens you control deal combat damage to a player, this creature becomes prepared" authored as two `[[abilities]]` (`timing = "etb"` and `timing = "deals_combat_damage_to_player"` `who = "your_tokens"`), each a single `become_prepared` effect — each event independently makes the permanent prepared, idempotently. Back face Maestro's Gift (`[back]` `{3}{U}{R}` sorcery) is a single `create_token_copy` `target = { permanent = { types = "creature", controller = "you" } }` with `haste = true` — the `haste` flag grants Haste via an until-EOT `TempBoost`, which is *exactly* "gains haste until end of turn," so no residual (unlike the sacrifice/exile-paired consumers whose printed haste is permanent). This was the finishing slice — **the become-a-copy/copy machinery of slices 1–3b and the Encore/anthem work were already complete; inspired_skypainter needed only prepare-DFC authoring, which is what makes #127 LANDED.** Tests in `crates/engine/tests/game.rs`: `inspired_skypainter_becomes_prepared_on_etb`, `inspired_skypainter_becomes_prepared_when_your_token_deals_combat_damage`, `inspired_skypainter_maestros_gift_copies_target_creature_with_haste`.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — hofri_ghostforge's slice-1 `leaves_returns_exiled` deferral now wired; #127's cards are now all *fully* faithful (residual closure, still LANDED).** Slice 1's note ("needs a per-object granted leaves trigger baking the exiled id") is closed. At mint (`ExileDeadCreatureCreateCopyWithSubtype`'s resolve arm), when `leaves_returns_exiled` is set, a new `Event::TokenGrantedReturnExiledOnLeave { token, exiled }` links the minted token to its specific exiled card in a new `Game::exile_links.token_leaves_returns_exiled: Vec<(ObjectId, ObjectId)>`. When that token leaves the battlefield (`Event::TokenCeasedToExist`), the new `Game::queue_token_return_exiled_trigger` reads the link and synthesizes a real, unauthored `Trigger::ThisPermanentLeavesBattlefield` ability directly onto `pending_trigger_groups` — the same synthesis idiom `queue_myriad_triggers`/`queue_prowess_triggers` use for a printed-def-less ability — carrying the new engine-internal `Effect::ReturnExiledCardToOwnersGraveyard { exiled }` payload (guard-returns if `exiled` is no longer in `Zone::Exile`). This is a real CR 603 triggered ability that goes on the stack, not an SBA-style departure sweep (unlike the illusion/O-Ring precedents) — matching `ThisPermanentLeavesBattlefield`'s own placement path exactly, per the brief's steer. **Bug found and fixed in the same change:** the payoff must NOT reuse `Event::MovedToGraveyard` — doing so falsely re-fires `Trigger::Dies`/creature-you-control-dies watchers (including Hofri's own) off a card that never died (CR 700.4 "died" requires *from the battlefield*; this card arrives from exile), which was observed to mint a runaway second Spirit token in testing. Fixed with a dedicated `Event::ReturnedExiledCardToGraveyard { card, from }` that skips all "died" bookkeeping — mirrors `Event::Milled`'s same reasoning for a library-to-graveyard arrival. hofri_ghostforge's `approximates` and the rider `# ponytail:` line are both deleted — **the card is now fully faithful, no residual**. Tests in `crates/engine/tests/game.rs`: `hofri_ghostforge_spirit_copy_returns_exiled_card_when_token_leaves`, `hofri_ghostforge_no_return_if_exiled_card_already_moved`, `hofri_ghostforge_multiple_deaths_each_token_returns_its_own_card`.

### 128. `replacement-doubling` — 3 cards, XL — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
General CR 614 replacement effects watching *other* objects' events — the counter_replacement/finality precedent grown into a would-event → modified-event bus: "twice that many tokens" (Doubling Season's token half; its counter half rides the existing counter pipeline), "if you would gain life, gain that much plus 1" (Pest Rescuer), "double the value of X" on your permanent X-spells (Unbound Flourishing — a cast-event modification). *Staged plan:* (1) a replacement hook at the token-creation choke point mirroring `counters_after_replacements` (Doubling Season's tokens — one site, one card); (2) the life-gain choke point (Pest Rescuer); (3) the cast-context X modification (Unbound Flourishing); (4) only then consider unifying the sites behind a shared bus — three named choke points may simply be enough.
*Cards:* doubling_season, pest_rescuer, unbound_flourishing
**Progress (2026-07-14) — slice 1 of 4 (token choke):** `Effect::TokenReplacement { times: i32 }` (TOML `token_replacement`, `times` defaulting to the multiplicative identity via the shared `de::one`) is the token-side twin of `counter_replacement` — a static that never resolves off the stack. `Game::token_count_after_replacements(recipient, base)` mirrors `counters_after_replacements`: `base == 0` → 0, else fold `product *= times` over every `Object::Permanent` the `recipient` owns carrying a `Static` + `TokenReplacement` ability, returning `base * product` (pure multiply, keyed on the token recipient — CR "under your control"). Wired at the three token-mint choke sites in `effects.rs` (`CreateToken` per-batch against each batch's own recipient, `CreateTreasure`, `CreateTokenCopy`). `doubling_season` **fully faithful** — both oracle sentences scripted (`token_replacement` + `counter_replacement`), `approximates` + token-drop ponytail header deleted. Slices **2 (Pest Rescuer life-gain choke), 3 (Unbound Flourishing cast-X modification), 4 (unify behind a shared would-event bus)** remain; NOT LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-14) — slice 2 of 4 (life-gain choke):** `Effect::LifeGainReplacement { plus: i32 }` (TOML `life_gain_replacement`, `plus` defaulting to the additive identity `0` via `#[serde(default)]`) is the life-gain twin of `token_replacement` — a static that never resolves off the stack. `Game::life_gain_after_replacements(recipient, base)` mirrors `token_count_after_replacements`: `base <= 0` → `base` (gaining 0 is not "gaining life"), else fold `total += plus` over every `Object::Permanent` whose **controller** is `recipient` carrying a `Static` + `LifeGainReplacement` ability, returning `base + total` (pure addend, additive across statics, keyed on the life-gaining player — CR "you gain life"). Wired at every life-*gain* choke: `Effect::GainLife` (controller), `Effect::GainLifeTargetController` (target's controller), the drain gain-halves (`DrainTarget`, `EachOpponentDrain`, `AttackerLosesLifeYouGain`), lifelink combat (`combat.rs::gain_lifelink` — source's controller), and the Serra Paragon exile-death rider (`apply.rs`). Life loss / life payment / damage-as-loss / `set_life` untouched. `pest_rescuer` now scripts sentence 2 (`life_gain_replacement`, `plus = 1`); its `approximates` trimmed to only the pre-existing each-upkeep residual (`timing = "upkeep"` fires on the controller's upkeep only, not literally each player's — a separate `each_upkeep`-timing gap, out of this slice). Slices **3 (Unbound Flourishing cast-X modification), 4 (unify behind a shared would-event bus)** remain; NOT LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-14) — slice 3 of 4 (cast-X choke):** `Effect::CastXReplacement { times: i32 }` (TOML `cast_x_replacement`, `times` defaulting to the multiplicative identity via the shared `de::one`) is the cast-context twin of `token_replacement` — a static that never resolves off the stack. `Game::cast_x_after_replacements(caster, def, base)` mirrors `token_count_after_replacements`: `base == 0` → 0, `def.cost.x == 0` → `base` (not an X-spell), a **non-permanent** spell (`CardKind::Spell`/`Land`) → `base` (CR 107.3 — the doubling is permanent-spells only; Unbound's instant/sorcery half is the unrelated copy ability), else fold `product *= times` over every `Object::Permanent` whose **controller** is `caster` carrying a `Static` + `CastXReplacement` ability, returning `base * product` (pure multiply, multiplicative across statics, keyed on the caster — CR "you cast"). Wired at the single cast choke: `apply.rs`'s `Event::SpellCast` arm wraps the `x` that goes into the constructed `Spell` (after cost payment in `Game::cast` — the CR ordering, so the doubled value flows to `Permanent::entered_with_x`, enters-with-X counters, and every `Amount::X` reader, while the cost is untouched). No `AdventureSpellCast`/other choke doubled. `unbound_flourishing` sentence 1 now faithful (`cast_x_replacement`, `times = 2`); its `approximates` trimmed to only the second ability's ability-copy residual ("or activate an ability … copy that ability" — no ability-copy mechanic in the pool; ability-copy ponytail header kept). Slice **4 (unify the three named choke points — token/life-gain/cast-X — behind a shared would-event bus)** remains; NOT LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — pest_rescuer fully faithful.** The each-upkeep residual left open by slice 2 is closed: its first ability's `timing` flipped `"upkeep"` → `"each_upkeep"` (the existing `Trigger::EachUpkeep`, already used by tendershoot_dryad/ophiomancer — no new engine surface), matching "At the beginning of each upkeep." Both sentences (each-upkeep Pest token + life-gain-plus-1 replacement from slice 2) now modeled; `approximates` deleted. #128 slice 4 still remains; NOT LANDED (overall).
**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 4 of 4 (close-out), #128 now LANDED.** All three cards (doubling_season, pest_rescuer, unbound_flourishing) are fully faithful. The unify-behind-a-shared-would-event-bus option is **declined** — pure indirection with no third caller and no card consumer (YAGNI). The three named choke points (`token_count_after_replacements` owner-scoped multiply, `life_gain_after_replacements` controller-scoped add, `cast_x_after_replacements` controller-scoped multiply with permanent-spell/`{X}` guards) are **kept as distinct sites**. The small shared-scan helper was also evaluated and **declined, leaving the loops explicit**: the three sites genuinely diverge on owner-vs-controller scoping, multiply-over-`times` vs add-over-`plus`, and the cast-X guards; a helper would need an owner-vs-controller flag (a boolean-param wart at each call site) while each caller still keeps its own fold and effect-match — it would obscure more than the ~6 lines of scan boilerplate it saves. Each function reads top-to-bottom with its own CR citation. No code moved; behavior unchanged, so no new test (covered by the existing doubling_season / pest_rescuer / unbound_flourishing tests in `game.rs`).

### 129. `trigger-doubling` — 2 cards, XL — **LANDED (2026-07-14)**
A trigger-placement replacement layer: "abilities of Shamans/Wizards you control trigger an additional time" (Harmonic Prodigy), "if a magecraft-style event causes a triggered ability of a permanent you control to trigger, it triggers an additional time" (Veyran). *Staged plan:* (1) a hook at `place_pending_triggers` that scans for doubling statics and re-places matching `TriggerGroup`s (both cards are this one slice); (2) the filter axes (subtype-scoped, event-kind-scoped) as data on the static. Bounded: placement is already a single choke point, which is why this is XL-with-a-small-core rather than hopeless.
*Cards:* harmonic_prodigy, veyran_voice_of_duality
**Landed:** `Effect::TriggerDoublingStatic { source_subtypes: &'static [&'static str], source_other: bool, caused_by_instant_or_sorcery_cast: bool }` — a `timing = "static"` ability read only at trigger placement (never resolves off the stack, the `AnthemStatic` posture). New `Game::double_pending_triggers` runs at the top of `place_pending_triggers` (CR 603.3c): for each pending `TriggerGroup`, it counts on-board doublers whose filter matches (`matching_trigger_doublers`) and appends that many identical copies, so the ability triggers one additional time per doubler (two doublers → three instances, stacking additively). A new `TriggerGroup::expanded` flag makes it idempotent — a copy is minted `expanded`, and every considered group is marked `expanded`, so a re-entrant placement pass (a pending choice answered mid-batch re-runs the whole post-intent pipeline) never re-doubles. Filter axes: `source_subtypes` gates on the triggering ability's SOURCE permanent's subtypes (Harmonic's Shaman/Wizard), `source_other` excludes the doubler's own source (CR "another" — Harmonic's own prowess isn't doubled), `caused_by_instant_or_sorcery_cast` requires a `SpellCast`/`SpellCopied` of an instant/sorcery by the doubler's controller in the same event batch (Veyran's magecraft cause — so her own magecraft pump doubles). Non-permanent sources (a spell's own cast trigger, a removed object) never match. Both cards fully faithful: harmonic_prodigy `approximates` + trigger-interception ponytail deleted; veyran_voice_of_duality trimmed to its Magecraft-pump-target residual only (the pump targets a creature you control, no fixed self-target). **ponytail:** "causes … to trigger" is approximated as "the same event batch holds the controller's instant/sorcery cast-or-copy" — the engine has no per-trigger causal link; exact for the pool (a magecraft trigger is always placed in the batch of its cause). Reusable for any future trigger-doubler (`Effect::TriggerDoublingStatic`, the `place_pending_triggers` hook, `TriggerGroup::expanded`).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** veyran_voice_of_duality's residual (the magecraft pump wrote `target = "creature_you_control"` and paused for a target) is closed — the pump is now `target = "this"`, resolved with no pause via the existing `TargetSpec::ThisPermanent` fixed-reference path in `Game::place_targeted_ability` (no engine change). `approximates` deleted; veyran is now fully faithful.

### 130. `damage-prevention` — 1 card, XL — **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
A damage-prevention shield pipeline: "prevent all combat damage this turn", with the prevented amount observable as an `Amount` (Inkshield's "create X Inklings where X = damage prevented"). *Staged plan:* (1) a prevention-shield record consulted at the two damage choke points (`damage_player`/`damage_creature`), all-combat-damage-this-turn scope only; (2) the prevented-total tally exposed to `resolve_amount`; (3) generalize scope (per-source, N-damage shields) only when a card needs it. One card today, but it's the front door to the whole prevention family — keep the first slice deliberately narrow.
*Cards:* inkshield
**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 1 landed, inkshield fully faithful (NOT LANDED overall; tajic remains).** A this-turn, per-player combat-damage prevention shield: `CombatExtras::combat_damage_prevention_shields: Vec<(PlayerId, CardDef)>` (runtime orchestration state on `Game`, kept off `Copy` `CardDef` — the token payload rides by value since `CardDef: Copy`), armed by a new no-target `Effect::PreventCombatDamageToYouCreatingTokens { token }` (TOML `prevent_combat_damage_to_you_creating_tokens` with an inline `[…token]` profile, parsed via the shared `token_profile` deserializer — resolves via the `&mut self` `Game::run` path, like the delayed combat-damage watches). Consulted at the combat-damage-to-a-**player** choke `Game::damage_player` (guard-return, before the life loss): a shielded player takes no combat damage — no `LifeChanged`, no commander-damage tally, no lifelink (CR 702.15e, no damage dealt) — and instead mints one 2/1 W/B flying Inkling per point prevented via `Event::TokenCreated` (routed through `token_count_after_replacements`, so Doubling Season doubles), replacing the loss with a public `Event::CombatDamagePrevented { player, amount }` (schema-mirrored). "this turn" = "until the next untap" (`combat_extras` cleared at `Step::Untap`, the `must_attack`/`pending_next_cast` idiom — behavior-exact for a combat-only shield). **Timing decision:** inkshield is cast *before* combat damage as a selective fog; its tokens are created *when the shield prevents damage*, not at spell resolution (at resolution zero damage has been prevented). So the backlog's slice-2 sketch (prevented-total exposed to `resolve_amount`, read by a `create_token count = …`) is **unfaithful for inkshield** — a `create_token` at spell resolution runs before any combat damage. The token mint is therefore **coupled to the prevention event**; the pure-tally `Amount::CombatDamagePreventedThisTurn` route is deferred (no pool card reads a prevented total *after* combat). **Residual — tajic (`Tajic, Legion's Edge`) remains #130's sole approximated consumer, deferred to slice 3:** it prevents *noncombat* damage to *other creatures you control* as a *permanent* static — a different choke (`deal_creature_damage`), a different scope, and a durationless shield, i.e. the scope generalization (per-source / to-creatures / noncombat / N-point). tajic's `approximates` left untouched. Not marked LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15) — slice 3 landed, tajic fully faithful; #130 now LANDED (inkshield + tajic both faithful, no other consumer).** A durationless permanent static, disjoint from inkshield's turn-scoped per-player combat-to-a-player shield: new fieldless `Effect::PreventNoncombatDamageToOtherCreaturesYouControl` (TOML `prevent_noncombat_damage_to_other_creatures_you_control`, authored `timing = "static"` — never resolved off the stack, the `AnthemStatic` posture; `CardDef`/`Effect` stay `Copy`). Predicate `Game::noncombat_damage_prevented_to_creature(target)` (beside `matching_anthems` in characteristics.rs) scans the battlefield: true iff some permanent carries that static, is controlled by `target`'s controller, and is a *different* object (CR "**other** creatures you control"). Wired at every **noncombat** creature-damage choke, and only those: `deal_creature_damage` (combat.rs) gained a `combat: bool` parameter — `damage_creature` passes `true` (combat, unprevented), `fight` passes `false` (fight damage is noncombat, CR 701.12); the guard-return prevention check sits after the protection guard so a prevented hit produces **no** `DamageMarked` (no deathtouch, no lifelink — CR 615, nothing happens). The three effect-damage sites (all inherently noncombat) got the predicate beside their existing `damage_prevented_by_protection` check: `DealDamage` single-object arm, `DamageEachCreature` mass filter, `DealDamageToEnteringPermanent`. No new `Event`, no schema change (a prevented hit is a silent absence — `// ponytail:` at the choke; add an `Event::DamagePrevented` mirroring inkshield's `Event::CombatDamagePrevented` only when a card must observe it). Combat damage, damage to the source itself, and opponents' creatures are all untouched. Reusable primitive for any future noncombat-damage-prevention static: `Effect::PreventNoncombatDamageToOtherCreaturesYouControl` + `Game::noncombat_damage_prevented_to_creature` + the `combat` flag on `deal_creature_damage`. tajic (`Tajic, Legion's Edge`) fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). Tests in `crates/engine/tests/game.rs`: `tajic_prevents_noncombat_damage_to_your_other_creatures`, `tajic_does_not_prevent_damage_to_itself`, `tajic_does_not_prevent_combat_damage`, `tajic_does_not_prevent_damage_to_opponents_creatures`, `tajic_prevents_fight_damage_to_your_creature`.

---

## Tier 4 — mechanic packages (multi-card keywords)

### 131. `adventure` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Adventure split cards: cast the instant/sorcery half from hand, exile "on an adventure" on resolve, then cast the creature from exile later. Rides the landed prepare back-face precedent (`CardDef::back`) plus a from-exile cast permission keyed to the adventure state (#86's permission shape) — Brazen Borrower's Petty Theft, Elusive Otter's Grove's Bounty.
*Cards:* brazen_borrower, elusive_otter
**Landed:** `CardDef::adventure: Option<&'static CardDef>` (an inline `[adventure]` card table — its own `cost`/`kind` (instant/sorcery)/`[[adventure.abilities]]` — parsed and leaked to `'static` exactly like `[back]`; the creature front face is the card's own top-level fields). `Intent::CastAdventure { player, source, target, x }` → `Game::cast_adventure` mirrors `cast_prepared` but the source is a **hand** card and its adventure (not back) face is cast: it pays the adventure face's cost, validates that face's targets (single or multi), and emits `Event::AdventureSpellCast`, which puts the card on the stack as a spell whose `def` is the adventure face (feeding `spells_cast_this_turn`/instant-or-sorcery counters like a normal cast) and records the creature front face in `PlayPermissions::adventure_fronts` (a side `Vec<(spell, CardDef)>` — kept off the `Copy` `Spell` struct, where an inline `CardDef` would double its size and flag `Object` as a `large_enum_variant`). On resolution, `finish_instant_sorcery_resolution` sees the recorded front and emits `Event::ExiledOnAdventure` (instead of the graveyard move): it restores the **creature** front face to exile and pushes an open-ended `PlayPermissions::on_adventure` cast permission (consulted by `may_play_from_exile`, so `playable_zone` returns `Zone::Exile` and the creature casts from exile at its normal `[cost]` via an ordinary `Intent::Cast` — no turn limit; the entry is consumed when the card is cast from exile). New `Intent::CastAdventure` + `Event::AdventureSpellCast`/`ExiledOnAdventure` mirrored in `crates/schema` (all public — the stack/exile are visible). brazen_borrower is fully faithful (`approximates` + adventure ponytail header deleted).
**Still blocked:** elusive_otter's adventure *flow* is faithful, but Grove's Bounty's "distribute X +1/+1 counters among any number of target creatures" keeps a trimmed `approximates` — modeled as X counters on **one** target creature you control, since `put_counters` puts a fixed count per target with **no divided mode** (only `deal_damage` has `divided`). Separate `put_counters.divided` gap (cf. #73/#96), not an adventure gap.

### 132. `cascade` — 2 cards, L
Cascade (CR 702.85): on cast, exile from the top until a nonland card with lesser MV, may cast it free, rest to bottom in a random order — composes the landed `LookAtTop`/exile piles + #86's free-cast permission + #116's injected RNG into a keyword field on `Cost`/`CardDef`. Throes of Chaos and Volcanic Torrent.
*Cards:* throes_of_chaos, volcanic_torrent

**LANDED (2026-07-12).** `CardDef::cascade: bool` (`cascade = true` in TOML) is a rules-keyword, not a `[[abilities]]` block: at the cast choke (`Event::SpellCast`), a `cascade = true` spell fabricates a synthetic single-ability `TriggerGroup` carrying `Effect::Cascade { mana_value }` (baked from `def.mana_value()` at placement — last-known info, CR 702.85b — no `{X}`-cost cascade card exists so this is exact), which rides the normal APNAP placement path onto the stack above the cascading spell (a real, respondable stack object resolving first, CR 702.85e), exactly as `fire_delayed_triggers` fabricates its groups. `Effect::Cascade` resolves via `Game::begin_cascade` (the `&mut self` path, like `RevealUntil`): reveal-until the first nonland of strictly lesser mana value (or library-empty, CR 702.85c), exiling each face-up via the reused `Event::ExiledFromLibraryToChooseCastFree` (public). A hit reuses the dig's #86 machinery wholesale — pause on `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledDigToCastFree` with the single hit as the only candidate, granting `may_cast_from_exile_free` on accept — and the rest bottom in random order via `Game::bottom_exiled_dig`, now a real Fisher-Yates shuffle on the injected `next_u64` splitmix PRNG (#116), which also upgrades Herald of Amity's dig ("in a random order") from its old deterministic stand-in. `cast_timing_ok` gained a free-cast-from-exile timing bypass (CR 601.3e) so the hit is castable with the cascading spell still on the stack. Landed (`approximates` deleted): Throes of Chaos (cascade + already-landed retrace/discard-land body) and Volcanic Torrent (cascade + already-landed `damage_each_creature` body). Reusable primitives (`Effect::Cascade`, `CardDef::cascade`) available for any future cascade card. Still blocked (pre-existing, pool-wide, not cascade-specific): Volcanic Torrent still drops the planeswalker half of "each creature and planeswalker" — no planeswalker permanent type exists (ponytail note in the TOML, mirrors #91); behaviorally complete against the current pool. Follow-ups: an `{X}`-cost cascade card would need `mana_value` widened to an `Amount` reading the on-stack `{X}` (CR 202.3b/702.85b), none in the pool; and a pre-existing retrace bug (from the retrace increment, not this wave) makes `cast_additional_cost_gate` demand a land discard even when Throes of Chaos is cast from hand — retrace's discard-a-land should gate the graveyard cast only (CR 702.83a).

### 133. `class-levels` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-14)**
Class enchantments: pay-to-level sorcery-speed activated abilities, a level status on the permanent, and level-gated abilities/statics — Advanced Reconstruction (level 3's cast-zone cost reducer rides #85) and Intermediate Chirography (level 2 needs #81's first-life-loss flag; level 3 needs "a modified creature died this turn" tracking). Sketch: a level counter + per-ability min-level gates in the activation/trigger scans.
*Cards:* advanced_reconstruction, intermediate_chirography
**Landed:** `Permanent::level: u8` (defaults 1 at every construction site — CR 717.4) and `Ability::min_level: u8` (`#[serde(default)]` 0). The level gate is wired at every ability scan: trigger placement (`Game::queue_trigger_group` skips `min_level > source.level`), the statics (`cost_reduction`, `matching_anthems`), and the activation gate (`ability_activation_gate`). New `Effect::LevelUp { level }` on a `sorcery_speed = true` activated ability sets the level via `Event::LeveledUp`; the activation gate offers it only while `source.level == level - 1` (CR 717.2 — each level gained exactly once, superseding `min_level`). Advanced Reconstruction fully faithful (`approximates` deleted; base upkeep-for-first-main-phase ponytail kept): level 2 = `Trigger::CardsLeaveYourGraveyard` → `each_opponent_loses_life`, level 3 = a `min_level = 3` `reduce_spell_cost` static reading the new `SpellFilter::CastFromNonHandZone` (the cast-from zone is threaded into `spell_matches_filter`/`cost_reduction`; #85's deferred cast-zone predicate). Intermediate Chirography levels 1–3 faithful: ETB Inkling + level-2 `Trigger::YouLoseLifeFirstTimeEachTurn` (new, off `Player::life_losses_this_turn`, fires only on the turn's first life *decrease*, CR 118.9/119.3) → `put_counters` on target creature you control; level-3 `{2}{B}: Level 3` + a `min_level = 3` `each_end_step` Inkling gated on the new `Condition::ModifiedCreatureDiedThisTurn` (see "Still blocked" below for how that flag is tracked). `Effect::LevelUp` labeled; `Event::LeveledUp` schema-mirrored (public). Reusable primitives for any future Class / life-loss / cast-zone / morbid-of-modified card: `Permanent::level`, `Ability::min_level`, `Effect::LevelUp`, `Trigger::YouLoseLifeFirstTimeEachTurn`, `SpellFilter::CastFromNonHandZone`, `Condition::ModifiedCreatureDiedThisTurn`.
**Still blocked:** none — Intermediate Chirography's level 3 residual closed (2026-07-14): new `Player::modified_creature_died_this_turn` (turn-scoped flag, set at the death choke — `Event::MovedToGraveyard`/`Event::TokenCeasedToExist` in `apply.rs` — by last-known information, read before the dying object's attachments/counters are torn down; reset at Untap) backs a new `Condition::ModifiedCreatureDiedThisTurn` (TOML `"modified_creature_died_this_turn"`). Level 3 (`{2}{B}: Level 3` + the `min_level = 3` `each_end_step` Inkling ability) is authored; both scope cards (advanced_reconstruction, intermediate_chirography) are now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).

### 134. `devour` — 2 cards, L — **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Devour N (CR 702.82): an as-enters sacrifice-any-number choice — a new ETB-replacement choice surface — with the creature entering with that many counters (× N). Mycoloth and Ribtruss Roaster; Ribtruss's counter-scaled token count is already expressible (`CreateToken.count` takes `PerCounterOnSource`), so devour is its real residual.
*Cards:* mycoloth, ribtruss_roaster
**Landed:** `CardDef::devour: Option<u32>` (a rules-keyword, `devour = N` in TOML — no `[[abilities]]`). In `resolve_spell`'s creature-enter path, right after `PermanentEntered`, `Game::begin_devour` pauses on a new `PendingChoice::Devour { player, source, multiplier, options }` (options = the *other* creatures the controller controls — the entering source isn't offered) so the controller may sacrifice any subset; `Game::answer_devour` (dispatched off the reused `Intent::ChooseSacrifices` wire shape) sacrifices them and places `multiplier × count` +1/+1 counters through `counters_after_replacements` (CR 614 doublers apply). Declining (empty selection) is legal → 0 counters; no other creature to give up → no pause. Ribtruss's end-step Pest generator authored (`create_token count = "per_counter_on_source"`, Pest token carrying the `blight_mound` `dies` → `gain_life` sub-ability). Both mycoloth and ribtruss_roaster fully faithful (`approximates` + devour header prose deleted). New `PendingChoiceView::Devour` mirrored in schema (candidates public). ponytail: modeled as an as-enters *step* (counters placed after the entry), not a true CR 614.13 replacement — not observable for this pool (both cards read their counters at a later upkeep/end step); upgrade to a real replacement hook when a devour card fields an ETB that reads its own devour counters.
**Still blocked:** none — both scope cards lost their `approximates` note; the as-enters-step model is a non-observable residual (no pool devour card reads its own counters during its ETB), not a card-level gap.

---

## Per-card exotics

Truly unique single-card gaps — real increments under the all-cards posture, one line each; schedule each when its card matters to a table. None blocks anything else.

- **annihilator** (eldrazi_conscription) — attack trigger forcing the *defending* player to sacrifice N; the `SacrificeEdict` choice fired at the defender read from `TriggerContext.attack`. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `Effect::DefendingPlayerSacrifices { count }` reuses `Game::begin_choose_own_sacrifices`/`PendingChoice::ChooseOwnSacrifices` (the "N of your own permanents, mandatory" shape `sacrifice_own` already uses) with the defender (read from `TriggerContext.attack.1`, baked in by `contextualize_effect` at trigger placement) standing in for the ability's controller and an unrestricted `PermanentFilter` (CR 701.16a: any permanent, not just creatures). No new `PendingChoice`/schema surface needed.
- **keyword-strip** (arcane_lighthouse) — "creatures your opponents control lose hexproof and shroud until end of turn and can't have hexproof or shroud": a negative entry in the until-EOT keyword records consulted by `effective_keywords`/`untargetable_by` — the follow-up v1 #62 named. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `Permanent::temp_lost_keywords: &'static [Keyword]` — the negative twin of `temp_keywords` — filtered out of the fully-unioned set at the end of `Game::compute_effective_keywords_uncached` (so "can't have" is free: a keyword granted by any source, including one applied after the strip lands this turn, is filtered right back out the same recompute) and cleared alongside `temp_keywords` at `Event::TempBoostsEnded`/cleanup. New `Effect::StripKeywordsFromOpponentsCreatures { keywords }` (mass, no target — mirrors `WeakenEachCreature`'s `controller_of(id) != controller` opponents scan) resolves to one `Event::KeywordsStripped` per opponent-controlled creature, unioned onto `temp_lost_keywords` (same union-not-clobber leak `TempBoost` already uses). arcane_lighthouse is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted): its `{T}: Add {C}` stays the `produces = "colorless"` land sugar; the `{1}, {T}` strip is a real activated ability (`ability_index = 0` in its `abilities` array, since `produces` isn't itself indexed there).
- **flash-permission-static** (alchemists_refuge) — "you may cast spells as though they had flash" (filtered): a static consulted by `Game::cast`'s sorcery-speed gate, mirroring `sorcery_speed = true` in reverse. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** The real card is unfiltered ("cast spells this turn," not a subset) and turn-scoped, not a passive static — modeled as `Player::flash_permission_this_turn`, a per-player turn flag set by a new fieldless `Effect::GrantFlashThisTurn`/`Event::FlashPermissionGranted` and cleared at the next Untap step alongside the other per-turn flags. `Game::cast_timing_ok` treats a permission-holding player's casts as instant-speed. alchemists_refuge is now fully faithful: `{T}: Add {C}` stays the `produces = "colorless"` land sugar; `{G}{U}, {T}: grant flash` is a real activated ability (`ability_index = 0`).
- **wheel-effect** (naktamun_lorespinner) — "each player discards their hand, then draws seven": mass discard-and-redraw; the discard event + per-player loop exist. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `Effect::EachPlayerDiscardsHandThenDraws { count }` — every living player, in APNAP order, discards their whole hand via the existing `discard_ids` zone-move (widened to `pub(crate)`, no choice — the entire hand goes, not a chosen subset) then draws `count` (a §6 `Amount`) via the existing `draw_events`. New `Condition::AnyPlayerHandSizeAtMost { at_most }` (an existential over every seated player, not just the controller) backs naktamun_lorespinner's front-face upkeep trigger, gating the already-landed `become_prepared`/prepare-DFC machinery (#71's template). naktamun_lorespinner is now fully faithful (`approximates` and its stale header prose deleted): front is `timing = "upkeep"` + `[abilities.condition] type = "any_player_hand_size_at_most"`; back face is Wheel of Fortune (`each_player_discards_hand_then_draws`, `count = 7`). ponytail: CR-simultaneous "each player discards, then each draws" is composed as per-player discard-then-draw sequential in APNAP order — same posture as defacing_duskmage's "each player loses 2 life" sequential note. Both primitives are reusable: the wheel effect for other "each player discards and redraws" cards, the hand-size condition for other hellbent/hand-size gates.
- **chosen-creature-type** (patchwork_banner) — "as this enters, choose a creature type", stored on the permanent, read by the subtype anthem. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `Permanent::chosen_subtype: Option<&'static str>` plus `Effect::ChooseCreatureType` (an ETB effect that pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseCreatureType` over `CREATURE_TYPES`, the pool's known creature types — answered by `Intent::ChooseCreatureType`, mirroring `ChooseManaColor`'s resolve-time single-choice-from-a-fixed-set shape). `Effect::AnthemStatic` gains a `chosen_subtype: bool` axis, ANDed against the source's own `chosen_subtype` in `matching_anthems` (no choice made yet matches nothing).
- **choose-a-color** (flickering_ward) — as-enters color choice feeding a dynamic `ProtectionFrom(chosen)` grant; also wire its "{W}: return this Aura to hand" via the landed `ReturnThisToHand`. L. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** `Permanent::chosen_color: Option<Color>` plus a fieldless `Effect::ChooseColor` (an ETB effect that pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseColor` over the fixed five colors — answered by `Intent::ChooseColor`, mirroring `ChooseCreatureType`/`ChooseManaColor`'s resolve-time single-choice-from-a-fixed-set shape; stored via a new public `Event::ColorChosen`, cache-invalidating the enchanted host the way `CreatureTypeChosen` invalidates the chooser's board). The dynamic protection grant is a new `grant_to_attached` axis `protection_from_chosen_color: bool`: read live in `compute_effective_keywords_uncached` off each attached Aura's own `chosen_color`, yielding `Keyword::ProtectionFrom(Color(chosen))` (nothing until a color is chosen) — a card-specific dynamic-scope axis, not a general grant-a-runtime-keyword surface. The "{W}: return this Aura to hand" half is pure authoring on the landed `Effect::ReturnThisToHand`. flickering_ward is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). ponytail: "This effect doesn't remove this Aura" (CR 702.16e) is a non-issue — the Aura-legality SBA (CR 704.5m/n) only detaches from a non-creature/absent host, never for a can't-be-enchanted quality. Both `Effect::ChooseColor` + `Permanent::chosen_color` are reusable for any future "as ~ enters, choose a color" card.
- **play-from-graveyard-permission** (serra_paragon) — continuous "you may play lands / cast permanent spells MV≤3 from your graveyard, once each per turn" checked in `playable_zone`, plus the exile-and-gain-2 leave rider. L. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** New fieldless static `Effect::PlayFromGraveyardOncePerTurn` (a battlefield marker read by `Game::grants_graveyard_recursion`, the `has_no_max_hand_size` scan pattern). `playable_zone`'s `Zone::Graveyard` arm widens alongside flashback/escape/retrace via `serra_graveyard_play_allowed` (controller grants the permission, `Player::graveyard_play_used_this_turn` not yet spent, and the card is a land or a nonland/non-instant-sorcery permanent card with MV≤3); `play_land` accepts `Zone::Graveyard` too. The once-per-turn budget is a per-player flag set at the `SpellCast`/`LandPlayed` apply choke — a graveyard play by neither flashback nor escape (nor a land-play, which no other effect grants) is derivably the Serra permission, so no new event is needed — and reset at Untap like the other per-turn flags. The granted leave rider is a `Spell::serra_recursion`/`Permanent::serra_recursion` tag copied onto the entering permanent (`PermanentEntered`/`LandPlayed`), redirected to exile at the `graveyard_or_command` death choke (the finality-counter pattern), and paid its +2 life by draining a `Game::pending_serra_lifegain` queue (captured at the `MovedToExile` choke) into `Event::LifeChanged` from the SBA fixpoint sweep (the `check_leaves_battlefield_illusions` rules-driven-follow-up pattern). serra_paragon is now fully faithful (`approximates` + body-only header deleted). ponytail: the rider is a rules-driven zone redirect, not the printed stack trigger — it never uses the stack / can't be responded to, and the permanent skips the graveyard, so its own Dies triggers and `permanents_died_this_turn` don't fire; no pool card observes that gap (same posture as `finality_counter`).
- **aura-token-attached** (scriv_the_obligator) — create a predefined Aura *token* carrying a triggered ability, entering attached to a chosen creature; token-with-abilities profiles landed, the Aura-kind + attach-on-creation target is new. L. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** A token profile may now be `CardKind::Aura` (`[…token.kind] type = "aura"`, its own `enchant = { … }` restriction + `[[…token.abilities]]`) — the `de::token_profile` `Full(CardDef)` form already accepted any kind, so no deserializer change. New `Effect::AttachMintedAuraToTarget { target }` is the mirror of the landed `attach_self_to_minted_token`: it reads back the Aura token this same `effects` sequence's preceding `create_token` step just minted (the most recent `Event::TokenCreated`) and pushes an `Event::AttachedTo` linking it to the ability's chosen target — so a `create_token` (Aura profile) + `attach_minted_aura_to_target` (`target = { permanent = { types = "creature", controller = "opponent" } }`) pair mints the Contract attached to a chosen opponent's creature (guard-returns if the token isn't an Aura or no token was minted — CR 303, CR 704.5m). The Contract's granted "Whenever enchanted creature attacks…" clause is a card-specific `Effect::EnchantedAttackerPumpAttackingOpponentElseControllerLosesLife { power, toughness, life }` (a `timing = "enchanted_creature_attacks"` effect, the else-carrying sibling of `pump_other_attackers_attacking_your_opponents`): pumps the enchanted host if its declared defender is one of the Aura-controller's opponents, else the host's controller loses `life`. No new `Event`/`PendingChoice`/schema surface (composes the existing `TokenCreated`/`AttachedTo`/`TempBoost`/`LifeChanged`). scriv_the_obligator is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted, stale "tokens are creature-only" claim gone) — the "enters or attacks" trigger is two `[[abilities]]` (`etb` + `attacks`) since no combined timing exists. The mint-Aura-token-attached-to-a-chosen-target primitive is reusable for any card that creates a targeted Aura token.
- **echo** (karmic_guide) — upkeep pay-echo-or-sacrifice, on the landed pay-cost trigger choice with a sacrifice-on-decline arm. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `CardDef::echo: Option<Cost>` (`[echo]` in TOML, same shape as `[cost]`) plus `Permanent::echo_unpaid: bool` (set when a permanent with echo enters, cleared at its controller's first upkeep whether paid or sacrificed — CR 702.31e's "since your last upkeep" without overloading `summoning_sick`, which clears one step earlier at untap). Bespoke `Game::queue_echo_triggers`/a `pending_echo: Vec<ObjectId>` queue (Echo isn't a `[[abilities]]`/`Trigger`, so it doesn't ride `queue_trigger_group`) drains one at a time after the ordinary trigger queue in `place_pending_triggers`, pausing on a new `PendingChoice::PayEchoOrSacrifice` — the permanent-scoped twin of `PayOrCounter` (same `Intent::PayOptionalCost` wire shape, same "declining does something" polarity: sacrifice via the existing `Effect::SacrificeObject`, not a new effect). No new `Event`.
- **kicker** (rite_of_replication) — optional additional cast cost with a was-kicked flag readable at resolution (1-vs-5 token count); rides the `[cost.additional]` skeleton. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `AdditionalCost::kicker: Option<&'static Cost>` (`[cost.additional.kicker]` in TOML, same shape as `[cost]`; `&'static` because `Cost` already embeds `AdditionalCost`, so a bare `Option<Cost>` would recurse infinitely). The caster opts in via `Intent::Cast { kicked: true }` (mirrors the existing `sacrifice_count` synchronous-additional-cost plumbing — no new `PendingChoice`); `cast_cost` folds the kicker's pips into the total, and the flag is recorded on `Spell::kicked`, read at resolution by the new `Amount::IfSpellKicked { then, else_ }` via `Game::spell_was_kicked`. Single-kicker only (multikicker / two-kicker-costs not modeled — grow from a card that needs it).
- **retrace** (throes_of_chaos) — repeatable cast-from-graveyard by discarding a land: the flashback skeleton + a discard-a-land additional cost, no exile rider. M. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** `CardDef::retrace: bool` (`retrace = true` in TOML) widens the graveyard-cast gate in `playable_zone` alongside flashback/escape, but pays the printed `[cost]` as normal (CR 702.83a — not an alternative cost like flashback/escape, so `cast_cost`'s graveyard-cost fallback is `.unwrap_or(def.cost)` rather than an `.expect`). New `AdditionalCost::discard_land: bool` (`discard_land = true` in `[cost.additional]`) shares the existing `discard`/`Intent::Cast.discard_cost` slot (no pool card combines the two) but requires the named card to be a land, checked in `cast_additional_cost_gate` (can't-pay gate) and `validate_cast_cost_picks` (land-type check on the actual pick). Crucially the resolved `Spell` never sets `cast_via_flashback`/`cast_via_escape` (both stay `false` for a retrace-only card, since `flashback`/`escape` are `None`), so `finish_instant_sorcery_resolution`'s exile-on-leave branch is skipped and the spell returns to the graveyard normally — repeatable, confirmed by a second cast in the same test. throes_of_chaos is faithful on retrace; its Cascade residual landed with #132 (now fully faithful, `approximates` deleted).
- **graveyard-cast-cost** (raffines_guidance) — a fixed alternative cost to cast a *permanent* from your graveyard, resolving normally onto the battlefield (no exile rider): "You may cast this card from your graveyard by paying {2}{W} rather than paying its mana cost." M. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** New `CardDef::graveyard_cast_cost: Option<Cost>` (CR 118.9, `[graveyard_cast_cost]` TOML, same shape as `[flashback]`), wired into `playable_zone`'s `Zone::Graveyard` gate and `cast_cost`'s graveyard base-cost fallback (`.or(def.graveyard_cast_cost)`) alongside flashback/escape/retrace. Distinct from flashback/escape (the card is a permanent — it enters the battlefield normally, never reaching the graveyard-or-exile fork those gate, so `cast_via_flashback`/`cast_via_escape` stay `false` and no exile-on-resolve fires) and from retrace (this *replaces* the printed cost rather than adding one on top). raffines_guidance is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). Tests: `raffines_guidance_casts_from_graveyard_for_alt_cost` (casts from graveyard for {2}{W}, resolves onto the battlefield, attaches, +1/+1 applies), `raffines_guidance_graveyard_cast_charges_the_alt_cost_not_the_printed_cost` (funding only the printed {W} is rejected `CannotPayCost`). Reusable for any future "cast a permanent from your graveyard for [cost]" card.
- **suspend** (rousing_refrain) — self-exile with N time counters, tick at upkeep, cast free at zero (+ the mana-doesn't-empty rider); needs #75's counter kinds on exiled cards + #86's free cast. L. **LANDED (2026-07-14).** Full suspend subsystem (CR 702.62): new `CounterKind::Time` (COUNT/ALL bumped); a `Game::exile_time_counters` store (time counters live on an exile-zone `Object::Card`, not a `Permanent`) read by the public `Game::time_counters`; public `Event::TimeCountersPlaced`/`TimeCountersRemoved` (+ `VisibleEvent` mirrors — exile counters are public); `CardDef::suspend: Option<Suspend { counters, cost: &'static Cost }>` rules-keyword (`[suspend]` TOML) with a new `Intent::Suspend`/`MeaningfulAction::Suspend` special action (`Game::suspend`: pay the cost, exile from hand with time counters); an upkeep turn-based tick (`perform_turn_based_actions` `Step::Upkeep`) that removes one counter per the owner's suspended card and, at zero, grants #86's `cast_from_exile_free` permission (CR 702.62d/e). rousing_refrain's on-resolution self-exile is a separate new `Effect::ExileSelfWithTimeCounters` redirecting the resolving spell in `finish_instant_sorcery_resolution`. Board-dependent ritual now faithful too: `Effect::AddMana` gained a `target` field + new `Amount::CardsInTargetPlayerHand` (reads the spell's chosen opponent's hand size), so `mana = ["red"]`, `repeat = "cards_in_target_player_hand"`, `target = "opponent"`. **This also clears rousing_refrain from #65's blocked list** (the board-dependent AddMana amount). Residual `approximates`: only the "you don't lose this mana as steps and phases end" rider (CR 500.4) — ponytailed, unobservable for a same-turn-spent ritual. ponytail: the free cast is a "may cast free this turn" permission, not real suspend's forced triggered cast + haste (CR 702.62e/f) — indistinguishable for a sorcery.
- **mentor** (tajic) — attack trigger targeting another attacking creature with lesser power (CR 702.121); attack triggers + counters exist, the comparative-power target spec is new. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** Two new `PermanentFilter` axes: `attacking` (checked against `combat.attackers`) and `power_less_than_source` (reads `Game::power` on both the candidate and the filter's own `source`, threaded through `legal_targets_for`'s `TargetSpec::Permanent` arm — previously `None`, which had also silently no-opped every pool card's `other` axis on a `{ permanent = … }` target; no pool card relied on that, so widening it to the real source is free). tajic's Mentor is now a real `[[abilities]]` (`timing = "attacks"`, `put_counters` targeting `{ permanent = { types = "creature", attacking = true, power_less_than_source = true, other = true } }`); bonus: also authored the `{R}{W}: gains first strike until end of turn` activated ability (`pump_until_end_of_turn`, `target = "this"`, landed #72 machinery, no new surface). Landed: tajic (Mentor + `{R}{W}` first-strike ability faithful). Still blocked: tajic's residual `approximates` note is trimmed to just the "Prevent all noncombat damage…" clause (damage prevention, #130, unlanded).
- **decayed** (jadar_ghoulcaller_of_nephalia) — token keyword: can't block + when-it-attacks sacrifice at end of combat, plus a "you control no decayed creatures" condition arm. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** `Keyword::Decayed` (CR 702.148): a can't-block guard alongside the other evasion checks in `Game::can_block`, plus a rules-defined "when it attacks, sacrifice it at end of combat" wired straight into `Game::declare_attackers` — each declared attacker with decayed schedules a delayed `Effect::SacrificeObject` against itself at `Step::EndCombat` via the landed `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled`/`Game::fire_delayed_triggers` machinery (widened to drain at `Step::EndCombat` as well as `Upkeep`/`End`). New `Condition::YouControlNoCreatureWithKeyword { keyword }`, the effective-keyword sibling of `YouControlNoSubtype`. jadar is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted): its Zombie token carries `keywords = ["decayed"]`/`colors = ["black"]`/`subtypes = ["Zombie"]`, gated by the new condition as the ability's intervening-if. No schema changes — `Keyword` isn't wire-mirrored. ponytail: modeled as a rules-keyword-driven schedule at declare-attackers rather than a literal per-token `Trigger` object, since decayed's "when it attacks" clause is CR-defined on every creature that has the keyword, not authored ability text.
- **ascend / city's blessing** (tendershoot_dryad) — permanent per-player designation set at 10+ permanents, checked continuously, gating a `Condition` arm on its Saproling anthem. M. **LANDED (2026-07-11).** Sticky `Player::has_citys_blessing`, set by a new state-based-action loop (`check_state_based_actions`) when a living player controls ten or more permanents (`permanents_controlled` helper) and never cleared, emitting `Event::CitysBlessingGained`. New `Condition::YouHaveCitysBlessing` (`you_have_citys_blessing` tag) plus an `AnthemStatic.condition: Option<Condition>` gate axis evaluated per anthem source against its own controller in `matching_anthems`; cache invalidation on the new event mirrors `CreatureTypeChosen`. Landed: tendershoot_dryad (fully faithful — `approximates` note removed; the conditional +2/+2 Saproling anthem is now live exactly while its controller holds the blessing). Still blocked: none. ponytail: ascend is SBA-time-checked rather than continuous per CR 702.131c — behaviorally identical for the pool.
- **voting** (fateful_tempest) — council's-dilemma: a per-player vote round (fan-out `PendingChoice`, #102's shape), tallies stored, vote-count `Amount`s. L. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** New generic `Effect::CouncilsDilemmaVote { options }` (CR 701.32): a per-player vote fan-out mirroring `each_player_exiles_from_graveyard`'s shape — walks every living player in turn order starting with the caster (CR 701.32a's "starting with you"), pausing each on a new `PendingChoice::CastVote` answered by the existing `Intent::ChooseMode` (a labeled-index pick — no new intent/schema-intent surface; the pending choice projects to the existing `PendingChoiceView::ChooseMode`, `labels` = the ballot options). The two tallies accumulate on resolution-scoped `Game::council_past_votes`/`council_present_votes`, read by new §6 amounts `"past_votes"`/`"present_votes"`; the payoff rides in the enclosing `effects` `Sequence`, resumed once every seat has voted. Fateful Tempest's outcomes are ordinary sequenced steps reading those tallies: `mill_self` (count `"past_votes"`) — now snapshots the total mana value of the milled cards onto `Game::milled_mana_value_this_way` (the `destroy_all`/`exile_all` at-the-choke snapshot idiom) for the new §6 amount `"total_mana_value_milled_this_way"` — then `each_opponent_loses_life` (amount `"total_mana_value_milled_this_way"`) and `exile_top_may_play` (count `"present_votes"`, `until_next_turn = true` — Atsushi's landed impulse-window machinery). fateful_tempest is now fully faithful (`approximates` + body-only header deleted). ponytail: the two tallies/amounts are hardcoded to the past/present ballot (Fateful Tempest is the pool's only council's-dilemma card — generalize to a label→tally map when a differently-balloted will-of-the-council/council's-dilemma card lands); "deals damage to each opponent" reuses `each_opponent_loses_life` since the engine uniformly models player damage as life loss (`DealDamage`'s `Target::Player` arm), so no player-damage prevention/redirection or "deals damage" watch is expressible in the pool. The vote primitive (`CouncilsDilemmaVote` + `PendingChoice::CastVote`) is reusable for future council's-dilemma / will-of-the-council cards.
- **phasing** (guardian_of_faith) — a phased-out status excluding the permanent from every scan (statics, combat, SBAs, targeting), phase-in at untap. L. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** Two reusable primitives: runtime `Permanent::phased_out: bool` (defaulted false, `is_phased_out` accessor) and `Effect::PhaseOut` (`phase_out` — Guardian's ETB). The phased-out status is enforced at the low chokes every scan routes through: `Game::battlefield()` (excludes phased permanents → statics/anthems, SBA sweep, board counts/`permanents_controlled`, trigger scans, and every `permanent_matches` filter all skip them), `permanent_matches` itself (a phased permanent matches no filter — counts, edicts, mass effects, and in-response target legality), `is_creature_on_battlefield` (creature targeting), and `can_attack`/`can_block` (combat). `Effect::PhaseOut` pauses at resolution on a new `PendingChoice::PhaseOut` over the *other* creatures you control (reusing `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s any-subset wire shape like `Proliferate` — zero is a legal "phase out nothing"); its answer emits `Event::PhasedOut` per chosen creature, whose apply cascades to everything attached to it (CR 702.26g — indirect phasing; the phased Aura's `attachment_grants` stop applying). Phase-in is a turn-based action at the start of the controller's untap step (before untapping), emitting `Event::PhasedIn` for each directly-phased permanent, cascading to its attachments. Phasing invalidates the whole characteristics cache (a static source moving in/out of every scan) plus the phasing permanent and its attachments explicitly (they're excluded from `battlefield()` while phased). Schema: `PhasedOut`/`PhasedIn` events + `PendingChoiceView::PhaseOut` mirrored public; `ObjectView.phased_out` exposed on the snapshot.
