Landed: guardian_of_faith fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). ponytail: targets chosen at resolution rather than as the trigger goes on the stack (CR 603.3d — no pool card responds to Guardian's specific targets); phase-in keyed on the phased permanent's live controller (stands in for "its controller's next turn"); the SBA lethal-damage exclusion rides the shared `battlefield()` choke but can't be reached by a pool card (every P/T modifier also skips phased permanents, so no modeled effect can make a phased creature 0-toughness). **Follow-ups:** no "phases in tapped" bit (CR 702.26e — Guardian phases out untapped creatures; `tapped` is preserved for free but a tapped-when-phased-out case would need a companion flag); a phased permanent whose controller changes mid-phase is unmodeled; opponents still see phased permanents in their snapshot (with the flag) rather than hidden as CR's "doesn't exist" — expose or omit per UI need.
- **exile-any-graveyard-card-then-conditional-token** (feral_appetite) — "{1}{G}: Exile target card from a graveyard. If a creature card is exiled this way, create a 1/1 black and green Pest…": an unrestricted exile-any-graveyard-card target plus a conditional "if a creature was exiled this way" payoff gate; the existing graveyard-exile family is either fixed-filter (noncreature/nonland or artifact/creature) or unconditional. M. **LANDED (2026-07-14).** New `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardCardThenIfCreature { then }` — a fixed `any_card` filter over any graveyard (`GraveyardScope::Any`, hardcoded like its noncreature-nonland sibling `exile_target_from_graveyard_with_this`, not TOML-authored); exiles the chosen card, then runs `then` only if the just-exiled card's own printed type is a creature (CR "if … this way" reads what was just exiled, not LKI). `then` is `&'static [Effect]`, the same `[[abilities.effects.then]]` array shape `each_player_sacrifices` already uses — feral_appetite puts a `create_token` step there, reusing the landed `blight_mound`-style Pest token profile (1/1 black-green, "when this token dies, you gain 1 life") verbatim. feral_appetite is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted; both abilities scripted).
- **copy-self-on-cast + name-filtered unblockable** (leitmotif_composer) — "Whenever you cast an instant or sorcery spell with mana value 5 or greater, create a token that's a copy of this creature" + "{2}{U}: Creatures named Leitmotif Composer can't be blocked this turn": the copy-self trigger is pure authoring on landed `CreateTokenCopy`/`Trigger::CastSpell`/`Condition::TriggeringSpellManaValueAtLeast`; the unblockable grant needed one new filter axis. M. **LANDED (2026-07-14).** New `PermanentFilter.name: Option<&'static str>` (CR 201.2 printed-name equality), matched in `Game::permanent_matches` against `def.name`. The copy trigger is `timing = "cast_spell"` (`spell_filter = "instant_or_sorcery"`, `caster = "you"`, `condition = triggering_spell_mana_value_at_least { at_least = 5 }`) + `create_token_copy { target = "this", count = 1 }` — no engine change (dirgur_focusmage's MV-gate shape, Tajic's `target = "this"` self-reference, `determined_iteration`'s `CreateTokenCopy`, all reused verbatim). The unblockable grant is `pump_creatures_you_control_until_end_of_turn` (#90) with `keywords = ["unblockable"]` and the new `filter = { name = "Leitmotif Composer" }`. leitmotif_composer is now fully faithful (`approximates` + header prose deleted). ponytail: the name axis matches printed name only (no pool card renames a permanent — CR 707.9 doesn't arise); the grant is scoped to creatures *you* control (inherited from `PumpCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn`'s hardcoded "you control" shape) rather than every creature anywhere named Leitmotif Composer — unobservable for this card, since every copy the pool ever mints is under its own caster's control. The `PermanentFilter.name` axis is reusable for any future named-permanent-matters card.
- **face-down-permanents / manifest** (reality_shift) — face-down 2/2 with a hidden real face + turn-face-up rules; a new permanent status + visibility surface, shared by the morph family. L. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** New runtime `Permanent::face_down: bool` (CR 708 — not a `CardDef` surface, so `CardDef: Copy` is preserved; the real def stays in `Permanent::def`, hidden). While face down the characteristics chokes short-circuit to the CR 708.2 profile — a 2/2 colorless creature with no name/types-other-than-creature/subtypes/keywords/abilities (`effective_types` → `CREATURE`, `pt_base` → 2/2, `effective_subtypes`/`functional_abilities`/`compute_effective_keywords_uncached` → empty). New `Effect::Manifest` (`type = "manifest"`, no target of its own — reads the enclosing sequence's shared target's controller like `gain_life_target_controller`) moves that player's top library card to the battlefield face down via `Event::Manifested` (CR 701.34; no-op on an empty library). New `Intent::TurnFaceUp`/`MeaningfulAction::TurnFaceUp` special action (modeled on the suspend special-action plumbing): offered in `query::meaningful_actions` for a face-down permanent whose owner holds priority and whose hidden card is a creature it can afford; `Game::turn_face_up` pays the hidden mana cost and emits `Event::TurnedFaceUp` (a noncreature manifest is never offered — CR 701.34e — and stays a 2/2 forever). Schema: `Manifested` drops the private moved-card identity (`from`) the way `Sacrificed` does; `TurnedFaceUp` is public; `ObjectView.face_down` anonymizes name/kind/mana-cost for every viewer; `Intent::TurnFaceUp` wire mirror + inbound conversion. reality_shift is now fully faithful (`approximates` + manifest ponytail header deleted; both effects scripted). **This finishes the entire Per-card exotics section — every exotic bullet above is now LANDED.** Redaction scope: the face-down card is hidden from *every* viewer (including its own controller, who in paper may look) — the simplest correct redaction; reveal-to-controller deferred (ponytail on `ObjectView.face_down`). The face-down-2/2 status is the reusable substrate for the morph family (CR 702.37 morph / megamorph / disguise) — no morph card is in the pool, so only plain manifest is built; a morph card would layer its face-down cost + the morph keyword on top (ponytail on `Permanent::face_down`). ponytail: turn-face-up gated on the permanent's owner (the engine-wide control/ownership conflation), same as the other special actions.
- **bestow / dual-nature Aura-creature** (eidolon_of_countless_battles) — a permanent creature card with an alternative Aura cast mode (CR 702.103): cast for its bestow cost it's an Aura spell with enchant creature; while attached it's an Aura, not a creature (702.103e), and becomes a creature again when it stops being attached (702.103i). L. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** Reusable bestow substrate: `CardDef::bestow: Option<Cost>` (`[bestow]` TOML, same `[cost]` shape as `[echo]`; `CardDef: Copy` preserved — the dual nature is *runtime* state, never the static def); runtime flags `Spell::bestowed`/`Permanent::bestowed`. New `Intent::CastBestow { object, target }` + `Game::cast_bestow` (modeled on `cast_adventure`): from hand, sorcery speed, pays the flat bestow cost, requires an enchant-creature target (validated by viewing the card as `CardKind::Aura` so `required_target` yields the creature spec), and emits `Event::SpellCast { bestowed: true }`. A bestowed spell resolves through the `CardKind::Aura` attach path (`PermanentEntered` + `AttachedTo`, enchant-legality re-checked, CR 303.4f) rather than entering as a creature; the entered `Permanent` carries `bestowed`. The dual nature is a live "bestowed **and** attached" gate (`Game::is_bestowed_and_attached`): while so, `effective_types` → `ENCHANTMENT` and `effective_subtypes` → `["Aura"]` (off combat, out of creature filters/wraths, counts as an Aura) and the toughness-≤0/lethal creature death SBAs are skipped; unattached it reverts to its printed creature nature for free. Unattach→creature needs no new SBA — since `def.kind` stays `Creature`, the unattached-Aura-to-graveyard SBA (CR 704.5n) never fires for it, and the host-leaves detach reuses the Equipment-detach arm. The enchanted-creature half of the buff is pure authoring: the two `self_only anthem_static`s (pumping Eidolon's own body) are paired with two `grant_to_attached` statics carrying the same per-creature/per-Aura `Amount`s (inert until bestowed/attached). Schema: `bestowed` rides `Event::SpellCast` (not surfaced on the wire yet, ponytail); `WireIntent::CastBestow` mirror + inbound conversion. eidolon_of_countless_battles is now fully faithful (`approximates` + "plain creature" header deleted). ponytail: bestow is single-card-scoped (Eidolon is the pool's only bestow card) — flat cost with no reduction/ward pipeline, and the dual-nature SBA covers only the tested attach/unattach cases. No `MeaningfulAction::CastBestow` (consistent with adventure — the card's normal creature cast already stops auto-pass; the client offers bestow from `def.bestow.is_some()`). Reusable for any future bestow card.
- **random-order bottoming** (songbirds_blessing, creative_technique) — the last two cards carrying the old "no `rand`" deterministic bottom-in-order stand-in for "put the rest on the bottom of your library in a random order," now stale since #116 landed the injected splitmix PRNG and #132's cascade already upgraded its own bottoming to a real Fisher-Yates (which also swept in Herald of Amity's dig). S. **LANDED (2026-07-14).** `Game::begin_reveal_until_may_deploy`/`Game::begin_reveal_until_exile_cast_free` now collect every non-matching revealed card into a `rest` pile (instead of bottoming each immediately as revealed) and hand it to a new shared `Game::bottom_pile_in_library` — the same Fisher-Yates-with-`next_u64` shuffle `Game::bottom_exiled_dig` already uses for Cascade/Herald of Amity, but emitting `Event::PutOnBottomOfLibrary` (same-zone reorder) instead of `Event::TuckedToLibrary` (exile→library is a real zone change). Both cards' `approximates` deleted. No new DSL/schema surface — an implementation swap behind the existing `reveal_until_may_deploy`/`reveal_until_exile_cast_free` effect tags.
- **regeneration** (rapid_hybridization) — regeneration shields + the "can't be regenerated" rider: a destroy-replacement shield in the death pipeline; currently vacuous (nothing grants regeneration) but a real increment under the all-cards posture. L. **LANDED (2026-07-12).** Two reusable front-door primitives: `Effect::RegenerateShield { target }` (`regenerate_shield` — grants one shield via `Event::RegenerationShieldCreated`, incrementing the new runtime `Permanent::regeneration_shields: u8`) and `Effect::DestroyTarget.cant_be_regenerated: bool` (`#[serde(default)]` false). At the `DestroyTarget` resolution, a sibling guard to the indestructible check: if `!cant_be_regenerated` and the target has a shield, consume one and emit `Event::Regenerated` (tap, remove from combat, heal marked damage) instead of the graveyard move (CR 701.15b); "can't be regenerated" (CR 701.15d) skips that guard. Unused shields reset at cleanup via `Event::RegenerationShieldsExpired` (CR 701.15b's "this turn"). Public accessor `Game::regeneration_shields`; three events mirrored in schema (public battlefield state, no redaction — `regeneration_shields` itself is not snapshot-mirrored, following `finality_counter`). Landed: rapid_hybridization fully faithful (`approximates` deleted; `cant_be_regenerated = true` authored on its `destroy_target`). ponytail: the shield is consulted only on the effect-driven `DestroyTarget` destroy, not the CR 704.5g lethal-marked-damage SBA destroy (also a "destroy" a shield should replace) — unobserved, since no pool card grants a shield; upgrade path noted at the check site. **Follow-ups:** no pool card *grants* a regeneration shield yet (`RegenerateShield` is tested directly as a bare primitive); a real granter would want per-source shields / "regenerate up to one target creature" grants (CR 701.15), and would motivate wiring the shield into the SBA lethal-damage path and mirroring `regeneration_shields` in the snapshot.
- **target-controller-ramp** (white_orchid_phantom) — "destroy up to one target nonbasic land. Its controller may search their library for a basic land card, put it onto the battlefield tapped, then shuffle": the ramp rider needs a library search targeted at the destroyed land's *controller*, an arbitrary player, not the ability's controller. S. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** Pure authoring: `SearchScope::TargetController` (landed as part of Path to Exile/Assassin's Trophy's own ramp riders) gets its second live consumer — `[[abilities.effects]]` chains `destroy_target` then `search_library { searcher = "target_controller", filter = "basic_land", to_zone = "battlefield", tapped = true }`, sharing the ability's one target the same way Path to Exile does. No engine change: `controller_of` already reads the destroyed land's last-known controller after the destroy step moves it to the graveyard. white_orchid_phantom is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). ponytail: the "may search" is modeled as fail-to-find on the search step, not a separate opt-out.
- **free-cast-graveyard-redirect** (quintorius_loremaster) — the activated ability's "If that spell would be put into a graveyard, put it on the bottom of its owner's library instead" (CR 614.6): a one-shot replacement scoped to the one cast object, on top of the landed free-cast permission (`CastExiledWithThisFree`). S. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** New `PlayPermissions::stack_object_bottoms_library_on_leave: Vec<ObjectId>`, flagged by a new sibling event `Event::CastFromExileFreeBottomsLibraryOnLeave { card }` pushed only from Quintorius's own `choose_exiled_with_card_to_cast` grant handler (`CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted` is shared by two other free-cast effects — Herald of Amity's dig, Dance with Calamity — so the redirect flag rides a second, Quintorius-only event rather than widening the shared one). Casting mints the exiled card a fresh stack object id (CR 400.7), so both graveyard chokes — `Game::finish_instant_sorcery_resolution` (resolve) and `Game::counter_spell` (countered) — match a flagged entry by following `Game::current_id` from the stored pre-cast id forward, then emit the existing `Event::TuckedToLibrary { to_top: false }` (reused verbatim from Mistveil Plains/Chaos Warp's tuck, extended with a `remove_spell_from_stack` call for the from-the-stack case) instead of `Event::MovedToGraveyard`. No new `Effect`/DSL surface — the rider is intrinsic to `cast_exiled_with_this_free`. quintorius_loremaster is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).
- **fetch-only-land** (fabled_passage) — the #6-era residual: Fabled Passage's `[kind]` wrongly carried `produces = "colorless"`, letting it tap for {C} on its own when the real card is fetch-only. S. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** Pure authoring, no engine change — matches the existing Terramorphic Expanse precedent exactly: deleted `produces = "colorless"` from `[kind]` (leaving `type = "land"` only, so it has no base tap-for-mana ability) plus the `approximates` line and its two mana-flattening `# ponytail:` comments. The fetch + four-or-more-lands conditional untap were already faithful and are untouched. fabled_passage is now fully faithful. Test: `fabled_passage_has_no_tap_for_mana` (mirrors `a_fetch_only_land_has_no_tap_for_mana`'s Prismatic Vista shape) asserts `Intent::TapForMana` on a bare Fabled Passage rejects `Reject::CannotProduceMana`.
- **ability-copy** (unbound_flourishing) — the "or activate an ability … copy that ability" half of Unbound Flourishing's second trigger (CR 707.10): a genuinely new mechanic — a trigger on *activating an ability* whose activation cost contains `{X}`, and an effect that *copies an ability* on the stack — with no consumer before this. L. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** Two reusable primitives plus the `{X}`-cost-activation substrate they need: (1) `{X}` in an activated ability's cost now flows end-to-end — `Intent::ActivateAbility` gained a chosen `x` (schema wire defaults 0, ponytail — no pool card is `{X}`-cost-activated), folded into the mana payment via the existing `Cost::with_x`, carried onto a new `StackItem::Ability.x` / `Event::TriggeredAbilityOnStack.x` (0 for every triggered ability; `StackEntry` unchanged — x is internal resolution state) and read at resolution so `Amount::X` resolves against it. (2) `Trigger::ActivateAbility { caster }` (`timing = "activate_ability"`, reusing `cast_spell`'s `caster` sibling) — fired directly from `Game::activate_ability` once the non-mana ability is placed, gated on `cost.mana.x > 0` (the *cost* containing `{X}`, not the chosen value — an `{X}` = 0 activation still fires, CR 707.10 copies value 0), via a new `queue_activate_ability_triggers` (the `queue_batch_attack_triggers` direct-queue shape, not the event scan). The triggering ability's source rides in `TriggerContext::triggering_ability`, baked into a matched `Effect::CopyTriggeringAbility` by `contextualize_effect`/`fill_triggering_ability`. (3) `Effect::CopyTriggeringAbility { may_choose_new_targets }` — mints one copy of that ability above the original on the stack (via `push_ability_group_with_x`, reusing the trigger-placement path; the copy isn't "activated", CR 707.10c) carrying its effect/target and its chosen `{X}` unchanged (CR 706.10 — an already-doubled X isn't re-doubled); guard-returns if the ability left the stack (countered, CR 603.4). No new `Event`/`PendingChoice`/schema surface — the copy reuses `TriggeredAbilityOnStack`. unbound_flourishing's first ability (`cast_x_replacement`) and spell half (`copy_triggering_spell`) were already faithful; the ability half is now scripted as a third `[[abilities]]` (`timing = "activate_ability"`, `caster = "you"`, `copy_triggering_ability { may_choose_new_targets = true }`). `approximates` trimmed to the one residual: a copied *activated* ability keeps its original targets — the "you may choose new targets" re-pick isn't offered for the ability half, since no pool card is a *targeted* `{X}`-cost activated ability to copy (ponytail on the effect; upgrade path: a copy-scoped retarget pause writing the new target onto the copy's stack item). **Follow-up:** a real `{X}`-cost activated ability in the pool would want the wire `Intent::ActivateAbility.x` (+ OpenAPI regen) so a client can choose X; and a *targeted* one would motivate the copy-retarget pause. Tests: `unbound_flourishing_copies_activated_x_ability` (X = 3 draw resolves twice), `_ignores_ability_without_x`, `_ignores_opponent_ability`, `_still_copies_x_sorcery_spell` (spell-half regression).
- **mass-exile-all-graveyards** (final_act) — the residual from the #105/Casualties-of-War modal landing above: "Exile all graveyards" was one of three dropped modes, blocked on there being no mass (untargeted) all-graveyards exile effect, only the single targeted-player `ExileGraveyard` (Bojuka Bog). S. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** New `Effect::ExileAllGraveyards` (`exile_all_graveyards`, fieldless, no target) — the mass twin of `ExileGraveyard`, looping every live object whose zone is `Graveyard` (dropping `ExileGraveyard`'s `owner_of(id) != player` filter) and emitting one `Event::MovedToExile` per card, same sequential-id-minting shape. Wired as Final Act's third mode; `choose_max` bumped `2` → `3`. final_act now scripts 3 of its 5 modes (destroy all creatures / destroy all planeswalkers / exile all graveyards); `approximates` trimmed to the two still-blocked modes (destroy all battles — no battle permanent type; each opponent loses all counters — no player-level counter tracking). Test: `final_act_exile_all_graveyards_mode_empties_every_graveyard` asserts every player's graveyard (including the caster's own) is exiled, contrasting the single-target `exile_target_players_graveyard_bojuka_bog` test which leaves other players' graveyards untouched.
- **reflexive-trigger** (forum_filibuster) — a real reflexive "when you do" triggered ability (CR 603.3b), replacing the same-resolution sequenced-payoff shortcut #69's 2026-07-12 note left as forum_filibuster's residual: the token's creation and the Aura's return-and-attach must be two separate stack objects with a priority window between them. M. **LANDED (2026-07-15).** Reusable primitive `Effect::ReflexiveTrigger { then }` (`type = "reflexive_trigger"`, a `[[abilities.effects.then]]` sub-array): placed after a `create_token` step, its resolution enqueues each `then` effect as its *own* separate triggered ability via the normal APNAP placement path (`Game::queue_reflexive_trigger` pushes a fabricated single-ability `TriggerGroup` onto `pending_trigger_groups`, mid-resolution, exactly the way `fire_delayed_triggers` does — then the pipeline's `TriggerPlacement` phase puts it on the stack with a fresh priority window). The "you do" condition is that the parent's preceding `create_token` minted a token this resolution (read back from the latest `Event::TokenCreated`, the `AttachTriggeringAuraToMintedToken` idiom); that token's id is threaded into each `then` effect (`Effect::with_reflexive_token`, the `fill_entering_permanent` threading pattern). The body `Effect::ReturnFromGraveyardAttachedToToken { filter, token }` is a real targeted ability: `target()` → `TargetSpec::CardInGraveyard { whose: Yours, filter }`, `target_count()` → `{0,1}` ("up to one"), so it chooses its Aura/Equipment target through the ordinary `ChooseTarget`/`place_targeted_ability` path as it goes on the stack (CR 601.2c) — declining (empty target) or an empty graveyard drops it with the token intact, the standard "up to one" treatment. At resolution it reanimates the chosen card attached to `token`, guard-returning (CR 608.2b) if the token has left the battlefield. The old `Effect::ReanimateAttachedToMintedToken` + its resolution-time `PendingChoice::ReanimateAttachedToMintedToken`/`begin_`/`answer_` handlers and the schema `PendingChoiceView`/projection mirror are all deleted (no dead shortcut left). forum_filibuster fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). **Augusta, Order Returned NOT migrated** — its reflexive counter payoff's "you do" is its own graveyard-exile fan-out, not a token creation, so it isn't threadable through this token-scoped primitive without generalizing the "you do" condition; left inline with a `ponytail:` at `effects.rs`'s `EachPlayerExilesFromGraveyard` arm pointing at `ReflexiveTrigger` as the upgrade target. Tests: `forum_filibuster_reflexive_return_is_a_separate_stack_object` (load-bearing — the reflexive ability sits on the stack with the Aura still in the graveyard and the active player holding priority before it resolves), `_reflexive_declined`, `_reflexive_no_op_if_token_gone`, `_mints_the_token_with_nothing_to_return`.

## Top 5 next increments (build in this order)

1. **`target-filter-adoption` (#66)** — 18 cards for an S: pure wiring of the already-landed `PermanentFilter` into the remaining targeted/mass effects. Highest leverage in the audit, zero new machinery.
2. **`amount-generalization-2` (#65, batch #96 pump-amount into it)** — 33 cards partially unblocked across the two; finishes what v1 #5 started so every numeric site takes an `Amount`, and threads `TriggerContext` values (MV/X/damage) that a dozen later increments assume.
3. **`color-filter-axis` → `token-color-subtype` (#63 → #64)** — the biggest single unlock (5 + 23 cards) and the last missing characteristic axis; every token-tribal payoff in Witherbloom/Silverquill/Prismari sits behind it.
4. **`spell-filter-extensions` (#67) + `condition-extensions` (#71)** — two S waves, 25 cards: the remaining filter/condition arms that cast triggers, cost reducers, and effect-level gates all consume.
5. **`multi-target-adoption` (#73) + `graveyard-card-filters-2` (#69)** — 24 cards across the charms/removal suite; both are adoption passes over landed L-machinery (`TargetCount`, `CardInGraveyard`).

(Strategic mention: start **#126 type-change-layers slice 1** — the behavior-preserving layer-entry migration — in parallel with the waves above. It's the longest-lead-time item in the backlog, five later increments lean on it, and slice 1 carries no card-visible risk.)
